      <!-- Director calibration — shifts every rule threshold + AI tone directive. -->
      <div id="directorBiasRow" style="margin-top:12px;padding:10px 12px;background:var(--glass);border:1px solid var(--glass-border);border-radius:var(--radius);">

        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:0.58rem;color:var(--text-faint);margin-top:2px;letter-spacing:0.04em;text-transform:uppercase;">
          <span>lean cautious</span>
          <span>balanced</span>
          <span>lean forward</span>
        </div>
        <div class="hint" style="font-size:0.66rem;margin-top:6px;line-height:1.4;">
          If sessions feel too intense or the Director pushes too hard → shift cautious.
          If the Director holds back too much or sessions feel muted → shift forward.
          <button type="button" id="directorBiasResetBtn" style="background:none;border:none;color:var(--neon-cyan);cursor:pointer;font-size:0.66rem;padding:0;margin-left:4px;text-decoration:underline;">reset to balanced</button>
        </div>
      </div>

<script>
  // ====================================================================
  // IDB STORAGE (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT)
  // Replaces localStorage for reliable persistence
  // ====================================================================
  const IDB_NAME = 'stillness-db';
  const IDB_VER  = 1;
  const IDB_STORE = 'kv';
  let _idb = null;
  let _idbOpenP = null;

  function _openIdb() {
    if (_idb) return Promise.resolve(_idb);
    if (_idbOpenP) return _idbOpenP;
    _idbOpenP = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const req = indexedDB.open(IDB_NAME, IDB_VER);
      req.onupgradeneeded = e => {
        const db = e.target.result;
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(IDB_STORE)) db.createObjectStore(IDB_STORE);
      };
      req.onsuccess = e => {
        _idb = e.target.result;
        _idb.onclose = () => { _idb = null; _idbOpenP = null; };
        resolve(_idb);
      };
      req.onerror = e => { _idbOpenP = null; reject(e.target.error ?? new Error('IDB open failed')); };
    });
    return _idbOpenP;
  }
  async function idbGet(key) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      return await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const r = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readonly').objectStore(IDB_STORE).get(key);
        r.onsuccess = () => res(r.result ?? null);
        r.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch { return null; }
  }
  async function idbSet(key, value) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const tx = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readwrite');
        tx.objectStore(IDB_STORE).put(value, key);
        tx.oncomplete = res;
        tx.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch {}
  }
  async function idbDel(key) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const tx = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readwrite');
        tx.objectStore(IDB_STORE).delete(key);
        tx.oncomplete = res;
        tx.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch {}
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TOAST NOTIFICATIONS (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT)
  // Non-blocking replacements for alert()
  // ====================================================================
  const TOAST_ICONS    = { info: 'ℹ', success: '✓', warn: '⚠', error: '✕' };
  const TOAST_DURATION = { info: 3500, success: 3000, warn: 5000, error: 0 };

  function toast(type, message, ms) {
    const container = $('toastContainer');
    if (!container) return;
    const duration = ms !== undefined ? ms : TOAST_DURATION[type] || 3500;
    const el = document.createElement('div');
    el.className = `toast toast-${type}`;
    el.innerHTML = `<span class="toast-icon">${TOAST_ICONS[type] || 'ℹ'}</span><span class="toast-text">${escapeHtml(message)}</span><button class="toast-close">×</button>`;
    el.querySelector('.toast-close').addEventListener('click', () => dismissToast(el));
    if (duration === 0) el.addEventListener('click', () => dismissToast(el));
    container.appendChild(el);
    requestAnimationFrame(() => el.classList.add('show'));
    let timer = null;
    if (duration > 0) timer = setTimeout(() => dismissToast(el), duration);
    function dismissToast(t) { clearTimeout(timer); t.classList.remove('show'); setTimeout(() => t.remove(), 220); }
    return el;
  }
  const notify = {
    info:    (msg, ms) => toast('info', msg, ms),
    success: (msg, ms) => toast('success', msg, ms),
    warn:    (msg, ms) => toast('warn', msg, ms),
    error:   (msg, ms) => toast('error', msg, ms),
  };

  function confirmAsync(message, opts = {}) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
      backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
      backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal" style="max-width:420px;">
        <div style="font-size:0.88rem;line-height:1.55;color:var(--text-dim);white-space:pre-line;">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>
        <div class="modal-actions" style="margin-top:16px;">
          <button class="btn secondary" id="_confirmNo">${opts.cancelText || 'cancel'}</button>
          <button class="btn" id="_confirmYes">${opts.okText || 'confirm'}</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
      const cleanup = (val) => { backdrop.remove(); resolve(val); };
      backdrop.querySelector('#_confirmYes').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(true));
      backdrop.querySelector('#_confirmNo').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(false));
      backdrop.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup(false); });
    });
  }

  function alertModal(title, message) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
      backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
      backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal" style="max-width:420px;">
        ${title ? `<h2 style="margin:0 0 12px;">${escapeHtml(title)}</h2>` : ''}
        <div style="font-size:0.84rem;line-height:1.55;color:var(--text-dim);white-space:pre-line;">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>
        <div class="modal-actions" style="margin-top:16px;">
          <button class="btn" id="_alertOk">ok</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
      const cleanup = () => { backdrop.remove(); resolve(); };
      backdrop.querySelector('#_alertOk').addEventListener('click', cleanup);
      backdrop.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup(); });
    });
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // iOS Safari viewport fix (from Perchance skill reference)
  // ====================================================================
  try {
    const isTouchScreen = window.matchMedia("(pointer: coarse)").matches;
    const isSafari = navigator.vendor?.indexOf('Apple') > -1
      && !navigator.userAgent.includes('CriOS')
      && !navigator.userAgent.includes('FxiOS');
    if (isSafari && window.innerWidth < 800 && isTouchScreen) {
      const viewportMeta = document.querySelector("[name=viewport]");
      if (viewportMeta && !viewportMeta.getAttribute("content").includes("maximum-scale")) {
        viewportMeta.setAttribute("content",
          viewportMeta.getAttribute("content") + ", maximum-scale=1");
      }
    }
  } catch(e) { console.error(e); }

  /** Sync state._debug from checkbox DOM. Called on load and on any debug checkbox change. */
  function _syncDebugState() {
    const d = state._debug;
    d.skipRescue       = !!document.getElementById('debugSkipRescue')?.checked;
    d.skipCooldown     = !!document.getElementById('debugSkipCooldown')?.checked;
    d.skipSafetyGate   = !!document.getElementById('debugSkipSafetyGate')?.checked;
    d.skipMethodGating = !!document.getElementById('debugSkipMethodGating')?.checked;
    d.verbose          = !!document.getElementById('debugVerbose')?.checked;
    _renderDebugBanner();
  }

  /** Show/hide the floating "DEBUG" indicator whenever any debug flag is active. */
  function _renderDebugBanner() {
    const anyOn = Object.values(state._debug).some(Boolean);
    let el = document.getElementById('_debugBanner');
    if (anyOn && !el) {
      el = document.createElement('div');
      el.id = '_debugBanner';
      el.textContent = '\u26A0 DEBUG';
      el.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:8px;right:8px;z-index:99999;background:rgba(220,60,60,0.92);color:#fff;font-size:0.62rem;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:0.08em;padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;pointer-events:none;box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);';
      document.body.appendChild(el);
    } else if (!anyOn && el) {
      el.remove();
    }
  }

  /** Verbose Smart Director logger. No-op unless state._debug.verbose is on. */
  function sdLog(...args) {
    if (state._debug?.verbose) console.log('[SmartDirector]', ...args);
  }

  let _personaCache = null;

  async function _initStorage() {
    // Migrate personas from localStorage → IDB
    _personaCache = await idbGet(PERSONA_KEY);
    if (!_personaCache) {
      try {
        const lsRaw = localStorage.getItem(PERSONA_KEY);
        if (lsRaw) { _personaCache = JSON.parse(lsRaw); await idbSet(PERSONA_KEY, _personaCache); localStorage.removeItem(PERSONA_KEY); }
      } catch {}
    }
    if (!Array.isArray(_personaCache)) _personaCache = [];

    // Normalize legacy history/settings/analytics stores
    try {
      const legacyHistory = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
      if (Array.isArray(legacyHistory) && legacyHistory.length) {
        const normalizedHistory = legacyHistory.map(normalizeHistoryEntry).sort((a,b)=>(b.date||0)-(a.date||0));
        await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', normalizedHistory);
      }
    } catch {}
    try {
      const analytics = await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY) || await idbGet('stillness_analytics_v2');
      if (analytics) await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, normalizeAnalyticsData(analytics));
    } catch {}
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v4') || localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v3') || localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v2');
      if (raw && !localStorage.getItem(SETTINGS_KEY)) {
        localStorage.setItem(SETTINGS_KEY, JSON.stringify(normalizeSettings(JSON.parse(raw))));
      }
    } catch {}

    // Persist browser storage so IDB isn't cleared
    if (navigator.storage?.persist) await navigator.storage.persist();
  }

  const loadCustomPersonas = () => _personaCache || [];
  const saveCustomPersonas = arr => { _personaCache = arr; idbSet(PERSONA_KEY, arr); return true; };

  /**
   * Load personas from community packs exposed via `root.communityPacks`.
   * Packs are lazy-loaded generators with a top-level `personas` list whose
   * items are JSON objects or serialisable list entries. Silent on failure.
   * @returns {Array} Array of persona objects (possibly empty)
   */
  function loadCommunityPackPersonas() {
    if (typeof root === 'undefined' || !root.communityPacks) return [];
    const out = [];
    try {
      // communityPacks is a DSL list where each sub-list is a `dynamicImport(...)`
      // Perchance materialises it as an object { <packName>: {personas: [...], ...}, ... }
      for (const [packName, pack] of Object.entries(root.communityPacks)) {
        if (!pack || !pack.personas) continue;
        const items = Array.isArray(pack.personas) ? pack.personas : [pack.personas];
        for (const raw of items) {
          try {
            // Accept either JS objects or JSON strings in the Perchance list
            const p = typeof raw === 'string' ? JSON.parse(raw) : raw;
            if (!p || !p.id || !p.name) continue;
            out.push({
              id: `pack:${packName}:${p.id}`,
              name: p.name,
              tagline: p.tagline || '',
              category: p.category || 'contemplative',
              systemPrompt: p.systemPrompt || '',
              isCommunity: true,
              packName,
            });
          } catch (e) { /* skip malformed entry */ }
        }
      }
    } catch (e) { console.warn('Community pack load failed:', e); }
    return out;
  }

  function refreshPersonas() {
    const custom = loadCustomPersonas().map(p => ({ ...p, isCustom: true, category: p.category || 'contemplative' }));
    const community = loadCommunityPackPersonas();
    state.personas = [...BUILTIN_PERSONAS, ...community, ...custom];
  }
  const escapeHtml = s => String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, c => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'})[c]);

  // ── Reusable helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);

  /** Set button to loading state or restore it */
  function setLoading(btnOrId, loading, originalText) {
    const btn = typeof btnOrId === 'string' ? $(btnOrId) : btnOrId;
    if (!btn) return;
    btn.disabled = loading;
    if (loading) btn.classList.add('loading');
    else { btn.classList.remove('loading'); if (originalText) btn.textContent = originalText; }
  }

  /** Start an elapsed-seconds timer. Returns a stop function. */
  function makeElapsedTimer(callback) {
    const start = Date.now();
    const id = setInterval(() => callback(Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000)), 1000);
    return () => clearInterval(id);
  }

  /** Show or hide an element by ID */
  function showEl(id, vis) {
    const el = typeof id === 'string' ? $(id) : id;
    if (el) el.style.display = vis === false ? 'none' : '';
  }

  /** Toggle a play/stop preview button pair. prefix = 'voice'|'sound'|'viz' */
  function togglePreviewBtns(prefix, playing) {
    showEl(prefix + 'PreviewBtn', !playing);
    showEl(prefix + 'StopBtn', playing);
  }

  /** Rebuild visible phase dots to match the current script/phase plan */
  function renderSessionPhaseDots(phases = []) {
    const wrap = $('phaseDots');
    if (!wrap) return;
    wrap.innerHTML = phases.map(p => `<div class="phase-dot" data-phase="${escapeHtml(p)}" title="${escapeHtml(getPhaseLabel(p).toLowerCase())}"></div>`).join('');
  }

  /** Update phase dot indicators: -1=reset, N=active, >=length=all done */
  function updatePhaseDots(activeIdx, totalCount = document.querySelectorAll('.phase-dot').length) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.phase-dot').forEach((d, i) => {
      d.classList.remove('active', 'done');
      if (activeIdx >= 0 && i < activeIdx) d.classList.add('done');
      if (i === activeIdx) d.classList.add('active');
      if (activeIdx >= totalCount) d.classList.add('done');
    });
  }

  /** Switch between the three main screens */
  function switchScreen(id) {
    ['setup-wizard', 'session-screen', 'post-screen'].forEach(s => {
      const el = $(s); if (el) el.style.display = s === id ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TOKEN BUDGET — priority-based trimming so long profiles,
  // adaptive context, and semantic memory don't silently exceed the
  // context window and cause quality cliffs.
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * Trim context blocks to fit within the Perchance AI token budget.
   * Lower priority = dropped first. Priority convention:
   *   1 = semantic/rolling memory      (first to trim)
   *   2 = adaptive block
   *   3 = profile context
   *   4 = crafted + affirmations       (last-ditch)
   *   5 = persona + method + task      (never trimmed)
   * Blocks can be null/empty; they're skipped.
   *
   * @param {Array<{name:string, text:string, priority:number}>} blocks
   * @param {number} reserveForOutput  Tokens to leave for the model's reply
   * @returns {string}  Concatenated, possibly trimmed, context
   */
  function trimToTokenBudget(blocks, reserveForOutput = 800) {
    const kept = blocks.filter(b => b && b.text && b.text.length > 0);
    const joined = () => kept.map(b => b.text).join('');
    // Best-effort — if Perchance AI isn't loaded, return everything and let the
    // caller hope it fits. The call is guarded so we never throw on errors.
    if (typeof root === 'undefined' || !root.aiTextPlugin) return joined();
    let meta;
    try { meta = root.aiTextPlugin({ getMetaObject: true }); } catch { return joined(); }
    const countTokens = meta?.countTokens;
    const limit = meta?.idealMaxContextTokens;
    if (!countTokens || !limit) return joined();
    const budget = limit - reserveForOutput;
    // Sort by priority ASC so we pop low-priority first.
    kept.sort((a, b) => (a.priority || 3) - (b.priority || 3));
    let total = countTokens(joined());
    while (total > budget && kept.length > 0) {
      // Don't drop priority-5 items — if we hit them, nothing we can do.
      const lowest = kept[0];
      if ((lowest.priority || 3) >= 5) break;
      console.warn(`[tokenBudget] Dropping "${lowest.name}" (${countTokens(lowest.text)} tokens, total ${total} > ${budget})`);
      kept.shift();
      total = countTokens(joined());
    }
    return joined();
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SEMANTIC MEMORY — augments the existing recency-based
  // 3-tier memory with embedding-based retrieval so "what worked for
  // this intention before" beats "what happened most recently."
  // Gracefully degrades when embedTexts isn't available.
  // ====================================================================
  const _EMBED_KEY = 'stillness_embed_v1';
  let _embedCache = null;

  async function _getEmbedStore() {
    if (_embedCache) return _embedCache;
    _embedCache = (await idbGet(_EMBED_KEY)) || { vectors: {} }; // { [digestId]: number[] }
    return _embedCache;
  }
  async function _saveEmbedStore(store) {
    _embedCache = store;
    await idbSet(_EMBED_KEY, store);
  }

  /** Cosine distance (lower = more similar). Returns 2 for bad inputs. */
  function cosineDistance(a, b) {
    if (!a || !b || a.length !== b.length || a.length === 0) return 2;
    let dot = 0, na = 0, nb = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < a.length; i++) { dot += a[i] * b[i]; na += a[i] * a[i]; nb += b[i] * b[i]; }
    const denom = Math.sqrt(na) * Math.sqrt(nb);
    if (denom === 0) return 2;
    return 1 - dot / denom;
  }

  /** Embed a digest and store its vector alongside the digest's sessionId. */
  async function embedAndStoreDigest(sessionId, digestText) {
    if (!window.textEmbedderFunction || !digestText) return false;
    try {
      const modelName = window.thread?.textEmbeddingModelName;
      const [vec] = await window.embedTexts({ textArr: [digestText], modelName });
      if (!vec || vec.length === 0) return false;
      // Serialize Float32Array → plain array for IDB.
      const arr = Array.from(vec);
      const store = await _getEmbedStore();
      store.vectors[String(sessionId)] = arr;
      // Cap store at 100 vectors, newest kept.
      const ids = Object.keys(store.vectors);
      if (ids.length > 100) {
        // We don't have dates here, but digests are stored in insertion order —
        // just drop the oldest half to stay simple.
        for (const old of ids.slice(0, ids.length - 100)) delete store.vectors[old];
      }
      await _saveEmbedStore(store);
      return true;
    } catch (e) { console.warn('embedAndStoreDigest failed:', e); return false; }
  }

  /**
   * Find the top-K most semantically similar past digests for a given query
   * (typically the user's new intention text). Returns [{ digest, distance }].
   * Returns [] if embeddings aren't available or no matches exist.
   */
  async function findRelevantDigests(queryText, k = 3) {
    if (!window.textEmbedderFunction || !queryText || queryText.length < 4) return [];
    try {
      const modelName = window.thread?.textEmbeddingModelName;
      const [qVec] = await window.embedTexts({ textArr: [queryText], modelName });
      if (!qVec) return [];
      const qArr = Array.from(qVec);
      const store = await _getEmbedStore();
      const memory = await getMemory();
      const digestsById = Object.fromEntries((memory.sessionDigests || []).map(d => [String(d.sessionId), d]));
      const scored = [];
      for (const [id, vec] of Object.entries(store.vectors)) {
        const d = digestsById[id];
        if (!d) continue; // digest was pruned, orphan vector
        scored.push({ digest: d, distance: cosineDistance(qArr, vec) });
      }
      scored.sort((a, b) => a.distance - b.distance);
      return scored.slice(0, k);
    } catch (e) { console.warn('findRelevantDigests failed:', e); return []; }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SHARE LINKS via uploadPlugin — publishes custom personas
  // and full session configs as shareable URLs. Falls back to hash-URL
  // for simple configs when uploadPlugin isn't available.
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * Upload a JSON payload via Perchance uploadPlugin and return a share URL.
   * Handles the `disallowed_content` error per Perchance skill guidance.
   * @returns {Promise<string|null>} Share URL or null on failure
   */
  async function createShareUpload(payload, opts = {}) {
    if (typeof root === 'undefined' || !root.uploadPlugin) return null;
    try {
      const json = JSON.stringify(payload);
      // Gzip client-side to fit larger configs under upload size limits.
      let blob;
      try {
        const stream = new Blob([json]).stream().pipeThrough(new CompressionStream('gzip'));
        blob = await new Response(stream).blob();
      } catch { blob = new Blob([json], { type: 'application/json' }); }
      const fileName = (opts.fileName || 'share') + '.' + Date.now() + '.gz';
      const file = new File([blob], fileName, { type: 'application/gzip' });
      // Per Perchance skill: uploadPlugin is called directly with a blob/file and returns { url, size, error }
      const uploaded = await root.uploadPlugin(file);
      if (!uploaded || !uploaded.url || uploaded.error) {
        throw new Error('Upload failed: ' + (uploaded?.error || 'no url returned'));
      }
      // url is like "https://user.uploads.dev/file/<filename>" — extract the filename for the share URL
      const uploadedFileName = uploaded.url.replace(/^https?:\/\/user\.uploads\.dev\/file\//, '');
      const base = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname;
      return `${base}?data=${encodeURIComponent(uploadedFileName)}`;
    } catch (e) {
      const msg = String(e?.message || e);
      if (msg.includes('disallowed_content')) {
        notify.error('Upload was rejected for disallowed content. If this persona/config is non-sexual and for adults, please report this — some content filters are overly strict.');
      } else {
        console.warn('createShareUpload failed:', e);
      }
      return null;
    }
  }

  /** Present a share-URL modal with copy button. */
  async function showShareLinkModal(url, title) {
    if (!url) { notify.warn('Could not create share link.'); return; }
    const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
    backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
    backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal" style="max-width:520px;">
      <h2>${escapeHtml(title || 'Share link')}</h2>
      <div style="font-size:0.82rem; color:var(--text-dim); line-height:1.55; margin-bottom:12px;">
        Anyone with this link can add this to their own library.
      </div>
      <input type="text" readonly id="_shareUrlInput" value="${escapeHtml(url)}"
        style="width:100%;padding:10px;background:var(--bg-softer);border:1px solid var(--glass-border);border-radius:6px;color:var(--text);font-family:monospace;font-size:0.78rem;">
      <div class="modal-actions">
        <button class="btn secondary" id="_shareClose">close</button>
        <button class="btn" id="_shareCopy">copy link</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
    document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
    const cleanup = () => backdrop.remove();
    backdrop.querySelector('#_shareClose').addEventListener('click', cleanup);
    backdrop.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup(); });
    backdrop.querySelector('#_shareCopy').addEventListener('click', async () => {
      try {
        await navigator.clipboard.writeText(url);
        notify.success('Share link copied to clipboard.');
      } catch {
        // Fallback — select the input so user can Cmd/Ctrl+C
        const input = backdrop.querySelector('#_shareUrlInput');
        input.select(); input.setSelectionRange(0, url.length);
        notify.info('Link selected — press Ctrl/Cmd+C to copy.');
      }
    });
    // Auto-select on open for easy keyboard copy
    setTimeout(() => {
      const input = backdrop.querySelector('#_shareUrlInput');
      if (input) { input.focus(); input.select(); }
    }, 50);
  }

  /** Share the current session config (persona + method + intention + settings). */
  async function shareCurrentConfig() {
    const payload = {
      version: 1,
      kind: 'session-config',
      createdAt: Date.now(),
      config: {
        selectedPersonaId: state.selectedPersonaId,
        selectedMethodId: state.selectedMethodId,
        intentionType: state.intentionType,
        length: state.length,
        soundscape: state.soundscape,
        vizOverride: state.vizOverride,
        speechRate: state.speechRate,
        voicePitch: state.voicePitch,
        tempoMultiplier: state.tempoMultiplier,
        affirmationMode: state.affirmationMode,
        intentionInput: $('intentionInput')?.value?.slice(0, 500) || '',
        userAffirmations: $('userAffirmations')?.value?.slice(0, 500) || '',
        // Include crafted suggestion if present (opt-in — only if user set one)
        craftedSuggestion: state.craftedSuggestion || null,
        // Optionally include generated script for a "share exact session"
        script: state.fullScript || null,
      },
      // Include custom persona definition IF the selected persona is custom —
      // otherwise recipient wouldn't have it.
      customPersona: (state.personas.find(p => p.id === state.selectedPersonaId)?.isCustom)
        ? state.personas.find(p => p.id === state.selectedPersonaId) : null,
    };
    setLoading('shareConfigBtn', true);
    try {
      const url = await createShareUpload(payload, { fileName: 'session-config' });
      if (url) {
        await showShareLinkModal(url, 'Share session config');
        await markFeatureUsed(FEAT.SHARE);
      } else {
        // Fallback: use the legacy hash-URL format (smaller, no upload)
        const params = new URLSearchParams();
        const c = payload.config;
        if (c.selectedPersonaId) params.set('p', c.selectedPersonaId);
        if (c.selectedMethodId) params.set('m', c.selectedMethodId);
        if (c.intentionType) params.set('i', c.intentionType);
        if (c.length) params.set('l', c.length);
        if (c.soundscape) params.set('s', c.soundscape);
        if (c.vizOverride) params.set('v', c.vizOverride);
        if (c.intentionInput) params.set('t', encodeURIComponent(c.intentionInput));
        if (c.userAffirmations) params.set('a', encodeURIComponent(c.userAffirmations));
        if (c.affirmationMode) params.set('am', c.affirmationMode);
        const fallback = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname + '#cfg=' + params.toString();
        await showShareLinkModal(fallback, 'Share session config (basic)');
      }
    } finally { setLoading('shareConfigBtn', false, '🔗 share link'); }
  }

  /** Share the persona currently open in the editor. */
  async function shareCurrentPersona() {
    const id = state.editingPersonaId;
    const name = $('personaFormName')?.value?.trim();
    const tagline = $('personaFormTagline')?.value?.trim();
    const category = $('personaFormCategory')?.value || 'contemplative';
    const systemPrompt = $('personaFormPrompt')?.value?.trim();
    if (!name || !systemPrompt) { notify.warn('Fill in name and voice instruction first.'); return; }
    const payload = {
      version: 1, kind: 'custom-persona', createdAt: Date.now(),
      persona: { id: id || ('shared-' + Date.now().toString(36)), name, tagline, category, systemPrompt, isCustom: true },
    };
    setLoading('personaShareBtn', true);
    try {
      const url = await createShareUpload(payload, { fileName: 'persona' });
      if (url) { await showShareLinkModal(url, 'Share persona'); await markFeatureUsed(FEAT.SHARE); }
      else notify.warn('Share link unavailable — uploadPlugin may not be loaded yet. Try again in a moment.');
    } finally { setLoading('personaShareBtn', false, '🔗 share'); }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // PHASE REGEN DIFF — when a user retries a phase, show the
  // old and new text side-by-side so they can pick the better one rather
  // than blindly overwriting.
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * @param {string} oldText  Original phase text
   * @param {string} newText  Newly generated phase text
   * @param {string} phaseLabel  Human-friendly label for modal header
   * @returns {Promise<'new'|'old'>} Which text to keep
   */
  function showPhaseDiffModal(oldText, newText, phaseLabel) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
      backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
      const wc = (t) => (t || '').trim().split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean).length;
      const oldW = wc(oldText), newW = wc(newText);
      backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal diff-modal">
        <h2>Compare: ${escapeHtml(phaseLabel)}</h2>
        <div style="font-size:0.8rem; color:var(--text-dim); line-height:1.55; margin-bottom:10px;">
          Pick which version to keep. You can always regenerate again.
        </div>
        <div class="diff-compare">
          <div class="diff-col diff-old">
            <div class="diff-col-label">← original</div>
            <div class="diff-col-text">${escapeHtml(oldText || '(empty)')}</div>
            <div class="diff-col-meta">${oldW} words</div>
          </div>
          <div class="diff-col diff-new">
            <div class="diff-col-label">new →</div>
            <div class="diff-col-text">${escapeHtml(newText || '(empty)')}</div>
            <div class="diff-col-meta">${newW} words</div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="modal-actions">
          <button class="btn secondary" id="_diffKeepOld">keep original</button>
          <button class="btn" id="_diffKeepNew">use new version</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
      const cleanup = (val) => { backdrop.remove(); resolve(val); };
      backdrop.querySelector('#_diffKeepOld').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup('old'));
      backdrop.querySelector('#_diffKeepNew').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup('new'));
      backdrop.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup('new'); });
    });
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SETTINGS PERSISTENCE (auto-save/load to localStorage)
  // ====================================================================
  const SETTINGS_KEY = 'stillness_settings_v5';
  const _kv = (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.kv) ? root.kv : null;
  let _saveTimeout = null;

  function _buildSettingsObj() {
    return {
      selectedPersonaId: state.selectedPersonaId,
      selectedMethodId: state.selectedMethodId,
      intentionType: state.intentionType,
      length: state.length,
      soundscape: state.soundscape,
      soundscapeOverridden: !!state._soundscapeOverridden,
      droneEnabled: state.droneEnabled,
      duckingEnabled: state.duckingEnabled,
      speechRate: state.speechRate,
      voicePitch: state.voicePitch,
      voiceVolume: state.voiceVolume,
      tempoMultiplier: state.tempoMultiplier,
      bgSource: state.bgSource,
      bgPrompt: state.bgPrompt,
      bgNegativePrompt: state.bgNegativePrompt,
      bgOrientation: state.bgOrientation,
      bgGuidance: state.bgGuidance,
      bgSteps: state.bgSteps,
      bgRotationSec: state.bgRotationSec,
      bgTransitionDuration: state.bgTransitionDuration,
      bgPlaybackOrder: state.bgPlaybackOrder,
      bgEnabledTransitions: state.bgEnabledTransitions,
      bgYoutubeUrl: state.bgYoutubeUrl,
      bgStaticUrl: state.bgStaticUrl,
      droneVolume: state.droneVolume,
      vizOverride: state.vizOverride,
      vizSettings: state.vizSettings,
      hud: state.hud,
      personaFilter: state.personaFilter,
      methodFilter: state.methodFilter,
      intentionInput: $('intentionInput')?.value || '',
      userAffirmations: $('userAffirmations')?.value || '',
      affirmationMode: $('affirmationMode')?.value || 'woven',
      voiceName: $('voiceSelect')?.value || '',
      remoteProcessingOptIn: !!$('remoteProcessingOptIn')?.checked,
      smartDirectorEnabled: !!$('smartDirectorEnabled')?.checked,
      directorBias: Number($('directorBiasSlider')?.value ?? state.directorBias ?? 0),
      settingsVersion: 5,
    };
  }

  function saveUserSettings() {
    clearTimeout(_saveTimeout);
    _saveTimeout = setTimeout(async () => {
      try {
        const settings = _buildSettingsObj();
        // Primary: Perchance KV storage (cloud-backed, cross-device)
        if (_kv) {
          await _kv.settings.set(SETTINGS_KEY, settings);
        }
        // Fallback: localStorage (local-only, survives page refresh)
        localStorage.setItem(SETTINGS_KEY, JSON.stringify(settings));
      } catch {}
    }, 1500);
  }

  function normalizeSettings(raw = {}) {
    const s = { ...(raw || {}) };
    if (s.voiceName == null) s.voiceName = s.narratorVoice || s.selectedVoice || s.voice || '';
    if (s.userAffirmations == null) s.userAffirmations = s.affirmations || s.customAffirmations || '';
    if (s.affirmationMode == null) s.affirmationMode = s.affirmMode || 'woven';
    if (s.vizSettings == null && s.visualSettings) s.vizSettings = s.visualSettings;
    if (s.vizOverride == null && s.visualMode) s.vizOverride = s.visualMode;
    if (s.tempoMultiplier == null && s.pauseTempo != null) s.tempoMultiplier = s.pauseTempo;
    if (s.length == null && s.sessionLength) s.length = s.sessionLength;
    if (s.intentionInput == null && s.intentionText) s.intentionInput = s.intentionText;
    if (s.remoteProcessingOptIn == null) s.remoteProcessingOptIn = !!(s.remoteBackupOptIn || s.cloudSyncOptIn || s.serverConsent);
    if (s.smartDirectorEnabled == null) s.smartDirectorEnabled = s.profileInjectionEnabled == null ? true : !!s.profileInjectionEnabled;
    if (s.directorBias == null) s.directorBias = 0;
    // Clamp to -3..+3 (slider range). Tolerates legacy/bad values without breaking the app.
    s.directorBias = Math.max(-3, Math.min(3, Math.round(Number(s.directorBias) || 0)));
    if (s.settingsVersion == null) s.settingsVersion = 1;
    return s;
  }

  function normalizeHistoryEntry(raw = {}) {
    const entry = { ...(raw || {}) };
    if (!entry.id) entry.id = entry.date || `legacy-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2)}`;
    if (!entry.date) entry.date = Date.now();
    if (entry.intentionText == null) entry.intentionText = entry.intentionInput || entry.prompt || '';
    if (entry.userAffirmations == null) entry.userAffirmations = entry.affirmations || entry.customAffirmations || '';
    if (entry.affirmationMode == null) entry.affirmationMode = entry.affirmMode || 'woven';
    if (entry.voiceName == null) entry.voiceName = entry.narratorVoice || entry.selectedVoice || '';
    if (entry.workBlockCount == null && entry.metrics?.workBlocks != null) entry.workBlockCount = entry.metrics.workBlocks;
    if (!Array.isArray(entry.phaseOrder) || !entry.phaseOrder.length) {
      try {
        if (entry.script) {
          const parsed = parseScript(entry.script);
          entry.phaseOrder = parsed?.ordered?.length ? parsed.ordered : (entry.phaseOrder || []);
        }
      } catch {}
    }
    if (entry.workflowVersion == null) entry.workflowVersion = entry.stepsTotal === 6 ? 10 : 9;
    if (entry.stepsTotal == null) entry.stepsTotal = entry.workflowVersion >= 10 ? 6 : 5;
    return entry;
  }

  function normalizeAnalyticsData(data) {
    const base = {
      v: 3,
      p: {}, m: {}, i: {}, s: {}, z: {}, ln: {}, am: {}, vc: {},
      hr: new Array(24).fill(0), dw: new Array(7).fill(0),
      mood: { preSum: 0, postSum: 0, deltaSum: 0, n: 0, postN: 0 },
      comp: { total: 0, finished: 0, emergency: 0 },
      dur: { sum: 0, n: 0 },
      shape: { phaseSum: 0, workSum: 0, affirmSum: 0, n: 0 },
      cfg: { rateSum: 0, pitchSum: 0, volSum: 0, droneSum: 0, n: 0 },
      feat: 0,
      ts: Date.now(),
    };
    const a = { ...base, ...(data || {}) };
    a.v = 3;
    a.p = a.p || {}; a.m = a.m || {}; a.i = a.i || {}; a.s = a.s || {}; a.z = a.z || {}; a.ln = a.ln || {};
    a.am = a.am || {}; a.vc = a.vc || {};
    a.hr = Array.isArray(a.hr) ? Array.from({length:24}, (_,i)=>Number(a.hr[i]||0)) : base.hr.slice();
    a.dw = Array.isArray(a.dw) ? Array.from({length:7}, (_,i)=>Number(a.dw[i]||0)) : base.dw.slice();
    a.mood = { ...base.mood, ...(a.mood || {}) };
    a.comp = { ...base.comp, ...(a.comp || {}) };
    a.dur = { ...base.dur, ...(a.dur || {}) };
    a.shape = { ...base.shape, ...(a.shape || {}) };
    a.cfg = { ...base.cfg, ...(a.cfg || {}) };
    return a;
  }

  function mergeAnalyticsData(existing, incoming) {
    const a = normalizeAnalyticsData(existing);
    const b = normalizeAnalyticsData(incoming);
    const sumMaps = ['p','m','i','s','z','ln','am','vc'];
    for (const key of sumMaps) {
      for (const [k,v] of Object.entries(b[key] || {})) a[key][k] = (a[key][k] || 0) + (Number(v) || 0);
    }
    a.hr = a.hr.map((v,i) => v + (Number(b.hr[i]) || 0));
    a.dw = a.dw.map((v,i) => v + (Number(b.dw[i]) || 0));
    for (const k of ['preSum','postSum','deltaSum','n','postN']) a.mood[k] = (a.mood[k] || 0) + (b.mood[k] || 0);
    for (const k of ['total','finished','emergency']) a.comp[k] = (a.comp[k] || 0) + (b.comp[k] || 0);
    for (const k of ['sum','n']) a.dur[k] = (a.dur[k] || 0) + (b.dur[k] || 0);
    for (const k of ['phaseSum','workSum','affirmSum','n']) a.shape[k] = (a.shape[k] || 0) + (b.shape[k] || 0);
    for (const k of ['rateSum','pitchSum','volSum','droneSum','n']) a.cfg[k] = (a.cfg[k] || 0) + (b.cfg[k] || 0);
    a.feat = (a.feat || 0) | (b.feat || 0);
    a.ts = Math.max(a.ts || 0, b.ts || 0, Date.now());
    return a;
  }

  async function loadUserSettings() {
    try {
      let s = null;
      // Try Perchance KV first (cloud-backed)
      if (_kv) {
        try { s = await _kv.settings.get(SETTINGS_KEY); } catch {}
      }
      // Fallback to localStorage
      if (!s) {
        const raw = localStorage.getItem(SETTINGS_KEY) || localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v4') || localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v3') || localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v2');
        if (raw) s = JSON.parse(raw);
      }
      if (!s) return false;
      s = normalizeSettings(s);

      if (s.selectedPersonaId) state.selectedPersonaId = s.selectedPersonaId;
      if (s.selectedMethodId) state.selectedMethodId = s.selectedMethodId;
      if (s.intentionType) { state.intentionType = s.intentionType; const el = $('intentionType'); if (el) el.value = s.intentionType; }
      if (s.length) { state.length = s.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = s.length; }
      if (s.soundscape != null) { state.soundscape = s.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = s.soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = s.soundscape; }
      if (s.soundscapeOverridden) state._soundscapeOverridden = true;
      if (s.speechRate != null) { state.speechRate = s.speechRate; const el = $('speechRate'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.speechRate * 100); const v = $('speechRateVal'); if (v) v.textContent = s.speechRate.toFixed(2) + '×'; }
      if (s.voicePitch != null) { state.voicePitch = s.voicePitch; const el = $('voicePitch'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.voicePitch * 100); const v = $('voicePitchVal'); if (v) v.textContent = s.voicePitch.toFixed(2); }
      if (s.voiceVolume != null) { state.voiceVolume = s.voiceVolume; const el = $('voiceVolume'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.voiceVolume * 100); const v = $('voiceVolVal'); if (v) v.textContent = Math.round(s.voiceVolume * 100); }
      if (s.tempoMultiplier != null) { state.tempoMultiplier = s.tempoMultiplier; const el = $('tempoSlider'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.tempoMultiplier * 100); const v = $('tempoVal'); if (v) v.textContent = s.tempoMultiplier.toFixed(1) + '×'; }
      if (s.bgSource) {
        // File objects don't survive reload; if a local file source was saved
        // but state._bgFile is missing, fall back to 'none' to avoid a broken bg at session start.
        let restoredSource = s.bgSource;
        if ((restoredSource === 'local-image' || restoredSource === 'local-video') && !state._bgFile) {
          restoredSource = 'none';
        }
        state.bgSource = restoredSource;
        const el = $('bgSourceSelect');
        if (el) { el.value = restoredSource; el.dispatchEvent(new Event('change')); }
      }
      if (s.bgPrompt) { state.bgPrompt = s.bgPrompt; const el = $('bgPromptInput'); if (el) el.value = s.bgPrompt; }
      if (s.bgNegativePrompt != null) {
        state.bgNegativePrompt = s.bgNegativePrompt;
        const el = $('bgNegativePromptInput'); if (el) el.value = s.bgNegativePrompt;
      }
      if (s.bgOrientation) {
        state.bgOrientation = s.bgOrientation;
        const el = $('bgOrientationSelect'); if (el) el.value = s.bgOrientation;
      }
      if (s.bgGuidance != null) {
        state.bgGuidance = Number(s.bgGuidance);
        const el = $('bgGuidanceSlider'); if (el) el.value = state.bgGuidance;
        const lbl = $('bgGuidanceVal'); if (lbl) lbl.textContent = state.bgGuidance;
      }
      if (s.bgSteps != null) {
        state.bgSteps = Number(s.bgSteps);
        const el = $('bgStepsSlider'); if (el) el.value = state.bgSteps;
        const lbl = $('bgStepsVal'); if (lbl) lbl.textContent = state.bgSteps;
      }
      if (s.bgRotationSec != null) {
        state.bgRotationSec = Number(s.bgRotationSec);
        const el = $('bgRotationSlider'); if (el) el.value = state.bgRotationSec;
        const lbl = $('bgRotationVal'); if (lbl) lbl.textContent = state.bgRotationSec;
        const hint = $('bgRotationHint'); if (hint) hint.textContent = state.bgRotationSec;
      }
      if (s.bgTransitionDuration != null) {
        state.bgTransitionDuration = Number(s.bgTransitionDuration);
        const el = $('bgTransitionDurSlider'); if (el) el.value = state.bgTransitionDuration;
        const lbl = $('bgTransitionDurVal'); if (lbl) lbl.textContent = state.bgTransitionDuration.toFixed(1);
      }
      if (s.bgPlaybackOrder) {
        state.bgPlaybackOrder = s.bgPlaybackOrder;
        const seg = $('bgOrderSeg');
        if (seg) seg.querySelectorAll('button').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.order === s.bgPlaybackOrder));
      }
      if (Array.isArray(s.bgEnabledTransitions)) {
        // Filter against the current registry — keys may have been renamed/removed
        state.bgEnabledTransitions = s.bgEnabledTransitions.filter(k => BG_TRANSITIONS[k]);
        if (typeof buildBgTransitionGrid === 'function') buildBgTransitionGrid();
      }
      if (s.bgYoutubeUrl) { state.bgYoutubeUrl = s.bgYoutubeUrl; const el = $('bgYoutubeUrl'); if (el) el.value = s.bgYoutubeUrl; }
      if (s.bgStaticUrl) { state.bgStaticUrl = s.bgStaticUrl; const el = $('bgUrlInput'); if (el) el.value = s.bgStaticUrl; }
      if (s.droneVolume != null) { state.droneVolume = s.droneVolume; const el = $('droneVolume'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.droneVolume * 100); const v = $('droneVolVal'); if (v) v.textContent = Math.round(s.droneVolume * 100); }
      if (s.vizOverride != null) { state.vizOverride = s.vizOverride; const el = $('vizSelect'); if (el) el.value = s.vizOverride; }
      if (s.hud) state.hud = { ...state.hud, ...s.hud };
      if (s.duckingEnabled != null) { state.duckingEnabled = s.duckingEnabled; const el = $('duckingToggle'); if (el) el.checked = s.duckingEnabled; }
      if (s.vizSettings) {
        state.vizSettings = { ...state.vizSettings, ...s.vizSettings };
        const vs = state.vizSettings;
        const speedEl = $('vizSpeed'); if (speedEl) { speedEl.value = Math.round(vs.speed * 100); const v = $('vizSpeedVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.speed.toFixed(1) + '×'; }
        const intEl = $('vizIntensity'); if (intEl) { intEl.value = Math.round(vs.intensity * 100); const v = $('vizIntensityVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.intensity.toFixed(1) + '×'; }
        const cmpEl = $('vizComplexity'); if (cmpEl) { cmpEl.value = Math.round(vs.complexity * 100); const v = $('vizComplexityVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.complexity.toFixed(1) + '×'; }
        const trEl = $('vizTrail'); if (trEl) { trEl.value = Math.round(vs.trail * 100); const v = $('vizTrailVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.trail.toFixed(2); }
      }
      // Restore HUD toggle checkboxes
      const hudMap = { fixationDot:'cfgFixationDot', textDisplay:'cfgTextDisplay', phaseDots:'cfgPhaseDots', phaseLabel:'cfgPhaseLabel', progressBar:'cfgProgressBar', sessionTime:'cfgSessionTime', labels:'cfgLabels' };
      for (const [key, elId] of Object.entries(hudMap)) { const el = $(elId); if (el) el.checked = state.hud[key] !== false; }
      // Restore filter tabs
      if (s.personaFilter) state.personaFilter = s.personaFilter;
      if (s.methodFilter) state.methodFilter = s.methodFilter;
      if (s.intentionInput) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = s.intentionInput; }
      if (s.userAffirmations != null) { const el = $('userAffirmations'); if (el) el.value = s.userAffirmations; }
      if (s.affirmationMode) { const el = $('affirmationMode'); if (el) el.value = s.affirmationMode; state.affirmationMode = s.affirmationMode; }
      if (s.voiceName) state._savedVoiceName = s.voiceName;
      state.remoteProcessingOptIn = !!s.remoteProcessingOptIn;
      const rpcb = $('remoteProcessingOptIn'); if (rpcb) rpcb.checked = !!state.remoteProcessingOptIn;
      state.smartDirectorEnabled = s.smartDirectorEnabled !== false;
      const sdcb = $('smartDirectorEnabled'); if (sdcb) sdcb.checked = state.smartDirectorEnabled;
      state.directorBias = s.directorBias ?? 0;
      const dbSlider = $('directorBiasSlider'); if (dbSlider) dbSlider.value = state.directorBias;
      _updateDirectorBiasUI(); // update label + enabled state
      applySavedVoiceSelection();
      updateVoiceInfo();
      return true;
    } catch { return false; }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // USER PROFILE (bio, appearance, goals — for AI personalization)
  // ====================================================================
  const PROFILE_KEY = 'stillness_profile_v1';
  let _profileSaveTimeout = null;

  function getProfile() {
    return {
      name: $('pfName')?.value?.trim() || '',
      useFirstName: !!$('pfUseFirstName')?.checked,
      pronouns: $('pfPronouns')?.value || '',
      age: $('pfAge')?.value || '',
      experience: $('pfExperience')?.value || 'beginner',
      about: $('pfAbout')?.value?.trim() || '',
      appearance: $('pfAppearance')?.value?.trim() || '',
      goals: $('pfGoals')?.value?.trim() || '',
    };
  }

  function applyProfileToForm(profile, opts = {}) {
    const p = profile || {};
    const setVal = (id, value, fallback = '') => {
      const el = $(id);
      if (el) el.value = value ?? fallback;
    };
    setVal('pfName', p.name, '');
    // Backward-compat: older profiles without useFirstName default to false (privacy-safe).
    const useName = $('pfUseFirstName');
    if (useName) useName.checked = !!p.useFirstName;
    setVal('pfPronouns', p.pronouns, '');
    setVal('pfAge', p.age, '');
    setVal('pfExperience', p.experience, 'beginner');
    setVal('pfAbout', p.about, '');
    setVal('pfAppearance', p.appearance, '');
    setVal('pfGoals', p.goals, '');
    const nameEl = $('sidebarDisplayName');
    if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = p.name || 'Practitioner';
    if (opts.save !== false) saveProfile();
  }

  function saveProfile() {
    clearTimeout(_profileSaveTimeout);
    _profileSaveTimeout = setTimeout(async () => {
      try {
        const profile = getProfile();
        if (_kv) await _kv.settings.set(PROFILE_KEY, profile);
        localStorage.setItem(PROFILE_KEY, JSON.stringify(profile));
        // Update sidebar display name
        const nameEl = $('sidebarDisplayName');
        if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = profile.name || 'Practitioner';
      } catch {}
    }, 1000);
  }

  async function loadProfile() {
    try {
      let p = null;
      if (_kv) { try { p = await _kv.settings.get(PROFILE_KEY); } catch {} }
      if (!p) { const raw = localStorage.getItem(PROFILE_KEY); if (raw) p = JSON.parse(raw); }
      if (!p) return;
      applyProfileToForm(p, { save: false });
    } catch {}
  }

  /** Build an AI context string from the user's profile for prompt injection */
  function getProfileContext() {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('getProfileContext returning empty — Smart Director off');
      return '';
    }
    const p = getProfile();
    const parts = [];
    // Only pass the subject's name to the AI when the user has opted in.
    if (p.name && p.useFirstName) parts.push(`The subject's name is ${p.name}. You may address them by name occasionally; do not overuse it.`);
    if (p.pronouns) parts.push(`Pronouns: ${p.pronouns}.`);
    if (p.age) parts.push(`Age range: ${p.age}.`);
    if (p.experience) parts.push(`Experience: ${p.experience}.`);
    if (p.about) parts.push(`About the subject: ${p.about}.`);
    if (p.appearance) parts.push(`Appearance: ${p.appearance}.`);
    if (p.goals) parts.push(`Goals: ${p.goals}.`);
    const result = parts.length > 0 ? '\nSUBJECT PROFILE: ' + parts.join(' ') : '';
    sdLog('getProfileContext built', { fieldCount: parts.length, charCount: result.length });
    return result;
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // LIVING PROFILE + DIRECTOR BRIEF
  // ====================================================================
  // Merges profile + memory + adaptive + history into one on-demand view, then
  // runs rule-based logic over it to produce a session brief. No new persistence
  // layer — source stores own their data.
  //
  // IMPORTANT: director logic stays RULE-BASED. AI-inferred clinical judgment is
  // a slippery slope this app should not take.

  /**
   * Build a unified "living profile" by merging user-edited profile + AI-observed
   * memory summaries + adaptive signals + recent session snapshot.
   *
   * Pure read — does not write anywhere. Returns `null` when Smart Director is
   * off OR when any underlying read fails.
   *
   * @returns {Promise<object|null>}
   */
  async function buildLivingProfile() {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('buildLivingProfile skipped — Smart Director off');
      return null;
    }
    try {
      const stated = getProfile();
      const memory = await getMemory();
      const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
      const history = ((await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || []).map(normalizeHistoryEntry);
      const analytics = await getAnalytics();

      // Recent mood trajectory — last 5 completed sessions with both pre+post scores.
      // Index 0 = most recent. A negative value = user felt worse after the session.
      const moodSessions = history.filter(s => s.completed && s.preMood != null && s.postMood != null).slice(0, 5);
      const recentMoodDeltas = moodSessions.map(s => s.postMood - s.preMood);
      const avgRecentMoodDelta = recentMoodDeltas.length > 0
        ? recentMoodDeltas.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / recentMoodDeltas.length
        : null;

      // Completion rate over last 10 — captures "bailing" patterns earlier than
      // the lifetime rate from analytics.comp which dilutes with history.
      const recent10 = history.slice(0, 10);
      const completionRate = recent10.length > 0
        ? recent10.filter(s => s.completed).length / recent10.length
        : null;

      // Average self-rated depth in recent sessions — helps calibrate next session.
      const recentDepths = history.slice(0, 5).map(s => s.depth).filter(d => d != null);
      const avgRecentDepth = recentDepths.length > 0
        ? recentDepths.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / recentDepths.length
        : null;

      // Top preference signals from analytics (what the user reaches for most).
      const topKey = (map) => {
        const entries = Object.entries(map || {});
        if (!entries.length) return null;
        return entries.sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0][0];
      };

      const living = {
        version: 1,
        updatedAt: Date.now(),
        stated: {
          name: stated.name,
          useFirstName: stated.useFirstName,
          pronouns: stated.pronouns,
          age: stated.age,
          experience: stated.experience,
          about: stated.about,
          appearance: stated.appearance,
          goals: stated.goals,
        },
        observed: {
          longTermProfile: memory.longTermProfile || '',
          rollingPatterns: memory.rollingWindow || '',
          digestCount: memory.sessionDigests?.length || 0,
        },
        adaptive: {
          traits: adaptive.traits || {},
          difficulty: adaptive.difficulty || {},
          memorySummary: adaptive.memorySummary || '',
          topPersona: topKey(analytics.p),
          topMethod: topKey(analytics.m),
          topIntention: topKey(analytics.i),
        },
        snapshot: {
          sessionCount: history.length,
          completedCount: history.filter(s => s.completed).length,
          emergencyExitCount: analytics.comp?.emergency || 0,
          completionRate,
          recentMoodDeltas,
          avgRecentMoodDelta,
          avgRecentDepth,
          lastSessionAt: history[0]?.date || null,
          daysSinceLast: history[0]?.date
            ? Math.floor((Date.now() - history[0].date) / 86400000)
            : null,
        },
      };

      sdLog('buildLivingProfile', living);
      return living;
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('buildLivingProfile failed:', e);
      return null;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Compute a structured Director Brief from the living profile. Rule-based —
   * every recommendation includes a plain-English reason that can be surfaced
   * to the user (Pass 3).
   *
   * Cold-start (fewer than 3 completed sessions): returns a brief with
   * `coldStart: true` and no active recommendations, so the AI falls back to
   * defaults rather than pretending expertise the app hasn't earned.
   *
   * @param {object|null} living     output of buildLivingProfile()
   * @param {object}       session   { persona, method, intention, length }
   * @returns {object|null}
   */
  function computeDirectorBrief(living, session = {}) {
    if (!living) return null;
    const snap = living.snapshot;
    // User-adjustable bias, -3..+3. Negative = lean cautious (easier triggers,
    // stricter caps); positive = lean forward (harder triggers, looser caps).
    // Clamped defensively in case the setting is stale or out of range.
    const bias = Math.max(-3, Math.min(3, Math.round(Number(state.directorBias) || 0)));
    const brief = {
      generatedAt: Date.now(),
      bias,
      forSession: {
        persona: session.persona || null,
        method: session.method || null,
        intention: session.intention || null,
        length: session.length || null,
      },
      coldStart: false,
      recoveryMode: false,
      recommendations: {}, // { suggestedDepth, suggestedLength, skipIntensification, maxDepth, preferBreath }
      warnings: [],        // user-facing flags
      reasoning: [],       // plain-English rationale (one entry per rule that fired)
    };

    // Bias-adjusted thresholds. The math is deliberately simple — each step
    // moves the threshold by a human-meaningful unit, so moving one notch
    // produces an observable shift without flipping the app's personality.
    const coldStartLimit     = Math.max(0, 3 - bias);           // B=-3: 6, 0: 3, +3: 0 (no cold start)
    const recoveryMoodLimit  = -2 - bias * 0.5;                  // B=-3: -0.5 (easy), 0: -2, +3: -3.5 (hard)
    const completionFloor    = 0.5 - bias * 0.05;                // B=-3: 0.65, 0: 0.5, +3: 0.35
    const daysSinceRentry    = 14 + bias * 3;                    // B=-3: 5, 0: 14, +3: 23
    const positivePacingFloor = 1.5 - bias * 0.3;                // B=-3: 2.4 (harder to praise), +3: 0.6 (easier)
    sdLog('computeDirectorBrief thresholds', { bias, coldStartLimit, recoveryMoodLimit, completionFloor, daysSinceRentry, positivePacingFloor });

    // --- Cold start -----------------------------------------------------
    if (snap.completedCount < coldStartLimit) {
      brief.coldStart = true;
      brief.reasoning.push(
        snap.completedCount === 0
          ? 'No completed sessions yet — using defaults and keeping things grounded.'
          : `Only ${snap.completedCount} completed session${snap.completedCount === 1 ? '' : 's'} so far — still calibrating.`
      );
      sdLog('computeDirectorBrief: cold start', brief);
      return brief;
    }

    // --- Recovery mode: 3+ consecutive strongly negative mood deltas -----
    // A "strongly negative" delta is ≤ recoveryMoodLimit on the 1–10 mood scale.
    const lastThree = snap.recentMoodDeltas.slice(0, 3);
    if (lastThree.length === 3 && lastThree.every(d => d <= recoveryMoodLimit)) {
      brief.recoveryMode = true;
      brief.recommendations.suggestedDepth = 'light';
      brief.recommendations.suggestedLength = 'short';
      brief.recommendations.skipIntensification = true;
      brief.warnings.push('Last 3 sessions ended with notable mood decline.');
      brief.reasoning.push(`Recovery mode triggered — recent sessions trended mood-negative (threshold ≤ ${recoveryMoodLimit}). Recommending a gentler, shorter session and skipping intensification.`);
      sdLog('computeDirectorBrief: recovery mode', brief);
      return brief;
    }

    // --- Low completion rate → shorter sessions -------------------------
    if (snap.completionRate != null && snap.completionRate < completionFloor) {
      brief.recommendations.suggestedLength = 'short';
      brief.warnings.push(`Recent completion rate is ${Math.round(snap.completionRate * 100)}%.`);
      brief.reasoning.push(`Recent completion rate is low (${Math.round(snap.completionRate * 100)}% < ${Math.round(completionFloor * 100)}%) — suggest a shorter session to rebuild the habit.`);
    }

    // --- Emergency-exit history → cap depth -----------------------------
    // Capped in both directions — emergency exits are a hard safety signal that
    // bias shouldn't fully suppress. At bias +3, still cap if 3+ exits on short history.
    const emergencyCap = bias >= 3 ? 3 : 2;
    if (snap.emergencyExitCount >= emergencyCap && snap.completedCount < 10) {
      brief.recommendations.maxDepth = 'medium';
      brief.reasoning.push(`${snap.emergencyExitCount} emergency exits on record with limited completed history — capping suggested depth at medium.`);
    }

    // --- Beginner cap ---------------------------------------------------
    // Beginner cap is a safety feature; bias can soften it but not skip entirely.
    if (living.stated.experience === 'beginner' && bias < 3) {
      brief.recommendations.maxDepth = brief.recommendations.maxDepth || 'medium';
      brief.reasoning.push('Self-identifies as beginner — capping suggested depth at medium.');
    }

    // --- Positive reinforcement — current pacing works ------------------
    if (snap.avgRecentMoodDelta != null && snap.avgRecentMoodDelta >= positivePacingFloor) {
      brief.reasoning.push(`Average mood delta is +${snap.avgRecentMoodDelta.toFixed(1)} — current pacing is working; stay the course.`);
    }

    // --- Long gap since last session ------------------------------------
    if (snap.daysSinceLast != null && snap.daysSinceLast >= daysSinceRentry) {
      brief.recommendations.suggestedDepth = brief.recommendations.suggestedDepth || 'light';
      brief.reasoning.push(`${snap.daysSinceLast} days since last session (≥ ${daysSinceRentry}) — treat as a re-entry and keep this one gentle.`);
    }

    sdLog('computeDirectorBrief', brief);
    return brief;
  }

  /**
   * Turn a Director Brief into a short prompt block for AI injection. Stays
   * under ~300 characters so it rarely gets dropped by trimToTokenBudget.
   *
   * Appends a tone directive derived from the Director calibration bias so
   * the AI's language leans cautious or forward in sympathy with the user's
   * manual correction — even when no rule fires.
   */
  function formatDirectorBriefForPrompt(brief) {
    if (!brief) return '';
    const parts = [];
    const bias = brief.bias || 0;

    if (brief.coldStart) {
      const coldBase = 'Early practitioner — follow defaults and keep the session welcoming and grounded.';
      const toneNote = _toneDirectiveFromBias(bias);
      return '\nDIRECTOR BRIEF: ' + coldBase + (toneNote ? ' ' + toneNote : '');
    }

    if (brief.recoveryMode) {
      parts.push('Recovery mode — keep this session lighter and shorter than usual. No intensification, no peak-state work. Gentle, supportive, reassuring tone.');
    }

    const r = brief.recommendations;
    const directives = [];
    if (r.suggestedDepth) directives.push(`aim for ${r.suggestedDepth} depth`);
    if (r.maxDepth)       directives.push(`do not exceed ${r.maxDepth} depth`);
    if (r.suggestedLength)directives.push(`favor a ${r.suggestedLength}-length pacing`);
    if (r.skipIntensification && !brief.recoveryMode) directives.push('skip intensification language');
    if (directives.length) parts.push('Adjustments: ' + directives.join('; ') + '.');

    const toneNote = _toneDirectiveFromBias(bias);
    if (toneNote) parts.push(toneNote);

    if (parts.length === 0) return '';
    return '\nDIRECTOR BRIEF: ' + parts.join(' ');
  }

  /** Bias → plain-English tone directive for the AI. Empty at bias=0. */
  function _toneDirectiveFromBias(bias) {
    if (bias <= -2) return 'Tone calibration: favor grounded, careful, gently reassuring language. Avoid pushing intensity or urgency.';
    if (bias === -1) return 'Tone calibration: lean slightly cautious and unhurried.';
    if (bias === 1)  return 'Tone calibration: lean slightly forward with warm momentum.';
    if (bias >= 2)  return 'Tone calibration: favor forward-momentum, energizing language. Trust the practitioner to engage fully with deeper work.';
    return '';
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TOKEN SUBSTITUTION — Perchance-chat-style \{\{placeholder\}\} system
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * Replaces double-curly-brace tokens in text with real values. Inspired by
   * Perchance AI Character Chat's \{\{user\}\} / \{\{char\}\} convention so users
   * writing or editing hypnosis scripts have a familiar substitution syntax.
   *
   * Supported tokens:
   *   \{\{user\}\}        -> the listener's first name (if checkbox on) or "you" (generic)
   *   \{\{nar\}\} / \{\{guide\}\} / \{\{persona\}\}
   *                   -> the active persona's name ("Aria", "Dr. Vale", etc.)
   *   \{\{intention\}\}   -> the short intention phrase from the intention step
   *   \{\{affirmation\}\} -> one of the user's affirmations (picked for variety —
   *                     multiple \{\{affirmation\}\} tokens rotate through the list)
   *
   * Unresolved tokens are left alone so a downstream pass (or the AI itself)
   * can handle them. Called both pre-prompt (so AI sees resolved values in
   * the generation context) and pre-TTS (so user edits with live tokens work).
   *
   * @param {string} text   Source text possibly containing \{\{...\}\} tokens.
   * @param {object} [opts] Overrides: { user, persona, intention, affirmations[] }.
   * @returns {string}
   */
  function resolveTokens(text, opts = {}) {
    if (!text || typeof text !== 'string') return text || '';
    if (text.indexOf('\u007B\u007B') === -1) return text; // fast path — no tokens present

    // Profile → \{\{user\}\}
    const profile = opts.profile || getProfile();
    const useName = !!profile.useFirstName && !!profile.name;
    const userValue = opts.user != null ? String(opts.user) : (useName ? profile.name : 'you');

    // Persona → \{\{nar\}\} \{\{guide\}\} \{\{persona\}\}
    let narValue = opts.persona;
    if (narValue == null) {
      try { narValue = getPersona()?.name || ''; } catch { narValue = ''; }
    }
    narValue = narValue || 'the narrator';

    // Intention → \{\{intention\}\}
    let intentionValue = opts.intention;
    if (intentionValue == null) {
      intentionValue = ($('intentionInput')?.value || '').trim();
    }

    // Affirmations → \{\{affirmation\}\} (rotates through list)
    let affirmArr = opts.affirmations;
    if (!Array.isArray(affirmArr)) {
      const raw = ($('userAffirmations')?.value || '').trim();
      affirmArr = raw ? raw.split(/\r?\n/).map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
    }
    let affirmIdx = 0;
    const nextAffirm = () => {
      if (!affirmArr.length) return '';
      const v = affirmArr[affirmIdx % affirmArr.length];
      affirmIdx++;
      return v;
    };

    // Replace using a single-pass regex. Token names are case-insensitive and
    // tolerate surrounding whitespace: \{\{ user \}\} works the same as \{\{user\}\}.
    return text.replace(/\{\{\s*([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\s*\}\}/g, (match, rawName) => {
      const name = rawName.toLowerCase();
      switch (name) {
        case 'user':        return userValue;
        case 'nar':
        case 'guide':
        case 'persona':     return narValue;
        case 'intention':   return intentionValue || match; // leave if empty
        case 'affirmation': return nextAffirm() || match;
        default:            return match; // unknown token — pass through for upstream handling
      }
    });
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // USAGE ANALYTICS — compact incremental aggregation (O(1) storage)
  // ====================================================================
  const ANALYTICS_KEY = 'stillness_analytics_v3';

  /** Get or initialize the analytics store */
  async function getAnalytics() {
    try {
      const data = await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY) || await idbGet('stillness_analytics_v2');
      if (data) return normalizeAnalyticsData(data);
    } catch {}
    return {
      v: 3,
      // Frequency maps: { id: count }
      p: {},   // persona usage
      m: {},   // method usage
      i: {},   // intention type usage
      s: {},   // soundscape usage
      z: {},   // visual effect usage
      ln: {},  // session length usage
      am: {},  // affirmation mode usage
      vc: {},  // narrator voice usage
      // Time patterns
      hr: new Array(24).fill(0),  // hourly distribution (0-23)
      dw: new Array(7).fill(0),   // day-of-week (0=Sun..6=Sat)
      // Mood & completion
      mood: { preSum: 0, postSum: 0, deltaSum: 0, n: 0, postN: 0 },
      comp: { total: 0, finished: 0, emergency: 0 },
      dur: { sum: 0, n: 0 },
      shape: { phaseSum: 0, workSum: 0, affirmSum: 0, n: 0 },
      // Settings usage (running sums for averages)
      cfg: { rateSum: 0, pitchSum: 0, volSum: 0, droneSum: 0, n: 0 },
      // Feature flags: which features the user has tried
      feat: 0, // bitmask: 1=affirmations 2=programs 4=custom-persona 8=skip-to-script 16=timing-fixer 32=share 64=backup 128=double-induction
      // Timestamp
      ts: Date.now(),
    };
  }

  /** Record a completed session into the analytics store */
  async function recordAnalytics(record, wasEmergency) {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('recordAnalytics skipped — Smart Director off');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();

      // Frequency tallies (increment counters)
      const inc = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + 1; };
      inc(a.p, record.personaId);
      inc(a.m, record.methodId);
      inc(a.i, record.intention);
      inc(a.s, record.soundscape);
      inc(a.z, record.vizOverride || state.vizOverride || 'auto');
      inc(a.ln, record.length);
      inc(a.am, record.affirmationMode || 'woven');
      inc(a.vc, record.voiceName || 'default');

      // Time patterns
      const d = new Date(record.date);
      a.hr[d.getHours()] = (a.hr[d.getHours()] || 0) + 1;
      a.dw[d.getDay()] = (a.dw[d.getDay()] || 0) + 1;

      // Mood tracking
      if (record.preMood != null) {
        a.mood.preSum += record.preMood;
        a.mood.n++;
      }

      // Completion
      a.comp.total++;
      if (wasEmergency) a.comp.emergency++;
      else if (record.completed) a.comp.finished++;

      // Duration
      if (record.durationSec > 0) {
        a.dur.sum += record.durationSec;
        a.dur.n++;
      }

      // Settings averages
      a.cfg.rateSum += (record.speechRate || 0.65);
      a.cfg.pitchSum += (record.voicePitch || 0.85);
      a.cfg.volSum += (record.voiceVolume ?? 1.0);
      a.cfg.droneSum += (record.droneVolume ?? 0.35);
      a.cfg.n++;

      const metrics = record.metrics || {};
      a.shape.phaseSum += metrics.phaseCount || (Array.isArray(record.phaseOrder) ? record.phaseOrder.length : 0);
      a.shape.workSum += record.workBlockCount || metrics.workBlocks || 0;
      a.shape.affirmSum += metrics.affirmBlocks || 0;
      a.shape.n++;

      a.ts = Date.now();
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch(e) { console.error('Analytics write failed:', e); }
  }

  /** Update post-session mood in analytics */
  async function recordPostMood(postVal) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      a.mood.postSum += postVal;
      a.mood.deltaSum += postVal - (state._preMood ?? 5);
      a.mood.postN = (a.mood.postN || 0) + 1; // separate counter — not every session fills post-mood
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch {}
  }

  /** Set a feature-used flag (bitmask) */
  async function markFeatureUsed(bit) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      if (!(a.feat & bit)) {
        a.feat |= bit;
        await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
      }
    } catch {}
  }

  // Feature bit constants
  const FEAT = { AFFIRMATIONS: 1, PROGRAMS: 2, CUSTOM_PERSONA: 4, SKIP_SCRIPT: 8, TIMING_FIX: 16, SHARE: 32, BACKUP: 64, DOUBLE_INDUCT: 128 };

  /** Rebuild analytics from remaining history — called after deletes to keep data consistent */
  async function rebuildAnalytics(historyArr) {
    try {
      const existing = await getAnalytics();
      const feat = existing.feat || 0; // preserve feature flags
      const a = { v: 3, p: {}, m: {}, i: {}, s: {}, z: {}, ln: {}, am: {}, vc: {},
        hr: new Array(24).fill(0), dw: new Array(7).fill(0),
        mood: { preSum: 0, postSum: 0, deltaSum: 0, n: 0, postN: 0 },
        comp: { total: 0, finished: 0, emergency: 0 },
        dur: { sum: 0, n: 0 }, shape: { phaseSum: 0, workSum: 0, affirmSum: 0, n: 0 }, cfg: { rateSum: 0, pitchSum: 0, volSum: 0, droneSum: 0, n: 0 },
        feat, ts: Date.now() };
      const inc = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + 1; };
      for (const r of historyArr) {
        inc(a.p, r.personaId); inc(a.m, r.methodId); inc(a.i, r.intention);
        inc(a.s, r.soundscape); inc(a.z, r.vizOverride || 'auto'); inc(a.ln, r.length); inc(a.am, r.affirmationMode || 'woven'); inc(a.vc, r.voiceName || 'default');
        const d = new Date(r.date); a.hr[d.getHours()]++; a.dw[d.getDay()]++;
        if (r.preMood != null) { a.mood.preSum += r.preMood; a.mood.n++; }
        if (r.postMood != null) { a.mood.postSum += r.postMood; a.mood.deltaSum += (r.postMood - (r.preMood ?? 5)); a.mood.postN = (a.mood.postN || 0) + 1; }
        a.comp.total++;
        if (r.completed) a.comp.finished++;
        else a.comp.emergency++; // history entries without completed=true were emergency-ended
        if (r.durationSec > 0) { a.dur.sum += r.durationSec; a.dur.n++; }
        a.cfg.rateSum += (r.speechRate || 0.65); a.cfg.pitchSum += (r.voicePitch || 0.85);
        a.cfg.volSum += (r.voiceVolume ?? 1.0); a.cfg.droneSum += (r.droneVolume ?? 0.35); a.cfg.n++;
        const metrics = r.metrics || {};
        a.shape.phaseSum += metrics.phaseCount || (Array.isArray(r.phaseOrder) ? r.phaseOrder.length : 0);
        a.shape.workSum += r.workBlockCount || metrics.workBlocks || 0;
        a.shape.affirmSum += metrics.affirmBlocks || 0;
        a.shape.n++;
      }
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch(e) { console.error('Analytics rebuild failed:', e); }
  }

  /** Derive insights from analytics — top preferences, patterns */
  function deriveInsights(a) {
    const topKey = obj => Object.entries(obj).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]?.[0] || null;
    const topN = (obj, n) => Object.entries(obj).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, n).map(e => e[0]);
    const avgMood = a.mood.n > 0 ? (a.mood.preSum / a.mood.n).toFixed(1) : null;
    // avgPost and avgDelta use postN (count of sessions where post-mood was filled).
    // a.mood.n tracks pre-mood fills, which can be much higher — using it here would under-estimate.
    const postN = a.mood.postN || 0;
    const avgPost = postN > 0 && a.mood.postSum > 0 ? (a.mood.postSum / postN).toFixed(1) : null;
    const avgDelta = postN > 0 ? (a.mood.deltaSum / postN).toFixed(1) : null;
    const avgDur = a.dur.n > 0 ? Math.round(a.dur.sum / a.dur.n) : 0;
    const peakHour = a.hr.indexOf(Math.max(...a.hr));
    const peakDay = a.dw.indexOf(Math.max(...a.dw));
    const dayNames = ['Sunday','Monday','Tuesday','Wednesday','Thursday','Friday','Saturday'];
    return {
      favPersona: topKey(a.p), favMethod: topKey(a.m), favSoundscape: topKey(a.s),
      favIntention: topKey(a.i), favViz: topKey(a.z), favLength: topKey(a.ln),
      topPersonas: topN(a.p, 3), topMethods: topN(a.m, 3),
      avgPreMood: avgMood, avgPostMood: avgPost, avgImprovement: avgDelta,
      avgDurationSec: avgDur, completionRate: a.comp.total > 0 ? Math.round(a.comp.finished / a.comp.total * 100) : 0,
      peakHour, peakDayName: dayNames[peakDay] || '—',
      totalSessions: a.comp.total,
      avgSpeechRate: a.cfg.n > 0 ? (a.cfg.rateSum / a.cfg.n).toFixed(2) : null,
      avgPhaseCount: a.shape?.n > 0 ? (a.shape.phaseSum / a.shape.n).toFixed(1) : null,
      avgWorkBlocks: a.shape?.n > 0 ? (a.shape.workSum / a.shape.n).toFixed(1) : null,
      favAffirmationMode: topKey(a.am || {}),
      favVoice: topKey(a.vc || {}),
      featuresUsed: Object.entries(FEAT).filter(([,bit]) => a.feat & bit).map(([name]) => name.toLowerCase().replace('_',' ')),
    };
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // ADAPTIVE INTELLIGENCE SYSTEM — Phases 1–9
  // Observe → Infer → Adapt → Reinforce → Evolve
  // ====================================================================
  const ADAPTIVE_KEY = 'stillness_adaptive_v1';

  /** Default adaptive profile (~300 bytes in IDB) */
  function defaultAdaptive() {
    return {
      v: 1,
      // Phase 2 — hidden profile traits (0–1 normalized)
      traits: {
        compliance: 0.5,      // finishes sessions?
        sensitivity: 0.5,     // mood responds to sessions?
        stability: 0.5,       // consistent improvement?
        noveltySeeking: 0.5,  // explores vs repeats?
        depthTolerance: 0.5,  // handles long/deep?
        controlPref: 0.5,     // authoritative (1) vs gentle (0)
        sensoryAudio: 0.5,    // uses soundscapes?
        sensoryVisual: 0.5,   // uses visuals?
      },
      // Phase 3 — reward-weighted preferences { id: weight }
      w: { p: {}, m: {}, s: {}, ln: {} },
      // Phase 4 — AI memory summary (updated every 5 sessions)
      memorySummary: '',
      memorySessCount: 0,  // sessions since last summary
      // Phase 6 — difficulty ramp
      difficulty: 0.3,  // 0=gentle 1=deep
      // Phase 7 — equilibrium
      recoveryMode: false,
      // Timestamp
      ts: 0,
    };
  }

  async function getAdaptive() {
    try { const d = await idbGet(ADAPTIVE_KEY); if (d?.v === 1) return d; } catch {}
    return defaultAdaptive();
  }

  // ── Phase 1: Derived signals ──
  function deriveSignals(analytics, history) {
    const a = analytics, h = history || [];
    const clamp = (v, lo = 0, hi = 1) => Math.max(lo, Math.min(hi, v));
    const compRate = a.comp.total > 0 ? a.comp.finished / a.comp.total : 0.5;
    const postN = a.mood.postN || 0; // only sessions where user filled post-mood
    const avgDelta = postN > 0 ? a.mood.deltaSum / postN : 0;
    const emergRate = a.comp.total > 0 ? a.comp.emergency / a.comp.total : 0;
    // Mood variance from last 10 sessions
    const recent = h.filter(s => s.preMood != null && s.postMood != null).slice(0, 10);
    const deltas = recent.map(s => s.postMood - s.preMood);
    const deltaVar = deltas.length > 1 ? deltas.reduce((s, d) => s + Math.pow(d - avgDelta, 2), 0) / deltas.length : 1;
    // Entropy of method usage (variety)
    const mEntries = Object.values(a.m || {});
    const mTotal = mEntries.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) || 1;
    const mEntropy = -mEntries.reduce((s, v) => { const p = v / mTotal; return s + (p > 0 ? p * Math.log2(p) : 0); }, 0);
    const maxEntropy = Math.log2(Math.max(mEntries.length, 1)) || 1;
    // Average session length normalized (0=micro, 1=long)
    const lenMap = { micro: 0, quick: 0.2, short: 0.4, medium: 0.6, long: 0.85, extended: 1 };
    const lenEntries = Object.entries(a.ln || {});
    const lenTotal = lenEntries.reduce((s, [, v]) => s + v, 0) || 1;
    const avgLen = lenEntries.reduce((s, [k, v]) => s + (lenMap[k] ?? 0.5) * v, 0) / lenTotal;
    // Control preference — ratio of authoritarian persona usage
    // IDs must match BUILTIN_PERSONAS entries with category 'authoritarian'
    const authPersonas = ['commander','headmistress','interrogator','drill-instructor','dominatrix','surgeon'];
    const authCount = authPersonas.reduce((s, id) => s + (a.p[id] || 0), 0);
    const totalPersona = Object.values(a.p || {}).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) || 1;
    // Soundscape & visual usage rates
    const soundNone = (a.s?.none || 0) / (a.comp.total || 1);
    const vizAuto = (a.z?.auto || 0) / (a.comp.total || 1);
    return {
      completionRate: compRate,
      avgImprovement: clamp(avgDelta / 5 + 0.5),
      moodVariance: clamp(1 - deltaVar / 10),
      noveltyEntropy: clamp(mEntropy / maxEntropy),
      depthNorm: clamp(avgLen),
      controlRatio: clamp(authCount / totalPersona),
      emergencyRate: emergRate,
      audioUsage: clamp(1 - soundNone),
      visualUsage: clamp(1 - vizAuto),
    };
  }

  // ── Phase 2: Update hidden profile traits ──
  function updateTraits(traits, sig) {
    const lerp = (old, target, rate = 0.15) => old + (target - old) * rate;
    return {
      compliance:     lerp(traits.compliance, sig.completionRate),
      sensitivity:    lerp(traits.sensitivity, sig.avgImprovement),
      stability:      lerp(traits.stability, sig.moodVariance),
      noveltySeeking: lerp(traits.noveltySeeking, sig.noveltyEntropy),
      depthTolerance: lerp(traits.depthTolerance, sig.depthNorm),
