      controlPref:    lerp(traits.controlPref, sig.controlRatio),
      sensoryAudio:   lerp(traits.sensoryAudio, sig.audioUsage),
      sensoryVisual:  lerp(traits.sensoryVisual, sig.visualUsage),
    };
  }

  // ── Phase 3: Reward function + weight update ──
  function computeReward(record, wasEmergency) {
    const delta = (record.postMood ?? 5) - (record.preMood ?? 5);
    return delta + (record.completed ? 1 : -1) - (wasEmergency ? 2 : 0);
  }

  function updateWeights(w, record, reward) {
    const decay = 0.98;
    const apply = (map, key) => { if (!key) return; for (const k in map) map[k] *= decay; map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + reward; };
    apply(w.p, record.personaId);
    apply(w.m, record.methodId);
    apply(w.s, record.soundscape);
    apply(w.ln, record.length);
  }

  function getPreferred(weightMap, n = 3) {
    return Object.entries(weightMap).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, n).map(e => e[0]);
  }

  // ── Phase 6: Difficulty ramp ──
  function computeDifficulty(sig, currentDiff) {
    const target = sig.completionRate * 0.4 + sig.avgImprovement * 0.3 + sig.depthNorm * 0.3;
    return currentDiff + (target - currentDiff) * 0.1; // very slow ramp
  }

  // ── Phase 7: Equilibrium ──
  function checkEquilibrium(sig, adaptive) {
    if (sig.emergencyRate > 0.3 || sig.completionRate < 0.5 || sig.avgImprovement < 0.3) {
      return { recoveryMode: true, difficulty: Math.max(0.1, adaptive.difficulty - 0.15) };
    }
    return { recoveryMode: false, difficulty: adaptive.difficulty };
  }

  // ── Phase 5 & 8: Recommendation engine ──
  function getRecommendation(adaptive, analytics) {
    const topW = (map) => Object.entries(map).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]?.[0] || null;
    const rec = {
      persona: topW(adaptive.w.p),
      method: topW(adaptive.w.m),
      soundscape: topW(adaptive.w.s),
      length: topW(adaptive.w.ln),
    };
    // Difficulty-based length override
    if (adaptive.recoveryMode) rec.length = 'short';
    else if (adaptive.difficulty > 0.7) rec.length = rec.length || 'long';
    else if (adaptive.difficulty < 0.3) rec.length = rec.length || 'short';
    return rec;
  }

  // ── Phase 5: Prompt shaping block ──
  function getAdaptivePromptBlock(adaptive) {
    if (!adaptive || adaptive.ts === 0) return '';
    const t = adaptive.traits;
    const lines = ['\n[ADAPTIVE CONTEXT — do not reveal these values]'];
    if (t.compliance < 0.4) lines.push('- User often stops early. Keep sessions engaging and check in more.');
    if (t.sensitivity > 0.7) lines.push('- User responds strongly to suggestions. Use moderate intensity.');
    else if (t.sensitivity < 0.3) lines.push('- User needs stronger, more direct suggestions to feel effects.');
    if (t.stability < 0.4) lines.push('- Mood responses vary widely. Prioritize grounding and safety.');
    if (t.noveltySeeking > 0.7) lines.push('- User enjoys variety. Introduce fresh metaphors and techniques.');
    else if (t.noveltySeeking < 0.3) lines.push('- User prefers familiar patterns. Reinforce known-effective approaches.');
    if (t.depthTolerance > 0.7) lines.push('- User tolerates deep trance. Allow longer pauses and deeper language.');
    else if (t.depthTolerance < 0.3) lines.push('- Keep trance light. Shorter pauses, more conversational tone.');
    if (t.controlPref > 0.65) lines.push('- User prefers authoritative direction.');
    else if (t.controlPref < 0.35) lines.push('- User prefers gentle, permissive approach.');
    if (adaptive.recoveryMode) lines.push('- RECOVERY MODE: Simplify. Shorter pauses. More grounding. Extra gentleness.');
    const diffLabel = adaptive.difficulty > 0.65 ? 'advanced' : adaptive.difficulty > 0.35 ? 'intermediate' : 'beginner';
    lines.push(`- Difficulty level: ${diffLabel} (${adaptive.difficulty.toFixed(2)})`);
    if (adaptive.memorySummary) lines.push(`- Memory: ${adaptive.memorySummary}`);
    return lines.length > 1 ? lines.join('\n') : '';
  }

  // ── Phase 4: Periodic AI memory summary ──
  async function updateMemorySummary(adaptive, history) {
    if (!history.length || adaptive.memorySessCount < 5) return adaptive.memorySummary;
    const recent = history.slice(0, 8).map(s => `${s.guide}/${s.method} ${s.length} mood:${s.preMood ?? '?'}→${s.postMood ?? '?'} ${s.completed ? '✓' : '✗'}`).join('; ');
    try {
      // route through hardened aiGenerate wrapper (consistent HTTP/empty-text handling).
      const data = await aiGenerate(
        `You are analyzing a hypnosis user's recent sessions. Write a 1-2 sentence behavioral summary noting: what works best, what to avoid, emotional trajectory. Be concise and clinical.\n\nRecent sessions: ${recent}\n\nPrevious summary: ${adaptive.memorySummary || 'none'}\n\nNew summary:`,
        { stopSequences: ['\n\n'] }
      );
      if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') return adaptive.memorySummary;
      const text = (data.generatedText || '').trim().slice(0, 250);
      return text || adaptive.memorySummary;
    } catch { return adaptive.memorySummary; }
  }

  // Master update — called after each completed session
  async function updateAdaptiveProfile(sessionRecord, wasEmergency) {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('updateAdaptiveProfile skipped — Smart Director off');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
      const analytics = await getAnalytics();
      const history = ((await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || []).map(normalizeHistoryEntry);
      // Phase 1: signals
      const sig = deriveSignals(analytics, history);
      // Phase 2: update traits
      adaptive.traits = updateTraits(adaptive.traits, sig);
      // Phase 3: reward + weights
      const reward = computeReward(sessionRecord, wasEmergency);
      updateWeights(adaptive.w, sessionRecord, reward);
      // Phase 6: difficulty
      adaptive.difficulty = computeDifficulty(sig, adaptive.difficulty);
      // Phase 7: equilibrium
      const eq = checkEquilibrium(sig, adaptive);
      adaptive.recoveryMode = eq.recoveryMode;
      adaptive.difficulty = eq.difficulty;
      // Phase 4: memory (every 5 sessions)
      adaptive.memorySessCount = (adaptive.memorySessCount || 0) + 1;
      if (adaptive.memorySessCount >= 5) {
        adaptive.memorySummary = await updateMemorySummary(adaptive, history);
        adaptive.memorySessCount = 0;
      }
      adaptive.ts = Date.now();
      await idbSet(ADAPTIVE_KEY, adaptive);
    } catch(e) { console.error('Adaptive update failed:', e); }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // STEP MANAGEMENT
  // ====================================================================
  function validateStep(n) {
    if (n === 1) return !!getPersona();
    if (n === 2) return !!getMethod();
    if (n === 3) {
      const skipCraft = ['trance', 'sleep'].includes(state.intentionType);
      return !!state.craftedSuggestion || skipCraft;
    }
    if (n === 4) return true;
    if (n === 5) return true;
    if (n === 6) return !!state.fullScript;
    return true;
  }

  function clearGeneratedScriptUi() {
    state.fullScript = null;
    state.parsedScript = null;
    state.generatedPhaseOrder = [];
    state.scriptSections = [];
    if (typeof _scriptEditedSinceGen !== 'undefined') _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
    if ($('scriptText')) $('scriptText').value = '';
    if ($('scriptStats')) $('scriptStats').innerHTML = '';
    if ($('scriptPreview')) $('scriptPreview').classList.remove('visible');
    if ($('phaseEditorPanel')) $('phaseEditorPanel').style.display = 'none';
    if ($('genProgress')) $('genProgress').style.display = 'none';
    if ($('scriptBuildProgress')) $('scriptBuildProgress').style.display = 'none';
    if ($('generateScriptBtn')) showEl('generateScriptBtn', true);
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // EXTERNAL AI ROUTER — wraps Perchance AI, Anthropic, OpenAI
  // ====================================================================
  async function aiGenerate(instruction, opts = {}) {
    const provider = state.extAiProvider || 'perchance';
    // Helper — ensure a returned object always has a usable shape and
    // surfaces empty/failed generations as errors rather than silent empty
    // strings that propagate into scripts.
    const asResult = (text, stopReason, note) => {
      const t = (text || '').trim();
      if (!t || stopReason === 'error') return { generatedText: '', stopReason: 'error', _note: note || 'empty or errored' };
      return { generatedText: t, stopReason: stopReason || 'stop' };
    };
    if (provider === 'anthropic' && state._extAiKey) {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-api-key': state._extAiKey, 'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01', 'anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access': 'true' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ model: opts.model || 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: opts.maxTokens || 2048, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: instruction }] }),
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
          console.warn(`Anthropic API HTTP ${res.status}, falling back to Perchance`);
          // fall through to Perchance below
        } else {
          const data = await res.json();
          if (data.error) {
            console.warn('Anthropic API returned error:', data.error);
          } else {
            const text = data.content?.[0]?.text || '';
            const stop = data.stop_reason === 'end_turn' || data.stop_reason === 'stop_sequence' ? 'stop'
              : data.stop_reason === 'max_tokens' ? 'max_tokens' : 'stop';
            const result = asResult(text, stop, 'anthropic empty');
            if (result.stopReason !== 'error') return result;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Anthropic API failed, falling back to Perchance:', e); }
    }
    if (provider === 'openai' && state._extAiKey) {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${state._extAiKey}` },
          body: JSON.stringify({ model: opts.model || 'gpt-4o-mini', messages: [{ role: 'user', content: instruction }], max_tokens: opts.maxTokens || 2048 }),
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
          console.warn(`OpenAI API HTTP ${res.status}, falling back to Perchance`);
        } else {
          const data = await res.json();
          if (data.error) {
            console.warn('OpenAI API returned error:', data.error);
          } else {
            const text = data.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || '';
            const finish = data.choices?.[0]?.finish_reason;
            const stop = finish === 'stop' ? 'stop' : finish === 'length' ? 'max_tokens' : 'stop';
            const result = asResult(text, stop, 'openai empty');
            if (result.stopReason !== 'error') return result;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) { console.warn('OpenAI API failed, falling back to Perchance:', e); }
    }
    // Default: Perchance AI
    if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.aiTextPlugin) {
      try {
        const data = await root.aiTextPlugin({ instruction, stopSequences: opts.stopSequences || ['\n\n\n'], hideStartWith: true, ...opts });
        if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') return asResult('', 'error', 'perchance ai error');
        return asResult(data.generatedText, data.stopReason, 'perchance empty');
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Perchance AI threw:', e); return asResult('', 'error', 'perchance threw'); }
    }
    return asResult('', 'error', 'no provider available');
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // 3-TIER HIERARCHICAL MEMORY SYSTEM
  // ====================================================================
  const MEMORY_KEY = 'stillness_memory_v1';
  async function getMemory() {
    const m = await idbGet(MEMORY_KEY);
    return m || { sessionDigests: [], rollingWindow: '', longTermProfile: '', lastRollingAt: 0, lastProfileAt: 0 };
  }
  async function saveMemory(m) { await idbSet(MEMORY_KEY, m); }

  // Tier 1: Per-session script digest (called in finishSession)
  async function digestSessionScript(script, record) {
    if (!script || script.length < 100) return null;
    const truncated = script.slice(0, 2000);
    const instruction = `Summarize this hypnosis session script in 2-3 sentences. Note: key imagery/metaphors, specific suggestions delivered, induction method, emotional tone. Be clinical and specific — this feeds a personalization system.

TIP: Ensure summaries use full, natural, readable sentences with correct grammar.
NOTE: Don't append commentary or word counts. Just do the task and end your response.

Script excerpt:
${truncated}

Session: guide=${record.guide || '?'}, method=${record.method || '?'}, mood Δ=${(record.postMood ?? 5) - (record.preMood ?? 5)}, depth=${record.depth ?? '?'}/10

Summary:`;
    try {
      const data = await aiGenerate(instruction, { stopSequences: ['\n\n', '\n---'] });
      if (data.stopReason === 'error') return null;
      return (data.generatedText || '').trim().replace(/\n+/g, ' ').replace(/---$/, '').trim().slice(0, 300);
    } catch { return null; }
  }

  // Tier 2: Rolling window summary (every 5 sessions)
  async function updateRollingMemory(memory) {
    if (memory.sessionDigests.length - memory.lastRollingAt < 5) return;
    const recent = memory.sessionDigests.slice(0, 10).map(d => d.digest).filter(Boolean).join('\n- ');
    if (!recent) return;
    const instruction = `You are analyzing a hypnosis user's recent session summaries. Write a 3-4 sentence behavioral analysis: what imagery/methods produce the best results, what to emphasize in future sessions, what to avoid. Previous analysis: "${memory.rollingWindow || 'none'}"

Recent sessions:
- ${recent}

Updated analysis (full, natural, readable sentences with correct grammar):`;
    try {
      const data = await aiGenerate(instruction, { stopSequences: ['\n\n'] });
      if (data.stopReason !== 'error') {
        memory.rollingWindow = (data.generatedText || '').trim().replace(/\n+/g, ' ').trim().slice(0, 500);
        memory.lastRollingAt = memory.sessionDigests.length;
      }
    } catch {}
  }

  // Tier 3: Long-term profile (every 15 sessions)
  async function updateLongTermProfile(memory) {
    if (memory.sessionDigests.length - memory.lastProfileAt < 15) return;
    const profile = getProfileContext();
    const instruction = `Write a ~150 word practitioner profile for a hypnosis user based on their data. Note: primary use case, best methods/guides, imagery preferences, depth patterns, session length preference, key insights about what works.

Profile data: ${profile}
Rolling analysis: ${memory.rollingWindow || 'none'}
Total sessions: ${memory.sessionDigests.length}

Practitioner profile (full, natural sentences):`;
    try {
      const data = await aiGenerate(instruction, { stopSequences: ['\n\n\n'] });
      if (data.stopReason !== 'error') {
        memory.longTermProfile = (data.generatedText || '').trim().slice(0, 600);
        memory.lastProfileAt = memory.sessionDigests.length;
      }
    } catch {}
  }

  // Master memory update — called after each completed session
  async function updateSessionMemory(script, record) {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('updateSessionMemory skipped — Smart Director off');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const memory = await getMemory();
      const digest = await digestSessionScript(script, record);
      if (digest) {
        const entry = { sessionId: record.date, date: record.date, digest, depth: record.depth, moodDelta: (record.postMood ?? 5) - (record.preMood ?? 5) };
        memory.sessionDigests.unshift(entry);
        while (memory.sessionDigests.length > 30) memory.sessionDigests.pop();
        // also persist an embedding vector so future sessions can
        // retrieve semantically relevant digests (not just recent ones).
        // Guarded — silent no-op if embedTexts isn't available in this browser.
        embedAndStoreDigest(entry.sessionId, digest).catch(() => {});
      }
      await updateRollingMemory(memory);
      await updateLongTermProfile(memory);
      await saveMemory(memory);
    } catch (e) { console.error('Memory update failed:', e); }
  }

  function resetWizardForNewSession(opts = {}) {
    const preserveSelections = opts.preserveSelections !== false;
    state.currentStep = 1;
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: false, 2: false, 3: false, 4: false, 5: false, 6: false };
    state._skippedToScript = false;
    state.abortFlag = false;
    state.paused = false;
    state.craftedSuggestion = null;
    // Reset pre-session check-in so prior session's values don't leak forward
    state._preMood = 5;
    state._preTension = 5;
    state._preEnergy = 5;
    document.querySelectorAll('.mood-emoji.selected').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
    const tEl = $('preTensionSlider'); if (tEl) tEl.value = 5;
    const tVal = $('preTensionVal'); if (tVal) tVal.textContent = '5';
    const eEl = $('preEnergySlider'); if (eEl) eEl.value = 5;
    const eVal = $('preEnergyVal'); if (eVal) eVal.textContent = '5';
    if (!preserveSelections) {
      state.selectedPersonaId = 'driver';
      state.selectedMethodId = 'highway';
      state.intentionType = 'trigger';
      state.length = 'medium';
      $('intentionInput').value = '';
      // Apply adaptive recommendations if available
      applyAdaptiveRecommendations();
    }
    clearGeneratedScriptUi();
    switchScreen('setup-wizard');
    goToStep(1);
    updateStepUI();
  }

  async function applyAdaptiveRecommendations() {
    try {
      const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
      const analytics = await getAnalytics();
      // Need at least 3 completed sessions for recommendations to be meaningful.
      // (Previously compared adaptive.ts — a Date.now() timestamp — against the literal 3,
      // which was always false after any session.)
      if (!adaptive || !analytics || (analytics.comp?.total || 0) < 3) return;
      const rec = getRecommendation(adaptive, analytics);
      if (rec.persona && state.personas.find(p => p.id === rec.persona)) state.selectedPersonaId = rec.persona;
      if (rec.method && METHODS.find(m => m.id === rec.method)) state.selectedMethodId = rec.method;
      if (rec.length) { state.length = rec.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = rec.length; }
      if (rec.soundscape) { state.soundscape = rec.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = rec.soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = rec.soundscape; }
      renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
    } catch(e) { console.debug('Adaptive recommendations skipped:', e); }
  }

  function goToStep(n) {
    if (n < 1 || n > TOTAL_STEPS) return;
    // Forward direction: validate current step
    if (n > state.currentStep) {
      for (let i = state.currentStep; i < n; i++) {
        if (!validateStep(i)) { return; }
        state.stepsCompleted[i] = true;
      }
    }
    // Going backward from a skip clears the skipped state
    if (n < state.currentStep && state._skippedToScript) {
      state._skippedToScript = false;
    }
    state.currentStep = n;
    // Stop all previews when leaving the Configure step
    if (typeof _stopAllPreviews === 'function') _stopAllPreviews();
    updateStepUI();
    if (n === 5) { renderConfigSummary(); }
    if (n === 6) { refreshSummary(); showEl('generateScriptBtn', true); }
    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

    // Accessibility: announce step change and move focus
    const stepNames = { 1: 'Choose Your Guide', 2: 'Choose Your Method', 3: 'Set Your Intention', 4: 'Add Your Own Affirmations', 5: 'Configure the Session', 6: 'Generate Your Session' };
    const announce = $('ariaStepAnnounce');
    if (announce) announce.textContent = `Step ${n} of ${TOTAL_STEPS}: ${stepNames[n] || ''}`;
    // Move focus to step heading
    const heading = document.querySelector(`.step-content[data-step="${n}"] .step-title`);
    if (heading) { heading.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); heading.focus(); }
  }

  function updateStepUI() {
    // Content
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-content').forEach(el => {
      el.classList.toggle('active', parseInt(el.dataset.step) === state.currentStep);
    });
    // Stepper circles
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-item').forEach(el => {
      const n = parseInt(el.dataset.step);
      const isSkipped = state._skippedToScript && n < state.currentStep && !state.stepsCompleted[n];
      el.classList.toggle('current', n === state.currentStep);
      el.classList.toggle('completed', n < state.currentStep && !isSkipped);
      el.classList.toggle('skipped', isSkipped);
      el.classList.toggle('clickable', n < state.currentStep && !isSkipped);
    });
    // Step values under circles — show "Skipped" for bypassed steps
    if (state._skippedToScript) {
      for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
        const el = $('stepValue' + i);
        if (el && !state.stepsCompleted[i]) el.textContent = 'skipped';
      }
    } else {
      $('stepValue1').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[1] ? getPersona().name : '';
      $('stepValue2').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[2] ? getMethod().name : '';
      let s3 = '';
      if (state.stepsCompleted[3]) {
        if (state.craftedSuggestion) s3 = 'crafted ✓';
        else if (state.intentionType === 'trance') s3 = 'pure trance';
      }
      $('stepValue3').textContent = s3;
      $('stepValue4').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[4] ? (($('userAffirmations')?.value || '').trim() ? 'custom ✓' : 'none') : '';
      $('stepValue5').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[5] ? state.length : '';
    }
    $('stepValue6').textContent = state.fullScript ? 'ready ✓' : '';
    // Nav
    $('btnBack').hidden = state.currentStep === 1;
    $('btnNext').hidden = state.currentStep === TOTAL_STEPS;
    $('btnNext').disabled = !validateStep(state.currentStep);
    const backLabels = {
      2: '← guide',
      3: '← method',
      4: '← intention',
      5: '← affirmations',
      6: state._skippedToScript ? '← pasted script setup' : '← session settings'
    };
    const nextLabels = {
      1: 'choose a method →',
      2: 'set your intention →',
      3: 'add affirmations →',
      4: 'choose session settings →',
      5: 'review & generate script →'
    };
    $('btnBack').textContent = backLabels[state.currentStep] || '← back';
    $('btnNext').textContent = nextLabels[state.currentStep] || 'next →';
    // Skip button — only visible on step 1
    const skipBtn = $('btnSkipToScript');
    if (skipBtn) skipBtn.hidden = state.currentStep !== 1;
  }

  function refreshSummary() {
    $('summaryGuide').textContent = getPersona().name;
    $('summaryMethod').textContent = getMethod().name;
    $('summaryLength').textContent = `${state.length.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + state.length.slice(1)} · ${getWorkBlockCount()} work block${getWorkBlockCount() === 1 ? '' : 's'}`;
    const rawIntent = $('intentionInput').value.trim();
    const intentFallback = state.intentionType === 'sleep' ? '(sleep induction)'
      : state.intentionType === 'trance' ? '(pure trance)'
      : '(no theme)';
    const intent = rawIntent || intentFallback;
    const affCount = (($('userAffirmations')?.value || '').split(/\n+/).map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)).length;
    if ($('summaryAffirmations')) $('summaryAffirmations').textContent = affCount ? `${affCount} custom · ${($('affirmationMode')?.value || 'woven')}` : 'none';
    $('summaryIntention').textContent = intent.length > 60 ? intent.substring(0, 57) + '...' : intent;
    updateBriefPreview();
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // RENDERING
  // ====================================================================
  function renderPersonaGrid() {
    const grid = $('personaGrid');
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    const filtered = state.personaFilter === 'all' ? state.personas : state.personas.filter(p => p.category === state.personaFilter);
    filtered.forEach(p => {
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = `card category-${p.category || 'contemplative'}` + (p.id === state.selectedPersonaId ? ' selected' : '') + (p.isCustom ? ' is-custom' : '');
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="card-name">${escapeHtml(p.name)}</div><div class="card-tagline">${escapeHtml(p.tagline)}</div>${p.isCustom ? `<div class="card-actions"><button class="card-action-btn" data-action="edit">edit</button><button class="card-action-btn" data-action="delete">×</button></div>` : ''}`;
      card.addEventListener('click', e => {
        if (e.target.dataset.action === 'edit') { e.stopPropagation(); openPersonaEditor(p.id); return; }
        if (e.target.dataset.action === 'delete') { e.stopPropagation(); deletePersona(p.id); return; }
        state.selectedPersonaId = p.id;
        saveUserSettings();
        renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); hideScript(); updateStepUI();
      });
      grid.appendChild(card);
    });
    const addCard = document.createElement('div');
    addCard.className = 'card add-new';
    addCard.innerHTML = '<span>+ create custom</span>';
    addCard.addEventListener('click', () => openPersonaEditor(null));
    grid.appendChild(addCard);
  }
  function renderPersonaDetail() {
    const p = getPersona();
    const el = $('personaDetail');
    if (!p) { el.innerHTML = ''; return; }
    el.innerHTML = `<div class="detail-title">${escapeHtml(p.name)}</div><div>${escapeHtml(p.systemPrompt)}</div>`;
  }
  function renderMethodGrid() {
    const grid = $('methodGrid');
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    const filtered = state.methodFilter === 'all' ? METHODS : METHODS.filter(m => m.category === state.methodFilter);
    filtered.forEach(m => {
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = `card category-${m.category}` + (m.id === state.selectedMethodId ? ' selected' : '');
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="card-name">${escapeHtml(m.name)}${m.recommended ? `<span class="card-badge">recommended</span>` : ''}</div><div class="card-tagline">${escapeHtml(m.tagline)}</div><div class="card-tags">${m.tags.map(t => `<span class="card-tag">${escapeHtml(t)}</span>`).join('')}</div>`;
      card.addEventListener('click', () => {
        state.selectedMethodId = m.id;
        saveUserSettings();
        // Update soundscape default when method changes — but only if the user
        // hasn't explicitly customized it. Otherwise switching methods would silently
        // overwrite their chosen soundscape.
        if (!state._soundscapeOverridden) {
          state.soundscape = m.drone ? 'drone' : 'none';
          state.droneEnabled = m.drone;
          const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect');
          if (ssSelect) ssSelect.value = state.soundscape;
        }
        renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail(); hideScript(); updateStepUI();
      });
      grid.appendChild(card);
    });
  }
  function renderMethodDetail() {
    const m = getMethod();
    const el = $('methodDetail');
    if (!m) { el.innerHTML = ''; return; }
    el.innerHTML = `<div class="detail-title">${escapeHtml(m.name)}</div><div>${escapeHtml(m.detail)}</div>`;
  }
  function updateIntentionHint() {
    const type = $('intentionType').value;
    state.intentionType = type;
    const typeData = INTENTION_TYPES[type];
    $('intentionTypeHint').textContent = typeData ? typeData.hint : '';
    hideCrafted();

    // Types that skip crafting — hide the craft button and intention input
    const skipCraft = ['trance', 'sleep'].includes(type);
    const craftBtn = $('craftBtn');
    const intentionInput = $('intentionInput');
    const intentionLabel = intentionInput?.previousElementSibling;

    if (skipCraft) {
      if (craftBtn) craftBtn.style.display = 'none';
      if (craftBtn?.nextElementSibling) craftBtn.nextElementSibling.style.display = 'none'; // sublabel
      if (intentionInput) intentionInput.style.display = 'none';
      if (intentionLabel) intentionLabel.style.display = 'none';
      showEl('affirmationGroup', false);
    } else {
      if (craftBtn) craftBtn.style.display = '';
      if (craftBtn?.nextElementSibling) craftBtn.nextElementSibling.style.display = '';
      if (intentionInput) intentionInput.style.display = '';
      if (intentionLabel) intentionLabel.style.display = '';
      showEl('affirmationGroup', true);
    }

    updateStepUI();
  }
  function updateBriefPreview() {
    const p = getPersona(); const m = getMethod();
    const rawIntent = $('intentionInput').value.trim();
    const intentFallback = state.intentionType === 'sleep' ? '[sleep induction]'
      : state.intentionType === 'trance' ? '[pure trance]'
      : '[no theme]';
    const intention = rawIntent || intentFallback;
    const el = $('briefPreview');
    if (!p) { el.textContent = ''; return; }
    const action = m.category === 'demonstration' ? `demonstrate the <strong>${escapeHtml(m.name)}</strong> effect` : `use the <strong>${escapeHtml(m.name)}</strong> method`;
    el.innerHTML = `<strong>Hey ${escapeHtml(p.name)}</strong> — ${action} for a <strong>${escapeHtml(state.length)}</strong> session on the theme: <strong>"${escapeHtml(intention)}"</strong>${state.craftedSuggestion ? ' (with the crafted suggestion embedded)' : ''}. Write the full script.`;
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // CONFIGURE PANEL (Step 5) — dynamic context rendering
  // ====================================================================
  function renderConfigSummary() {
    const p = getPersona(), m = getMethod();
    const el = $('configSummary');
    if (!el || !p || !m) return;

    // Category badges
    const catColors = {
      contemplative: 'var(--accent)', showman: 'var(--accent-warm)',
      somatic: 'var(--accent-green)', authoritarian: '#d46a6a',
      therapeutic: '#8a9aaa', demonstration: 'var(--accent-purple)',
      rapid: '#d4a74a', advanced: '#e06888',
    };
    const pColor = catColors[p.category] || 'var(--text-dim)';
    const mColor = catColors[m.category] || 'var(--text-dim)';

    el.innerHTML = `
      <div style="display:flex;gap:12px;align-items:flex-start;flex-wrap:wrap;">
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:140px;">
          <div style="font-size:0.62rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;color:var(--text-faint);margin-bottom:4px;">guide</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.92rem;color:var(--text);font-weight:500;">${escapeHtml(p.name)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:${pColor};margin-top:2px;">${escapeHtml(p.category)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:140px;">
          <div style="font-size:0.62rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;color:var(--text-faint);margin-bottom:4px;">method</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.92rem;color:var(--text);font-weight:500;">${escapeHtml(m.name)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:${mColor};margin-top:2px;">${escapeHtml(m.category)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>`;

    // Auto-select recommended soundscape based on method
    const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect');
    const ssHint = $('soundscapeHint');
    if (ssSelect && ssHint) {
      // Recommend a soundscape based on method
      const recommendations = {
        highway: 'drone', spiral: 'drone', confusion: 'drone',
        'breath-478': 'none', progressive: 'ocean', ericksonian: 'rain',
        'heartbeat-sync': 'heartbeat', 'floating-body': 'binaural',
        'time-distortion': 'binaural', somnambulism: 'binaural',
        'double-induction': 'brown',
      };
      const rec = recommendations[m.id];
      // Only apply the recommendation if the user hasn't customized the soundscape.
      // Otherwise coming back to Configure would silently overwrite their choice.
      if (rec && ssSelect.value === state.soundscape && !state._soundscapeOverridden) {
        ssSelect.value = rec; state.soundscape = rec; state.droneEnabled = rec !== 'none';
      }
      if (m.drone) ssHint.textContent = `Recommended for ${escapeHtml(m.name)}. Procedurally generated — never loops.`;
      else ssHint.textContent = 'Optional. Procedurally generated — never loops. Use headphones for binaural.';
    }

    // Speed hint based on method category
    const speedHint = $('speechRateHint');
    if (speedHint) {
      if (m.category === 'rapid') speedHint.textContent = 'Rapid methods work well at normal or slightly faster speed.';
      else if (m.category === 'advanced') speedHint.textContent = 'Advanced methods benefit from a slow, deliberate pace.';
      else if (p.category === 'authoritarian') speedHint.textContent = 'Authoritarian guides often work well at a slightly faster pace.';
      else speedHint.textContent = 'Slower is more hypnotic.';
    }

    // Length recommendation hint
    const lengthHint = $('lengthHint');
    if (lengthHint) {
      if (m.category === 'rapid') lengthHint.textContent = 'Rapid methods are designed to be short. "Short" is usually plenty.';
      else if (m.category === 'advanced') lengthHint.textContent = 'Advanced methods benefit from longer sessions to build depth.';
      else if (state.intentionType === 'sleep') lengthHint.textContent = 'Sleep sessions work best at medium or long — give yourself time to drift off.';
      else lengthHint.textContent = '';
    }

    // Warnings for specific combinations
    const warnEl = $('configWarning');
    if (warnEl) {
      const warnings = [];
      if (m.category === 'advanced' && state.length === 'short') {
        warnings.push('Advanced methods may not reach full depth in a short session. Consider medium or long.');
      }
      if (p.category === 'authoritarian' && m.category === 'therapeutic' && m.pacing === 'permissive') {
        warnings.push('An authoritarian guide with a permissive method is an unusual combination. It can work, but the tones may clash.');
      }
      if (state.intentionType === 'sleep') {
        warnings.push('Sleep sessions skip wake and reintroduction. You will not be re-alerted — the session ends in silence.');
      }
      if (warnings.length) {
        warnEl.style.display = 'block';
        warnEl.innerHTML = '<strong>Note:</strong> ' + warnings.join(' · ');
      } else {
        warnEl.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // VOICES, AUDIO, VISUAL
  // ====================================================================
  function loadVoices() {
    const voices = speechSynthesis.getVoices();
    const select = $('voiceSelect');
    select.innerHTML = '';
    const scored = voices.filter(v => v.lang.startsWith('en')).map(v => {
      let s = 0;
      const n = v.name + ' ' + v.lang;
      if (/neural|natural|online/i.test(n)) s += 100;
      if (/enhanced|premium/i.test(n)) s += 90;
      if (/siri/i.test(n)) s += 85;
      if (/google/i.test(n) && !v.localService) s += 50;
      if (/male/i.test(n) && !/female/i.test(n)) s += 10;
      if (/uk|british|gb/i.test(n)) s += 5;
      if (/daniel|oliver|arthur|james|aaron/i.test(n)) s += 4;
      if (/espeak|compact/i.test(n)) s -= 50;
      if (v.localService) s += 2;
      const tier = s >= 85 ? 'neural' : s >= 50 ? 'cloud' : s > 0 ? 'local' : 'basic';
      return { voice: v, score: s, tier };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);

    // Group by tier
    const tiers = { neural: '★ Neural / Premium', cloud: '● Cloud', local: 'Local', basic: 'Basic' };
    const groups = {};
    scored.forEach(item => {
      if (!groups[item.tier]) groups[item.tier] = [];
      groups[item.tier].push(item);
    });

    let first = true;
    for (const tier of ['neural', 'cloud', 'local', 'basic']) {
      if (!groups[tier] || groups[tier].length === 0) continue;
      const og = document.createElement('optgroup');
      og.label = tiers[tier];
      groups[tier].forEach(item => {
        const opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = item.voice.name;
        opt.textContent = item.voice.name + ' (' + item.voice.lang + ')';
        opt.dataset.tier = tier;
        opt.dataset.local = item.voice.localService ? '1' : '0';
        if (first) { opt.selected = true; first = false; }
        og.appendChild(opt);
      });
      select.appendChild(og);
    }
    applySavedVoiceSelection();
    updateVoiceInfo();
  }
  function applySavedVoiceSelection() {
    const select = $('voiceSelect');
    if (!select) return;
    if (state._savedVoiceName) {
      const opts = [...select.querySelectorAll('option')];
      const exact = opts.find(opt => opt.value === state._savedVoiceName);
      if (exact) select.value = state._savedVoiceName;
    }
  }

  // ── Voice Pack System — persona-matched voice recommendations ──
  const VOICE_PACKS = {
    contemplative: { names: ['Samantha', 'Karen', 'Moira', 'Fiona', 'Google UK English Female', 'Microsoft Hazel'], hints: ['Female', 'en-GB'], rate: 0.58, pitch: 0.8 },
    authoritarian: { names: ['Alex', 'Daniel', 'James', 'Google UK English Male', 'Microsoft George'], hints: ['Male', 'en-GB', 'en-US'], rate: 0.63, pitch: 0.75 },
    showman: { names: ['Tom', 'Rishi', 'Google US English', 'Microsoft Mark'], hints: ['Male', 'en-US'], rate: 0.68, pitch: 0.9 },
    somatic: { names: ['Samantha', 'Moira', 'Fiona', 'Google UK English Female'], hints: ['Female', 'en-GB'], rate: 0.55, pitch: 0.82 },
  };
  function getVoicePackFor(personaCategory) {
    return VOICE_PACKS[personaCategory] || VOICE_PACKS.contemplative;
  }
  function autoSelectVoiceForPersona() {
    if (state._savedVoiceName) return; // user manually chose — don't override
    const persona = getPersona();
    const pack = getVoicePackFor(persona.category);
    const voices = speechSynthesis.getVoices().filter(v => v.lang.startsWith('en'));
    for (const name of pack.names) {
      const match = voices.find(v => v.name.includes(name));
      if (match) { $('voiceSelect').value = match.name; state.speechRate = pack.rate; state.voicePitch = pack.pitch; break; }
    }
  }

  function updateVoiceInfo() {
    const select = $('voiceSelect');
    const info = $('voiceInfo');
    if (!info || !select.selectedOptions[0]) return;
    const opt = select.selectedOptions[0];
    const tier = opt.dataset.tier || 'local';
    const local = opt.dataset.local === '1';
    const labels = { neural: '★ Neural voice — highest quality', cloud: '● Cloud voice — good quality, slight latency', local: 'Local voice — instant, lower quality', basic: 'Basic voice — functional' };
    info.textContent = (labels[tier] || '') + (local ? ' · runs offline' : ' · requires internet');
  }
  if (typeof speechSynthesis !== 'undefined') { loadVoices(); speechSynthesis.onvoiceschanged = loadVoices; }
  const getSelectedVoice = () => { const name = $('voiceSelect').value; return speechSynthesis.getVoices().find(v => v.name === name) || null; };

  // ====================================================================
  // SOUNDSCAPE ENGINE — procedural ambient audio (replaces AudioDrone)
  // Recipes from ROADMAP: rain, ocean, fire, bowls, heartbeat, binaural,
  // white/pink/brown noise, plus the original engine drone.
  // ====================================================================
  class SoundscapeEngine {
    constructor() { this.ctx = null; this.master = null; this.compressor = null; this.nodes = []; this.running = false; this.type = 'drone'; this._duckGain = null; }

    async start(volume = 0.35, type = 'drone') {
      if (this.running) await this.stop();
      this.type = type;
      this.ctx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
      if (this.ctx.state === 'suspended') await this.ctx.resume();

      // Master chain: sceneGain → compressor → destination
      this.compressor = this.ctx.createDynamicsCompressor();
      this.compressor.threshold.value = -18; this.compressor.knee.value = 24;
      this.compressor.ratio.value = 3; this.compressor.attack.value = 0.01; this.compressor.release.value = 0.25;
      this.compressor.connect(this.ctx.destination);
      this._duckGain = this.ctx.createGain(); this._duckGain.gain.value = 1.0;
      this._duckGain.connect(this.compressor);
      this.master = this.ctx.createGain(); this.master.gain.value = 0;
      this.master.connect(this._duckGain);

      const c = this.ctx, m = this.master, ns = this.nodes;
      const mkNoise = (filterType, freq, q) => {
        const buf = c.createBuffer(1, 2 * c.sampleRate, c.sampleRate);
        const d = buf.getChannelData(0); let lo = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < d.length; i++) {
          const w = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
          if (filterType === 'brown') { d[i] = (lo + 0.02 * w) / 1.02; lo = d[i]; d[i] *= 3.5; }
          else d[i] = w;
        }
        const src = c.createBufferSource(); src.buffer = buf; src.loop = true;
        if (filterType !== 'white' && filterType !== 'brown') {
          const f = c.createBiquadFilter(); f.type = filterType; f.frequency.value = freq || 1000; if (q) f.Q.value = q;
          src.connect(f); ns.push(src, f); return f;
        }
        ns.push(src); return src;
      };
      const mkOsc = (freq, type = 'sine') => { const o = c.createOscillator(); o.type = type; o.frequency.value = freq; ns.push(o); return o; };
      const mkGain = (v) => { const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = v; ns.push(g); return g; };
      const connect = (...chain) => { for (let i = 0; i < chain.length - 1; i++) chain[i].connect(chain[i + 1]); };
      const startAll = () => ns.forEach(n => { try { n.start && n.start(); } catch(e) {} });

      if (type === 'drone') {
        const bass = mkOsc(70); const bg = mkGain(0.4); connect(bass, bg, m);
        const harm = mkOsc(141); const hg = mkGain(0.18); connect(harm, hg, m);
        const noise = mkNoise('brown'); const ng = mkGain(0.25); const nf = c.createBiquadFilter(); nf.type = 'lowpass'; nf.frequency.value = 280; ns.push(nf);
        connect(noise, nf, ng, m);
        const lfo = mkOsc(0.07); const lg = mkGain(0.08); connect(lfo, lg); lg.connect(bg.gain);
      } else if (type === 'rain') {
        const bed = mkNoise('bandpass', 1200, 0.8); const bg = mkGain(0.5); connect(bed, bg, m);
        const rumble = mkNoise('brown'); const rf = c.createBiquadFilter(); rf.type = 'lowpass'; rf.frequency.value = 200; ns.push(rf);
        const rg = mkGain(0.08); connect(rumble, rf, rg, m);
        // Droplet scheduler
        const droplet = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          const osc = c.createOscillator(); osc.frequency.value = 2000 + Math.random() * 4000;
          const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0; osc.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime; g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.15 + Math.random() * 0.1, t + 0.005);
          g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.02 + Math.random() * 0.015);
          osc.start(t); osc.stop(t + 0.04);
          setTimeout(droplet, 20 + Math.random() * 60);
        };
        setTimeout(droplet, 500);
      } else if (type === 'ocean') {
        const noise = mkNoise('bandpass', 650, 0.5); const ng = mkGain(0.45);
        const lfo = mkOsc(1 / 11); const lg = mkGain(0.35); connect(lfo, lg); lg.connect(ng.gain);
        connect(noise, ng, m);
        const foam = mkNoise('bandpass', 3000, 1); const fg = mkGain(0.06); connect(foam, fg, m);
      } else if (type === 'fire') {
        const bed = mkNoise('brown'); const bg = mkGain(0.12);
        const bf = c.createBiquadFilter(); bf.type = 'lowpass'; bf.frequency.value = 400; ns.push(bf);
        connect(bed, bf, bg, m);
        const crackle = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          const b = c.createBuffer(1, Math.floor(c.sampleRate * 0.008), c.sampleRate); const d = b.getChannelData(0);
          for (let i = 0; i < d.length; i++) d[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * (1 - i / d.length);
          const s = c.createBufferSource(); s.buffer = b;
          const f = c.createBiquadFilter(); f.type = 'bandpass'; f.frequency.value = 1500 + Math.random() * 3000; f.Q.value = 2;
          const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0.15 + Math.random() * 0.2;
          s.connect(f).connect(g).connect(m); s.start();
          setTimeout(crackle, 80 + Math.random() * 300);
        };
        setTimeout(crackle, 200);
      } else if (type === 'bowls') {
        const ratios = [1, 2.02, 3.07, 4.16, 5.38]; const decays = [10, 7, 5, 4, 3];
        const strike = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          const root = 180 + Math.random() * 60;
          ratios.forEach((r, i) => {
            const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = root * r;
            const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0.12 / (i + 1);
            o.connect(g).connect(m); const t = c.currentTime;
            g.gain.setValueAtTime(g.gain.value, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + decays[i]);
            o.start(t); o.stop(t + decays[i] + 0.1);
          });
          setTimeout(strike, 8000 + Math.random() * 12000);
        };
        strike();
      } else if (type === 'heartbeat') {
        const beat = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          [0, 0.14].forEach(delay => {
            const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 55;
            const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0;
            const f = c.createBiquadFilter(); f.type = 'lowpass'; f.frequency.value = 200;
            o.connect(f).connect(g).connect(m); const t = c.currentTime + delay;
            g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.5, t + 0.03);
            g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.25);
            o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.3);
          });
          setTimeout(beat, 1050 + Math.random() * 120);
        };
        beat();
      } else if (type === 'binaural') {
        const carrier = 200, beatHz = 6; // Theta range
        const oL = mkOsc(carrier - beatHz / 2); const oR = mkOsc(carrier + beatHz / 2);
        const gL = mkGain(0.3); const gR = mkGain(0.3);
        const merger = c.createChannelMerger(2); ns.push(merger);
        oL.connect(gL).connect(merger, 0, 0); oR.connect(gR).connect(merger, 0, 1);
        merger.connect(m);
      } else if (type === 'pink' || type === 'brown' || type === 'white') {
        const noise = mkNoise(type === 'pink' ? 'lowpass' : type, type === 'pink' ? 800 : undefined);
        const ng = mkGain(type === 'white' ? 0.15 : 0.35); connect(noise, ng, m);
      } else if (type === 'forest') {
        // Layered: breeze (filtered brown), bird chirps (scheduled sine pips)
        const breeze = mkNoise('lowpass', 500); const bg = mkGain(0.2); connect(breeze, bg, m);
        const chirp = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 2200 + Math.random() * 2000;
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime + Math.random() * 0.5;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.08, t + 0.02);
          g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.08 + Math.random() * 0.1);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.15);
          setTimeout(chirp, 1500 + Math.random() * 4000);
        };
        chirp(); setTimeout(chirp, 800);
      } else if (type === 'stream') {
        // Gentle water: filtered white noise + subtle babble modulation
        const water = mkNoise('bandpass', 1200, 0.5); const wg = mkGain(0.3); connect(water, wg, m);
        const lfo = mkOsc(0.3); const lg = mkGain(100); lfo.connect(lg);
        const wf = c.createBiquadFilter(); wf.type = 'bandpass'; wf.frequency.value = 1200; ns.push(wf);
        lg.connect(wf.frequency); water.connect(wf).connect(wg);
      } else if (type === 'wind') {
        // Gusting wind: brown noise with slow LFO on gain
        const wind = mkNoise('lowpass', 600); const wg = mkGain(0.35); connect(wind, wg, m);
        const lfo = mkOsc(0.08 + Math.random() * 0.04); const lg = mkGain(0.2);
        lfo.connect(lg); lg.connect(wg.gain);
      } else if (type === 'thunder') {
        // Deep rumble base + periodic thunder rolls
        const rumble = mkNoise('lowpass', 120); const rg = mkGain(0.3); connect(rumble, rg, m);
        const rain = mkNoise('highpass', 3000); const raing = mkGain(0.08); connect(rain, raing, m);
        const roll = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          // Inline a self-contained noise burst so we can explicitly start/stop it.
          // (mkNoise pushes its source into ns expecting startAll(), which has already run.)
          const buf = c.createBuffer(1, Math.max(1, Math.floor(c.sampleRate * 0.2)), c.sampleRate);
          const d = buf.getChannelData(0);
          for (let i = 0; i < d.length; i++) d[i] = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
          const src = c.createBufferSource(); src.buffer = buf; src.loop = true;
          const f = c.createBiquadFilter(); f.type = 'lowpass'; f.frequency.value = 80;
          const g = c.createGain();
          src.connect(f).connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          const dur = 3 + Math.random() * 2;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);
          g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.5, t + 0.3);
          g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + dur);
          try { src.start(t); src.stop(t + dur + 0.1); } catch {}
          setTimeout(roll, 8000 + Math.random() * 15000);
        };
        setTimeout(roll, 3000 + Math.random() * 5000);
      } else if (type === 'chimes') {
        // Random tuned sine pips with long decay
        const base = mkNoise('bandpass', 400, 0.3); const bg = mkGain(0.05); connect(base, bg, m);
        const chime = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const freqs = [523, 587, 659, 784, 880, 1047, 1175];
          const f = freqs[Math.floor(Math.random() * freqs.length)];
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.15, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 2 + Math.random() * 2);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 4);
          setTimeout(chime, 2000 + Math.random() * 5000);
        };
        chime(); setTimeout(chime, 1200);
      } else if (type === 'cave') {
        // Sparse drips with long reverb/echo
        const bg = mkNoise('bandpass', 120, 0.3); const bgg = mkGain(0.03); connect(bg, bgg, m);
        const drip = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 2000 + Math.random() * 2000; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.08, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.8 + Math.random());
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 2);
          setTimeout(drip, 3000 + Math.random() * 8000);
        };
        drip(); setTimeout(drip, 1500); setTimeout(drip, 4500);
      } else if (type === 'crickets') {
        // Chirping insects — filtered noise bursts at cricket-like rates
        const wind = mkNoise('lowpass', 300); const wg = mkGain(0.04); connect(wind, wg, m);
        const chirp = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 4000 + Math.random() * 2000; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime, dur = 0.04 + Math.random() * 0.02;
          const reps = 3 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 4);
          for (let i = 0; i < reps; i++) {
            g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.06, t + i * dur * 2); g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t + i * dur * 2 + dur);
          }
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + reps * dur * 2 + 0.1);
          setTimeout(chirp, 1500 + Math.random() * 4000);
        };
        chirp(); setTimeout(chirp, 800); setTimeout(chirp, 2200);
      } else if (type === 'temple') {
        // Deep bell strikes + sustained tonal drone
        const drone1 = c.createOscillator(); drone1.frequency.value = 110; drone1.type = 'sine';
        const drone2 = c.createOscillator(); drone2.frequency.value = 165; drone2.type = 'triangle';
        const dg1 = mkGain(0.12); const dg2 = mkGain(0.06);
        connect(drone1, dg1, m); connect(drone2, dg2, m);
        this.nodes.push(drone1, drone2);
        const bell = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const f = [220, 277, 330, 440][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.2, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 5 + Math.random() * 3);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 8);
          setTimeout(bell, 6000 + Math.random() * 10000);
        };
        bell(); setTimeout(bell, 3000);
      } else if (type === 'spaceship') {
        // Low engine hum + subtle sci-fi bleeps
        const eng1 = c.createOscillator(); eng1.frequency.value = 42; eng1.type = 'sawtooth';
        const eng2 = c.createOscillator(); eng2.frequency.value = 43.5; eng2.type = 'sawtooth';
        const lp = c.createBiquadFilter(); lp.type = 'lowpass'; lp.frequency.value = 120;
        const eg1 = mkGain(0.15); const eg2 = mkGain(0.12);
        eng1.connect(eg1).connect(lp).connect(m); eng2.connect(eg2).connect(lp);
        this.nodes.push(eng1, eng2);
        const bleep = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const f = [880, 1320, 1760, 2200][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.02, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.15);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.2);
          setTimeout(bleep, 4000 + Math.random() * 12000);
        };
        bleep(); setTimeout(bleep, 6000);
      } else if (type === 'underwater') {
        // Deep submerged ambience with bubble chirps
        const noise = mkNoise('brown'); const ng = mkGain(0.35);
        const lp = c.createBiquadFilter(); lp.type = 'lowpass'; lp.frequency.value = 400; ns.push(lp);
        connect(noise, ng, lp, m);
        const drone = mkOsc(55, 'sine'); const dg = mkGain(0.08); connect(drone, dg, m);
        const bubble = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const f = 1200 + Math.random() * 2000;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.015, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.08);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.1);
          setTimeout(bubble, 800 + Math.random() * 4000);
        };
        bubble(); setTimeout(bubble, 2000); setTimeout(bubble, 4500);
      } else if (type === 'clock') {
        // Grandfather clock — tick-tock + periodic chime
        const tick = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 800; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.06, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.03);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.05);
          setTimeout(tick, 1000);
        };
        tick();
        const roomNoise = mkNoise('brown'); const rg = mkGain(0.04);
        const rlp = c.createBiquadFilter(); rlp.type = 'lowpass'; rlp.frequency.value = 200; ns.push(rlp);
        connect(roomNoise, rg, rlp, m);
        const chime = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          [220, 330, 440].forEach((f, i) => {
            const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
            const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
            const t = c.currentTime + i * 0.3;
            g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.04, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 2);
            o.start(t); o.stop(t + 2.5);
          });
          setTimeout(chime, 90000 + Math.random() * 60000);
        };
        setTimeout(chime, 30000);
      } else if (type === 'train') {
        // Railway car — rhythmic clack + rumble
        const rumble = mkNoise('brown'); const rg = mkGain(0.3);
        const rlp = c.createBiquadFilter(); rlp.type = 'lowpass'; rlp.frequency.value = 180; ns.push(rlp);
        connect(rumble, rg, rlp, m);
        const clack = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = mkNoise('white'); const g = mkGain(0.08);
          const bp = c.createBiquadFilter(); bp.type = 'bandpass'; bp.frequency.value = 2000; bp.Q.value = 3; ns.push(bp);
          o.connect(g).connect(bp).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.08, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.06);
          try { o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.08); } catch {}
          setTimeout(clack, 450 + Math.random() * 100);
        };
        clack(); setTimeout(clack, 225);
      } else if (type === 'city') {
        // City night — distant traffic + ambient
        const traffic = mkNoise('brown'); const tg = mkGain(0.15);
        const tlp = c.createBiquadFilter(); tlp.type = 'lowpass'; tlp.frequency.value = 150; ns.push(tlp);
        connect(traffic, tg, tlp, m);
        const hum = mkOsc(60, 'sine'); const hg = mkGain(0.03); connect(hum, hg, m);
        const siren = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          o.frequency.setValueAtTime(600, t); o.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(800, t + 1);
          o.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(600, t + 2);
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.005, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.012, t + 0.5);
          g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 3);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 3.5);
          setTimeout(siren, 30000 + Math.random() * 60000);
        };
        setTimeout(siren, 15000 + Math.random() * 20000);
      }

      startAll();
      this.master.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(volume, this.ctx.currentTime + 4);
      this.running = true;
    }

    setVolume(v) { if (this.master && this.ctx) this.master.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(Math.max(0, v), this.ctx.currentTime + 0.5); }

    // Ducking: called from speakScript to lower ambience during narration
    duck() { if (this._duckGain && this.ctx) { this._duckGain.gain.cancelScheduledValues(this.ctx.currentTime); this._duckGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.15, this.ctx.currentTime + 0.25); } }
    unduck() { if (this._duckGain && this.ctx) { this._duckGain.gain.cancelScheduledValues(this.ctx.currentTime); this._duckGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(1.0, this.ctx.currentTime + 1.2); } }

    setPhaseFreq(phase) {
      if (this.type !== 'drone' || !this.ctx) return;
      const freqMap = { settling: 70, induction: 67, deepener: 63, work: 60, lightener: 66, wake: 72, reintroduction: 74, emergence: 72 };
      const target = freqMap[phase] || 70;
      if (this.nodes[0]?.frequency) this.nodes[0].frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(target, this.ctx.currentTime + 4);
      if (this.nodes[2]?.frequency) this.nodes[2].frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(target * 2.01, this.ctx.currentTime + 4);
    }

    async stop() {
      if (!this.running || !this.ctx) return;
      this.master.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, this.ctx.currentTime + 2);
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 2100));
      this.nodes.forEach(n => { try { n.stop?.(); n.disconnect?.(); } catch(e) {} });
      try { this.ctx.suspend(); } catch(e) {}
      this.ctx = null; this.master = null; this._duckGain = null; this.compressor = null; this.nodes = []; this.running = false;
    }
  }
  const drone = new SoundscapeEngine();

  // ====================================================================
  // BACKGROUND IMAGE ENGINE
  // ====================================================================
  // Max concurrent image generations. Perchance text-to-image-plugin handles up
  // to 4 parallel requests well; beyond that the provider starts queuing and it
  // just adds latency rather than throughput.
  const BG_MAX_PARALLEL = 4;

  // Orientation → resolution map. "default" delegates to the plugin default.
  const BG_RESOLUTIONS = {
    default: null,            // omit resolution → plugin picks
    square: '512x512',
    portrait: '512x768',
    landscape: '768x512',
  };

  // ====================================================================
  // BG TRANSITION REGISTRY — 12 effects, backported from Slideshow spinoff.
  // Adapted for <img> elements (not background-image divs) and for the
  // session-bg dim cap of 0.35 (so text stays readable over the images).
  //
  // Each entry: { label, run(oldEl, newEl, url, durSec) }
  //   • Sets newEl.src, arranges z-index, and starts the visual transition.
  //   • Safe to call concurrently — scheduleCleanup guards against clobber.
  //
  // Fade-through-black/white use the #bgFlash overlay inside #bgLayer,
  // which dims/lightens everything below it (images) without touching UI.
  // ====================================================================
  const BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY = 0.35;

  function _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl) {
    // Reset newEl state so the next transition starts clean
    newEl.style.transition = 'none';
    newEl.style.transform = '';
    newEl.style.filter = '';
    newEl.style.clipPath = '';
    newEl.style.opacity = '0';
    newEl.style.zIndex = '2';
    oldEl.style.zIndex = '1';
    void newEl.offsetWidth; // force reflow so subsequent transitions animate
  }
  function _bgScheduleCleanup(el, delayMs) {
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (el.style.zIndex !== '2') { // don't clobber a slide the next transition just promoted
        el.style.transition = 'none';
        el.style.transform = '';
        el.style.filter = '';
        el.style.clipPath = '';
        el.style.opacity = '0';
        el.classList.remove('active');
      }
    }, delayMs);
  }

  const BG_TRANSITIONS = {
    cut: {
      label: 'Cut',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
      },
    },
    crossfade: {
      label: 'Crossfade',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease`;
        oldEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
      },
    },
    fadeBlack: {
      label: 'Fade → black',
      async run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        const flash = $('bgFlash');
        if (flash) {
          flash.style.background = '#000';
          flash.style.transition = `opacity ${dur / 2}s ease`;
          flash.style.opacity = '1';
        }
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, dur * 500));
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 50));
        if (flash) flash.style.opacity = '0';
      },
    },
    fadeWhite: {
      label: 'Fade → white',
      async run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        const flash = $('bgFlash');
        if (flash) {
          flash.style.background = '#fff';
          flash.style.transition = `opacity ${dur / 2}s ease`;
          flash.style.opacity = '1';
        }
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, dur * 500));
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 50));
        if (flash) {
          flash.style.opacity = '0';
          setTimeout(() => { flash.style.background = '#000'; }, dur * 1000 + 300);
        }
      },
    },
    slideLeft: {
      label: 'Slide left',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.transform = 'translateX(100%)';
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `transform ${dur}s ease`;
        oldEl.style.transition = `transform ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.transform = 'translateX(0)';
        oldEl.style.transform = 'translateX(-100%)';
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        _bgScheduleCleanup(oldEl, dur * 1000 + 100);
      },
    },
    slideUp: {
      label: 'Slide up',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.transform = 'translateY(100%)';
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `transform ${dur}s ease`;
        oldEl.style.transition = `transform ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
        oldEl.style.transform = 'translateY(-100%)';
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        _bgScheduleCleanup(oldEl, dur * 1000 + 100);
      },
    },
    zoomIn: {
      label: 'Zoom in',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.transform = 'scale(0.3)';
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease, transform ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease`;
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
      },
    },
    zoomOut: {
      label: 'Zoom out',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.transform = 'scale(1.8)';
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease, transform ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease`;
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
      },
    },
    kenburns: {
      label: 'Ken Burns',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        // Crossfade in, then slow zoom over the full rotation interval
        const intervalSec = Number(state.bgRotationSec) || 45;
        const zooms = [
          { from: 'scale(1.0) translate(0, 0)',      to: 'scale(1.18) translate(-3%, -2%)' },
          { from: 'scale(1.18) translate(-3%, -2%)', to: 'scale(1.0) translate(0, 0)'      },
          { from: 'scale(1.0) translate(0, 0)',      to: 'scale(1.15) translate(3%, -2%)'  },
          { from: 'scale(1.12) translate(2%, 2%)',   to: 'scale(1.0) translate(0, 0)'      },
        ];
        const z = zooms[Math.floor(Math.random() * zooms.length)];
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.transform = z.from;
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease, transform ${intervalSec}s ease-in-out`;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.transform = z.to;
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease`;
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
      },
    },
    blur: {
      label: 'Blur',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.filter = 'blur(30px)';
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease, filter ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.filter = 'blur(0px)';
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        oldEl.style.transition = `opacity ${dur}s ease, filter ${dur}s ease`;
        oldEl.style.filter = 'blur(30px)';
        oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        oldEl.classList.remove('active');
        setTimeout(() => { oldEl.style.filter = ''; }, dur * 1000 + 150);
      },
    },
    iris: {
      label: 'Iris',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.clipPath = 'circle(0% at 50% 50%)';
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `clip-path ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.clipPath = 'circle(150% at 50% 50%)';
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        setTimeout(() => {
          oldEl.classList.remove('active');
          oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        }, dur * 1000 + 50);
      },
    },
    wipe: {
      label: 'Wipe',
      run(oldEl, newEl, url, dur) {
        _bgPrep(oldEl, newEl);
        newEl.src = url;
        newEl.style.opacity = String(BG_ACTIVE_OPACITY);
        newEl.style.clipPath = 'inset(0 100% 0 0)';
        void newEl.offsetWidth;
        newEl.style.transition = `clip-path ${dur}s ease`;
        newEl.style.clipPath = 'inset(0 0 0 0)';
        newEl.classList.add('active');
        setTimeout(() => {
          oldEl.classList.remove('active');
          oldEl.style.opacity = '0';
        }, dur * 1000 + 50);
      },
    },
  };

  // Default-enabled transition keys — calm ones that suit a hypnosis session.
  // User can toggle any subset via the checkbox grid in Step 5.
  const BG_DEFAULT_ENABLED = ['crossfade', 'fadeBlack', 'kenburns', 'blur'];

  const bgEngine = {
    source: 'none',
    prompt: '',
    queue: [],
    currentSlot: 0,
    interval: null,
    activeGenerations: 0,   // replaces boolean `generating` — counter for parallel tracking
    rotationSec: 45,
    _localObjectUrl: null,

    /** True if any generation is in flight. Preserved for UI handlers. */
    get generating() { return this.activeGenerations > 0; },

    /** Read current generation parameters from state. Pure — no DOM access.
     *  Centralized so generateOne() + anyone else stays in sync. */
    _currentParams() {
      const resolution = BG_RESOLUTIONS[state.bgOrientation || 'landscape'] || null;
      return {
        prompt: this.prompt || state.bgPrompt || 'abstract dark ethereal misty landscape, dreamlike, hypnotic, soft focus',
        negativePrompt: state.bgNegativePrompt || 'text, words, letters, bright, harsh, sharp, neon, ugly, deformed',
        resolution,
        guidanceScale: Number(state.bgGuidance) || 7,
        numInferenceSteps: Number(state.bgSteps) || 30,
        seed: -1,
      };
    },

    /** Generate exactly one image. Safe to call concurrently up to BG_MAX_PARALLEL;
     *  additional callers wait briefly for a free slot. Returns objectUrl or null. */
    async generateOne() {
      if (typeof root === 'undefined' || !root.textToImagePlugin) { console.warn('bgEngine: textToImagePlugin not available'); return null; }
      // Fairness spinlock — yield to the event loop until a slot frees up.
      while (this.activeGenerations >= BG_MAX_PARALLEL) {
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 150));
      }
      this.activeGenerations++;
      try {
        const params = this._currentParams();
        // resolution: null tells the plugin to use its default; omit the key entirely
        // rather than passing null to avoid confusing the plugin.
        // Steps is passed under both common names — Perchance's plugin accepts one
        // or the other depending on backend; extras are silently ignored.
        const call = {
          prompt: params.prompt,
          negativePrompt: params.negativePrompt,
          negative: params.negativePrompt,
          guidanceScale: params.guidanceScale,
          numInferenceSteps: params.numInferenceSteps,
          steps: params.numInferenceSteps,
          seed: params.seed,
        };
        if (params.resolution) call.resolution = params.resolution;
        const result = await root.textToImagePlugin(call);
        const dataUrl = result.dataUrl || String(result);
        if (dataUrl && dataUrl.startsWith('data:')) {
          await bgCacheStore(dataUrl, params.prompt);
          const blob = await fetch(dataUrl).then(r => r.blob());
          const objectUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
          this.queue.push(objectUrl);
          return objectUrl;
        }
        return null;
      } catch(e) { console.error('bgEngine generate:', e); return null; }
      finally { this.activeGenerations--; }
    },

    /** Fire N image generations in parallel, respecting BG_MAX_PARALLEL.
     *  Returns array of objectUrls (nulls removed) in completion order. */
    async generateBatch(count = BG_MAX_PARALLEL) {
      const n = Math.min(Math.max(1, count), BG_MAX_PARALLEL);
      const results = await Promise.all(
        Array.from({ length: n }, () => this.generateOne())
      );
      return results.filter(Boolean);
    },

    async pregenerate(count = 5) {
      // Load from Blob cache first
      const urls = await bgCacheGetAllUrls();
      if (urls.length > 0) this.queue = urls;
      // Kick off rotation now if we have cached images and source is 'ai'
      if (this.source === 'ai' && this.queue.length > 0) this.startRotation();
      // Generate new ones in parallel batches (up to BG_MAX_PARALLEL at a time)
      const needed = Math.max(0, count - this.queue.length);
      if (needed === 0) return;
      let produced = 0;
      while (produced < needed) {
        if (state.abortFlag) break;
        const batchSize = Math.min(BG_MAX_PARALLEL, needed - produced);
        await this.generateBatch(batchSize);
        produced += batchSize;
        // Kick off rotation as soon as the first batch lands
        if (this.source === 'ai' && this.queue.length > 0 && !this.interval) this.startRotation();
      }
    },

    startRotation() {
      if (this.source !== 'ai' || this.queue.length === 0) return;
      if (this.interval) return; // already rotating — don't stack intervals
      this._playOrder = this._buildPlayOrder();
      this._playCursor = 0;
      this.swap(this.queue[this._playOrder[0]]);
      const secs = Number(state.bgRotationSec) || this.rotationSec;
      this.interval = setInterval(() => {
        if (state.paused) return;
        this._playCursor = (this._playCursor + 1) % this._playOrder.length;
        // Rebuild order at each full wrap — picks up new queue items + re-shuffles
        if (this._playCursor === 0) this._playOrder = this._buildPlayOrder();
        const idx = this._playOrder[this._playCursor];
        if (idx != null && this.queue[idx]) this.swap(this.queue[idx]);
        // Silently generate more in background while under the cap
        if (!this.generating && this.queue.length < 20) this.generateOne();
      }, secs * 1000);
    },

    /** Rebuild the play-order array — identity for sequential, shuffled for random */
    _buildPlayOrder() {
      const order = this.queue.map((_, i) => i);
      if (state.bgPlaybackOrder === 'random') {
        for (let i = order.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
          const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
          [order[i], order[j]] = [order[j], order[i]];
        }
      }
      return order;
    },

    stopRotation() {
      if (this.interval) { clearInterval(this.interval); this.interval = null; }
    },

    /** Swap to a new image using a random enabled transition.
     *  Replaces the old single-style crossfade(). Falls back to crossfade if
     *  the randomly-picked one throws or no transitions are enabled. */
    swap(src) {
      const imgs = [$('bgImg0'), $('bgImg1')];
      if (!imgs[0] || !imgs[1] || !src) return;
      const oldEl = imgs[this.currentSlot];
      const newEl = imgs[1 - this.currentSlot];
      const enabled = Array.isArray(state.bgEnabledTransitions) && state.bgEnabledTransitions.length
        ? state.bgEnabledTransitions
        : BG_DEFAULT_ENABLED;
      const validEnabled = enabled.filter(k => BG_TRANSITIONS[k]);
      const pick = validEnabled.length
        ? validEnabled[Math.floor(Math.random() * validEnabled.length)]
        : 'crossfade';
      const tx = BG_TRANSITIONS[pick] || BG_TRANSITIONS.crossfade;
      const dur = Number(state.bgTransitionDuration) || 3;
      try {
        Promise.resolve(tx.run(oldEl, newEl, src, dur)).catch(e => {
          console.error('bg transition async fail:', pick, e);
        });
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('bg transition sync fail:', pick, e);
        try { BG_TRANSITIONS.crossfade.run(oldEl, newEl, src, dur); } catch {}
      }
      this.currentSlot = 1 - this.currentSlot;
    },

    /** Legacy alias — some callers still reference crossfade() directly. */
    crossfade(src) { this.swap(src); },

    setStaticImage(src) {
      const img = $('bgImg0');
      if (img) { img.src = src; img.classList.add('active'); }
      if ($('bgImg1')) $('bgImg1').classList.remove('active');
    },

    setLocalFile(file) {
      if (this._localObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(this._localObjectUrl);
      this._localObjectUrl = URL.createObjectURL(file);
      if (file.type.startsWith('video/')) {
        this.source = 'local-video';
        const vid = $('bgLocalVideo');
        if (vid) { vid.src = this._localObjectUrl; vid.style.display = 'block'; vid.play().catch(() => {}); }
      } else {
        this.source = 'local-image';
        this.setStaticImage(this._localObjectUrl);
      }
    },

    setYouTube(url) {
      const match = url.match(/(?:v=|youtu\.be\/|\/embed\/)([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{11})/);
      if (!match) return;
      const vid = match[1];
      const wrap = $('bgYoutubeWrap');
      const iframe = $('bgYoutube');
      if (wrap && iframe) {
        const cc = $('bgSubtitleToggle')?.checked ? 1 : 0;
        iframe.src = `https://www.youtube.com/embed/${vid}?autoplay=1&mute=1&loop=1&playlist=${vid}&controls=0&showinfo=0&cc_load_policy=${cc}`;
        wrap.style.display = 'block';
      }
    },

    activate() {
      const layer = $('bgLayer');
      if (layer) layer.style.display = '';
      document.body.classList.add('bg-active');
      if (this.source === 'ai') this.startRotation();
      else if (this.source === 'local-image' || this.source === 'url') { /* already set */ }
      else if (this.source === 'local-video') { const v = $('bgLocalVideo'); if (v && v.src) v.play().catch(() => {}); }
      else if (this.source === 'youtube') { const y = $('bgYoutubeUrl'); if (y?.value) this.setYouTube(y.value); }
    },

    clear() {
      this.stopRotation();
      // Revoke object URLs from queue to free memory
      this.queue.forEach(u => { try { URL.revokeObjectURL(u); } catch {} });
      this.queue = [];
      const imgs = [$('bgImg0'), $('bgImg1')];
      imgs.forEach(i => { if (i) { i.src = ''; i.classList.remove('active'); } });
