      const vid = $('bgLocalVideo'); if (vid) { vid.pause(); vid.src = ''; vid.style.display = 'none'; }
      const yt = $('bgYoutubeWrap'); if (yt) { yt.style.display = 'none'; }
      const yf = $('bgYoutube'); if (yf) yf.src = '';
      if (this._localObjectUrl) { URL.revokeObjectURL(this._localObjectUrl); this._localObjectUrl = null; }
      const layer = $('bgLayer'); if (layer) layer.style.display = 'none';
      document.body.classList.remove('bg-active');
    }
  };

  // ── Background image cache — per-image Blob storage ──
  // Manifest at 'bg_manifest' holds metadata [{id, prompt, createdAt}]
  // Each image stored separately at 'bg_img_<id>' as a Blob (no base64 overhead)
  const BG_MANIFEST_KEY = 'bg_manifest';
  const BG_MAX_IMAGES = 50;

  async function bgCacheStore(dataUrl, prompt) {
    const id = 'bg_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6);
    const blob = await fetch(dataUrl).then(r => r.blob());
    const manifest = (await idbGet(BG_MANIFEST_KEY)) || [];
    manifest.push({ id, prompt: prompt || '', createdAt: Date.now() });
    // Evict oldest if over limit
    while (manifest.length > BG_MAX_IMAGES) {
      const old = manifest.shift();
      await idbDel('bg_img_' + old.id);
    }
    await idbSet('bg_img_' + id, blob);
    await idbSet(BG_MANIFEST_KEY, manifest);
    return id;
  }
  async function bgCacheGetManifest() { return (await idbGet(BG_MANIFEST_KEY)) || []; }
  async function bgCacheGetUrl(id) {
    const blob = await idbGet('bg_img_' + id);
    return blob ? URL.createObjectURL(blob) : null;
  }
  async function bgCacheGetAllUrls() {
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    const urls = [];
    for (const entry of manifest) {
      const url = await bgCacheGetUrl(entry.id);
      if (url) urls.push(url);
    }
    return urls;
  }
  async function bgCacheDelete(id) {
    await idbDel('bg_img_' + id);
    const manifest = (await idbGet(BG_MANIFEST_KEY)) || [];
    await idbSet(BG_MANIFEST_KEY, manifest.filter(m => m.id !== id));
  }
  async function bgCacheClear() {
    const manifest = (await idbGet(BG_MANIFEST_KEY)) || [];
    for (const entry of manifest) await idbDel('bg_img_' + entry.id);
    await idbSet(BG_MANIFEST_KEY, []);
  }
  async function bgCacheDownload(id) {
    const blob = await idbGet('bg_img_' + id);
    if (!blob) return;
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = id + '.png';
    a.click();
    setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href), 5000);
  }

  async function renderBgGallery() {
    const grid = $('bgGalleryGrid');
    const info = $('bgGalleryInfo');
    const countEl = $('bgCacheCount');
    if (!grid) return;
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    if (countEl) countEl.textContent = manifest.length;
    if (info) info.textContent = `${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} · stored as binary blobs (no base64 overhead)`;
    if (!manifest.length) { grid.innerHTML = '<div class="sublabel" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;">No cached images yet. Generate some with the preview button or during a session.</div>'; return; }
    // Build grid with placeholder thumbnails, load blobs lazily
    grid.innerHTML = manifest.map(c => `
      <div class="bg-gallery-item" data-id="${c.id}">
        <img alt="" loading="lazy" style="background:#111;">
        <button class="bg-del" data-id="${c.id}" title="delete">✕</button>
        <button class="bg-dl" data-id="${c.id}" title="download">⬇</button>
      </div>`).join('');
    // Load thumbnails lazily
    for (const entry of manifest) {
      const url = await bgCacheGetUrl(entry.id);
      const img = grid.querySelector(`.bg-gallery-item[data-id="${entry.id}"] img`);
      if (img && url) img.src = url;
    }
    grid.querySelectorAll('.bg-del').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async (e) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        await bgCacheDelete(btn.dataset.id);
        renderBgGallery();
      });
    });
    grid.querySelectorAll('.bg-dl').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        bgCacheDownload(btn.dataset.id);
      });
    });
  }

  let highwayRAF = null;
  let vizRAF = null;
  let stageResizeObs = null;

  // ── Canvas Visual Renderers (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT) ──
  function hexToRgb(hex) {
    let h = hex.replace('#','');
    if (h.length === 3) h = h[0]+h[0]+h[1]+h[1]+h[2]+h[2];
    const r = parseInt(h.slice(0,2),16), g = parseInt(h.slice(2,4),16), b = parseInt(h.slice(4,6),16);
    return `${Number.isFinite(r)?r:128},${Number.isFinite(g)?g:128},${Number.isFinite(b)?b:128}`;
  }

  function renderTunnel(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.hypot(cx,cy)*1.1, RINGS = 18;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let i = RINGS; i >= 0; i--) {
      const frac = ((i/RINGS) + (t*0.18)) % 1, r = frac*maxR, alpha = (1-frac)*0.65+0.05;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,r,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5+(1-frac)*3; ctx.stroke();
    }
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx,cy,0,cx,cy,maxR*0.15);
    g.addColorStop(0,`rgba(${rgb},0.7)`); g.addColorStop(1,`rgba(${rgb},0)`);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,maxR*0.15,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = g; ctx.fill();
  }

  function renderPendulumViz(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rx = W*0.38, ry = H*0.38, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.beginPath();
    for (let i = 0; i <= 2400; i++) {
      const frac = i/2400, s = (t - frac*4);
      const x = cx + rx*Math.sin(s*1.23+0.4)*Math.cos(s*0.71);
      const y = cy + ry*Math.sin(s*0.97+1.1)*Math.cos(s*1.03);
      i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
    }
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.6)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.2; ctx.stroke();
  }

  function renderVortex(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.44, ARMS = 6;
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let arm = 0; arm < ARMS; arm++) {
      const baseAngle = (arm/ARMS)*Math.PI*2 + t*0.6;
      ctx.beginPath();
      for (let i = 0; i <= 300; i++) {
        const frac = i/300, angle = baseAngle + frac*Math.PI*3;
        const r = frac * maxR * (0.8 + 0.2*Math.sin(t*1.5+arm));
        const x = cx + r*Math.cos(angle), y = cy + r*Math.sin(angle);
        i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${0.35+0.25*Math.sin(t+arm)})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1; ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  function renderMandala(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, petals = 8, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.7)`; ctx.shadowColor = color; ctx.shadowBlur = 12;
    for (let layer = 0; layer < 4; layer++) {
      const R = (layer+1)*Math.min(W,H)*0.1;
      const spin = t*(layer%2===0 ? 0.2 : -0.15) + layer*0.4;
      ctx.globalAlpha = 0.6-layer*0.1; ctx.lineWidth = 1.8-layer*0.3;
      for (let p = 0; p < petals; p++) {
        const base = (p/petals)*Math.PI*2 + spin, tip = base + Math.PI/petals;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx,cy);
        ctx.quadraticCurveTo(cx+R*1.5*Math.cos(base+0.3),cy+R*1.5*Math.sin(base+0.3),cx+R*Math.cos(tip),cy+R*Math.sin(tip));
        ctx.stroke();
      }
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,R*0.4,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  }

  function renderLissajous(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, R = Math.min(W,H)*0.42, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.85)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.8;
    ctx.shadowColor = color; ctx.shadowBlur = 10;
    const a = 3, b = 2, delta = t*0.4;
    ctx.beginPath();
    for (let i = 0; i <= 600; i++) {
      const th = (i/600)*Math.PI*2;
      const x = cx + R*Math.sin(a*th+delta), y = cy + R*Math.sin(b*th);
      i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
    }
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.08; ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  }

  function renderColorWash(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const hue = (t*12 + parseInt(color.replace('#',''),16)%360) % 360, hue2 = (hue+40)%360;
    const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.4,H*0.4,0,W/2,H/2,Math.max(W,H)*0.7);
    grad.addColorStop(0,`hsla(${hue},70%,35%,1)`);
    grad.addColorStop(0.5,`hsla(${hue2},60%,20%,1)`);
    grad.addColorStop(1,`hsla(${(hue+180)%360},50%,8%,1)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2,H/2,H*0.2,W/2,H/2,H*0.75);
    vig.addColorStop(0,'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  function renderCanvasPulse(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.46;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
      const phase = (t*0.45 + i/6) % 1, r = phase*maxR, alpha = (1-phase)*0.7;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,r,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 2+(1-phase)*5; ctx.stroke();
    }
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,10+4*Math.sin(t*3),0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.85)`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Breathing circle — the single most evidence-based hypnotic visual
  function renderBreathingCircle(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.38, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    // 4-7-8 cycle: 4s inhale, 7s hold, 8s exhale = 19s total
    const cycle = 19, phase = t % cycle;
    // Haptic at cycle start (once per 19s)
    if (phase < 0.05 && t > 0.1) vibrateBreath();
    let frac; // 0-1 breath position
    if (phase < 4) frac = phase / 4; // inhale: expand
    else if (phase < 11) frac = 1; // hold: full
    else frac = 1 - (phase - 11) / 8; // exhale: contract
    frac = frac * frac * (3 - 2 * frac); // smoothstep ease

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const r = maxR * 0.3 + maxR * 0.7 * frac;

    // Concentric rings at phase offsets
    for (let ring = 4; ring >= 0; ring--) {
      const ringFrac = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, frac - ring * 0.04));
      const rr = maxR * 0.3 + maxR * 0.7 * ringFrac * (3 - 2 * ringFrac);
      const alpha = 0.08 + ring * 0.04;
      // Color shift: cool blue inhale → warm amber exhale
      const hue = 210 - frac * 30; // 210 (blue) → 180 (teal) at full
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, rr, 0, Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 50%, 60%, ${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5; ctx.stroke();
    }

    // Main circle
    const mainHue = 210 - frac * 40;
    const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, cy, r * 0.3, cx, cy, r);
    grad.addColorStop(0, `hsla(${mainHue}, 55%, 55%, 0.35)`);
    grad.addColorStop(1, `hsla(${mainHue}, 45%, 40%, 0.08)`);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fill();
    ctx.strokeStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 50%, 60%, 0.5)`; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();

    // Label
    let label = '';
    if (phase < 4) label = 'breathe in';
    else if (phase < 11) label = 'hold';
    else label = 'breathe out';
    ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 40%, 70%, 0.6)`;
    ctx.font = '0.8rem -apple-system, sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.fillText(label, cx, cy + r + 24);

    // Center dot
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, 4 + 2 * frac, 0, Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 50%, 70%, 0.8)`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Moiré — historically the most potent trance device (per ROADMAP)
  // Two concentric-ring patterns with one center slowly orbiting the other
  function renderMoire(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, maxR = Math.max(W, H) * 0.8;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(136,136,136,0.45)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    // First grating: centered
    for (let r = 6; r < maxR; r += 12) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    // Second grating: orbiting offset
    const ox = cx + Math.cos(t * 0.15) * 18;
    const oy = cy + Math.sin(t * 0.12) * 14;
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(136,136,136,0.4)';
    for (let r = 6; r < maxR; r += 12) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(ox, oy, r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    // Soft vignette
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, cy, maxR * 0.2, cx, cy, maxR * 0.6);
    vig.addColorStop(0, 'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Starfield warp tunnel — 3D stars projected to 2D with streak lines
  function renderStarfield(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, STARS = 200, focal = 180, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    if (!renderStarfield._pool) {
      renderStarfield._pool = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < STARS; i++) renderStarfield._pool.push({
        x: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 600, y: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 600,
        z: Math.random() * 600, psx: 0, psy: 0
      });
    }
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    const speed = 1.5 + Math.sin(t * 0.3) * 0.5;
    for (const s of renderStarfield._pool) {
      const psx = s.psx, psy = s.psy;
      s.z -= speed;
      if (s.z < 1) { s.x = (Math.random()-0.5)*600; s.y = (Math.random()-0.5)*600; s.z = 600; s.psx = cx; s.psy = cy; continue; }
      const sx = s.x / s.z * focal + cx;
      const sy = s.y / s.z * focal + cy;
      s.psx = sx; s.psy = sy;
      if (sx < 0 || sx > W || sy < 0 || sy > H) continue;
      const brightness = Math.min(1, (600 - s.z) / 400);
      const size = Math.max(0.5, (1 - s.z / 600) * 3);
      ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${brightness})`;
      // Streak line from previous position
      if (psx > 0 && Math.abs(sx - psx) < 40) {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(psx, psy); ctx.lineTo(sx, sy);
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${brightness * 0.5})`; ctx.lineWidth = size * 0.5; ctx.stroke();
      }
      ctx.fillRect(sx - size/2, sy - size/2, size, size);
    }
  }

  // Candle focal — soft radial glow with position jitter (classic Mesmerist's candle)
  function renderCandle(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H * 0.4, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    // Flame jitter
    const jx = cx + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4;
    const jy = cy + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 3;
    const baseR = 30 + Math.sin(t * 2.5) * 5 + Math.sin(t * 4.1) * 3;
    // Outer glow
    const outer = ctx.createRadialGradient(jx, jy, 0, jx, jy, baseR * 3);
    outer.addColorStop(0, `rgba(${rgb},0.15)`);
    outer.addColorStop(0.4, `rgba(${rgb},0.05)`);
    outer.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    ctx.fillStyle = outer; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    // Inner flame
    const inner = ctx.createRadialGradient(jx, jy - 4, 0, jx, jy, baseR);
    inner.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,240,200,0.7)');
    inner.addColorStop(0.3, `rgba(${rgb},0.4)`);
    inner.addColorStop(0.7, `rgba(${rgb},0.08)`);
    inner.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(jx, jy, baseR, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = inner; ctx.fill();
    // Bright core
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(jx, jy - 2, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,240,0.9)'; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Flow-field particles — simplex noise driven, additive glow
  // Uses a simplified 2D noise (value noise with smoothstep) since we can't import simplex
  function renderFlowField(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    const N = W < 500 ? 250 : 600; // Mobile vs desktop
    if (!renderFlowField._p) {
      renderFlowField._p = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) renderFlowField._p.push({ x: Math.random()*W, y: Math.random()*H, px: 0, py: 0 });
    }
    const ps = renderFlowField._p;
    // Resize pool if canvas changed
    if (ps.length < N) while (ps.length < N) ps.push({ x: Math.random()*W, y: Math.random()*H, px: 0, py: 0 });

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';

    const scale = 0.003, speed = 0.5;
    for (const p of ps) {
      p.px = p.x; p.py = p.y;
      // Simple hash-based noise field
      const nx = p.x * scale, ny = p.y * scale, nt = t * 0.08;
      const angle = (Math.sin(nx * 3.1 + nt) + Math.cos(ny * 2.7 - nt * 0.7) + Math.sin((nx + ny) * 1.4 + nt * 0.3)) * Math.PI;
      p.x += Math.cos(angle) * speed;
      p.y += Math.sin(angle) * speed;
      // Wrap around
      if (p.x < 0) p.x += W; if (p.x > W) p.x -= W;
      if (p.y < 0) p.y += H; if (p.y > H) p.y -= H;
      // Draw streak
      const dx = p.x - p.px, dy = p.y - p.py;
      if (Math.abs(dx) < 20 && Math.abs(dy) < 20) {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(p.px, p.py); ctx.lineTo(p.x, p.y);
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.3)`; ctx.lineWidth = 0.8; ctx.stroke();
      }
    }
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
    // Vignette
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H/2, Math.min(W,H)*0.2, W/2, H/2, Math.min(W,H)*0.6);
    vig.addColorStop(0, 'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Classic plasma — sum of sines mapped through HSV palette
  function renderPlasma(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    // Render at reduced resolution for performance
    const rW = 192, rH = Math.round(rW * H / W);
    if (!renderPlasma._img || renderPlasma._img.width !== rW) {
      renderPlasma._off = (typeof OffscreenCanvas !== 'undefined') ? new OffscreenCanvas(rW, rH) : document.createElement('canvas');
      renderPlasma._off.width = rW; renderPlasma._off.height = rH;
      renderPlasma._img = renderPlasma._off.getContext('2d').createImageData(rW, rH);
      // Precompute sine LUT
      renderPlasma._sin = new Float32Array(1024);
      for (let i = 0; i < 1024; i++) renderPlasma._sin[i] = Math.sin(i * Math.PI * 2 / 1024);
    }
    const data = renderPlasma._img.data, sinLut = renderPlasma._sin;
    const S = v => sinLut[((v % 1024) + 1024) % 1024 | 0];

    for (let y = 0; y < rH; y++) {
      for (let x = 0; x < rW; x++) {
        const v = S(x * 3 + t * 40) + S(y * 4 - t * 30) + S((x + y) * 2 + t * 20) + S(Math.sqrt(x*x + y*y) * 2 - t * 50);
        const hue = ((v + 4) / 8 * 360 + t * 15) % 360;
        // HSV to RGB (S=0.7, V=0.6)
        const c = 0.42, x2 = c * (1 - Math.abs((hue / 60) % 2 - 1));
        let r1=0,g1=0,b1=0;
        const h = Math.floor(hue / 60) % 6;
        if (h===0){r1=c;g1=x2;}else if(h===1){r1=x2;g1=c;}else if(h===2){g1=c;b1=x2;}
        else if(h===3){g1=x2;b1=c;}else if(h===4){r1=x2;b1=c;}else{r1=c;b1=x2;}
        const m = 0.18;
        const idx = (y * rW + x) * 4;
        data[idx] = (r1+m)*255; data[idx+1] = (g1+m)*255; data[idx+2] = (b1+m)*255; data[idx+3] = 255;
      }
    }
    const offCtx = renderPlasma._off.getContext('2d');
    offCtx.putImageData(renderPlasma._img, 0, 0);
    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
    ctx.drawImage(renderPlasma._off, 0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Kaleidoscope — wraps any sub-renderer with N-fold mirror symmetry
  function makeKaleidoscope(subRenderer, folds = 6) {
    return function(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
      const cx = W/2, cy = H/2;
      // Render sub-effect to an offscreen canvas
      if (!makeKaleidoscope._off || makeKaleidoscope._off.width !== W) {
        makeKaleidoscope._off = document.createElement('canvas');
        makeKaleidoscope._off.width = W; makeKaleidoscope._off.height = H;
      }
      const offCtx = makeKaleidoscope._off.getContext('2d');
      subRenderer(offCtx, W, H, t, color);
      // Draw N wedges with alternating mirrors
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);
      const wedgeAngle = Math.PI * 2 / folds;
      for (let i = 0; i < folds; i++) {
        ctx.save();
        ctx.translate(cx, cy);
        ctx.rotate(wedgeAngle * i);
        if (i % 2 === 1) ctx.scale(-1, 1); // Mirror alternate wedges
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, 0);
        ctx.lineTo(Math.max(W, H), 0);
        ctx.arc(0, 0, Math.max(W, H), 0, wedgeAngle);
        ctx.closePath();
        ctx.clip();
        ctx.translate(-cx, -cy);
        ctx.drawImage(makeKaleidoscope._off, 0, 0);
        ctx.restore();
      }
    };
  }

  // Aurora borealis — undulating gradient curtains
  function renderAurora(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    for (let b = 0; b < 4; b++) {
      const ph = b * 1.7 + t * 0.0004;
      const y = H * 0.25 + Math.sin(ph) * H * 0.12 + Math.sin(ph * 0.7 + b) * H * 0.06;
      const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, y - 100, 0, y + 140);
      grad.addColorStop(0, 'transparent');
      grad.addColorStop(0.3, `rgba(${rgb},${0.035 + b * 0.008})`);
      grad.addColorStop(0.7, `rgba(${rgb},${0.05 - b * 0.008})`);
      grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
      ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    }
  }

  // Rain drops — falling streaks with splash
  function renderRain(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    if (!renderRain._drops) { renderRain._drops = []; for (let i = 0; i < 120; i++) renderRain._drops.push({ x: Math.random() * W, y: Math.random() * H, len: 8 + Math.random() * 18, speed: 4 + Math.random() * 6 }); }
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.25)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    for (const d of renderRain._drops) {
      d.y += d.speed; if (d.y > H) { d.y = -d.len; d.x = Math.random() * W; }
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(d.x, d.y); ctx.lineTo(d.x - 0.5, d.y + d.len); ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  // Sacred geometry — Flower of Life
  function renderSacredGeo(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color), cx = W/2, cy = H/2, R = Math.min(W,H) * 0.18;
    const rot = t * 0.00015;
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${0.15 + Math.sin(t * 0.001) * 0.05})`; ctx.lineWidth = 0.8;
    const pts = [[0,0]]; for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) pts.push([Math.cos(i * Math.PI/3) * R, Math.sin(i * Math.PI/3) * R]);
    for (let ring = 0; ring < 2; ring++) for (const [px,py] of pts) {
      const r = R * (ring === 0 ? 1 : 1.73);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx + px * (ring+1) * Math.cos(rot) - py * Math.sin(rot), cy + px * (ring+1) * Math.sin(rot) + py * Math.cos(rot), r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  // Waveform — phase-aware frequency shift (beta→theta)
  function renderWaveform(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color), cy = H/2;
    const freq = 0.02 + Math.sin(t * 0.0003) * 0.015; // shifts over time
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, cy);
    for (let x = 0; x < W; x++) {
      const amp = H * 0.15 * (1 + Math.sin(t * 0.0005) * 0.3);
      ctx.lineTo(x, cy + Math.sin(x * freq + t * 0.002) * amp * Math.sin(x / W * Math.PI));
    }
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.4)`; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
  }

  // Smoke / fog — drifting translucent circles
  function renderSmoke(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    if (!renderSmoke._puffs) { renderSmoke._puffs = []; for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) renderSmoke._puffs.push({ x: Math.random() * W, y: Math.random() * H, r: 60 + Math.random() * 120, vx: (Math.random()-0.5)*0.3, vy: (Math.random()-0.5)*0.2 }); }
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.02)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (const p of renderSmoke._puffs) {
      p.x += p.vx; p.y += p.vy;
      if (p.x < -p.r) p.x = W + p.r; if (p.x > W + p.r) p.x = -p.r;
      if (p.y < -p.r) p.y = H + p.r; if (p.y > H + p.r) p.y = -p.r;
      const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(p.x, p.y, 0, p.x, p.y, p.r);
      grad.addColorStop(0, `rgba(${rgb},0.025)`); grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
      ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(p.x - p.r, p.y - p.r, p.r * 2, p.r * 2);
    }
  }

  const VIZ_RENDERERS = {
    tunnel: renderTunnel,
    'pendulum-viz': renderPendulumViz,
    vortex: renderVortex,
    mandala: renderMandala,
    lissajous: renderLissajous,
    colorwash: renderColorWash,
    'canvas-pulse': renderCanvasPulse,
    breathing: renderBreathingCircle,
    moire: renderMoire,
    starfield: renderStarfield,
    candle: renderCandle,
    flowfield: renderFlowField,
    plasma: renderPlasma,
    'kaleidoscope-flow': makeKaleidoscope(renderFlowField, 6),
    'kaleidoscope-plasma': makeKaleidoscope(renderPlasma, 8),
    aurora: renderAurora,
    rain: renderRain,
    'sacred-geo': renderSacredGeo,
    waveform: renderWaveform,
    smoke: renderSmoke,
  };

  // Phase-based speed multipliers for visuals
  const PHASE_VIZ_SPEED = { settling: 0.5, induction: 1.0, deepener: 0.7, work: 0.9, lightener: 0.75, wake: 0.95, reintroduction: 0.8, emergence: 0.95 };

  // ====================================================================
  // PREVIEW ENGINES (Configure tab — separate from session playback)
  // ====================================================================

  // Soundscape preview — uses a separate SoundscapeEngine instance
  const _previewDrone = new SoundscapeEngine();
  let _previewDroneTimeout = null;

  async function previewSoundscape() {
    const type = $('soundscapeSelect')?.value;
    if (!type || type === 'none') { notify.info('Select a soundscape first.'); return; }
    await stopSoundscapePreview();
    try {
      await _previewDrone.start(state.droneVolume, type);
      togglePreviewBtns('sound', true);

      $('soundPreviewHint').textContent = 'playing ' + type + '...';
      // Auto-stop after 10 seconds
      _previewDroneTimeout = setTimeout(() => stopSoundscapePreview(), 10000);
    } catch(e) { notify.warn('Could not start audio preview.'); }
  }

  async function stopSoundscapePreview() {
    clearTimeout(_previewDroneTimeout);
    await _previewDrone.stop();
    togglePreviewBtns('sound', false);

    $('soundPreviewHint').textContent = 'Listen to a 10-second preview.';
  }

  // Viz preview — renders to the mini canvas with its own rAF loop
  let _vizPreviewRaf = null;
  let _vizPreviewStart = 0;

  function startVizPreview() {
    stopVizPreview();
    const sel = $('vizSelect')?.value;
    const vizKey = sel === 'auto' ? (getMethod().visual) : sel;
    const renderer = VIZ_RENDERERS[vizKey];
    if (!renderer) {
      // Non-canvas types (highway, spiral, pulse, none) — show a label instead
      const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
      if (wrap) { wrap.style.display = 'block'; }
      const canvas = $('vizPreviewCanvas');
      if (canvas) { const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height); ctx.fillStyle = '#4a6a84'; ctx.font = '13px -apple-system, sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; ctx.fillText(vizKey === 'none' ? 'Black screen — no visual' : vizKey + ' (non-canvas preview)', canvas.width/2, canvas.height/2); }
      $('vizPreviewLabel').textContent = vizKey;
      togglePreviewBtns('viz', true);

      return;
    }

    const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
    const canvas = $('vizPreviewCanvas');
    if (!wrap || !canvas) return;
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth || 300;
    canvas.height = 120;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha: false });
    const color = '#6b94b8';
    _vizPreviewStart = performance.now();
    $('vizPreviewLabel').textContent = vizKey;
    togglePreviewBtns('viz', true);

    function frame() {
      const t = ((performance.now() - _vizPreviewStart) / 1000) * (state.vizSettings.speed || 1.0);
      try { renderer(ctx, canvas.width, canvas.height, t, color); } catch(e) {}
      _vizPreviewRaf = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
    }
    _vizPreviewRaf = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
  }

  function stopVizPreview() {
    if (_vizPreviewRaf) { cancelAnimationFrame(_vizPreviewRaf); _vizPreviewRaf = null; }
    const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
    if (wrap) wrap.style.display = 'none';
    togglePreviewBtns('viz', false);

  }

  // Voice preview state
  let _voicePreviewing = false;

  function setupVisual(visualType) {
    const stage = $('stage');
    // Clean up previous visuals
    if (vizRAF) { cancelAnimationFrame(vizRAF); vizRAF = null; }
    if (highwayRAF) { cancelAnimationFrame(highwayRAF); highwayRAF = null; }
    if (stageResizeObs) { stageResizeObs.disconnect(); stageResizeObs = null; }
    Array.from(stage.children).forEach(c => {
      if (!c.classList.contains('fixation-dot') && !c.classList.contains('audio-indicator')
        && !c.classList.contains('persona-indicator') && !c.classList.contains('method-indicator')
        && !c.classList.contains('session-progress-wrap')) c.remove();
    });

    // Canvas-based renderer (new visual types)
    const renderer = VIZ_RENDERERS[visualType];
    if (renderer) {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas'); canvas.className = 'highway-canvas';
      canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
      stage.insertBefore(canvas, stage.firstChild);
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      const color = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--accent').trim() || '#6b94b8';
      // Resize observer
      stageResizeObs = new ResizeObserver(() => { canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight; });
      stageResizeObs.observe(stage);
      (function draw(ts) {
        if (state.abortFlag) return;
        const speed = (PHASE_VIZ_SPEED[state._currentPhase] || 1.0) * (state.vizSettings.speed || 1.0);
        renderer(ctx, canvas.width, canvas.height, (ts/1000)*speed, color);
        vizRAF = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
      })(0);
      return;
    }

    if (visualType === 'highway') {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas'); canvas.className = 'highway-canvas';
      canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
      stage.insertBefore(canvas, stage.firstChild);
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      // Resize observer
      stageResizeObs = new ResizeObserver(() => { canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight; });
      stageResizeObs.observe(stage);
      const lines = []; for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) lines.push({ y: (canvas.height / 8) * i, speed: 1.2 + Math.random() * 0.4 });
      (function draw() {
        if (state.abortFlag) return;
        const W = canvas.width, H = canvas.height;
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(212,220,232,0.55)'; ctx.lineWidth = 4;
        lines.forEach(l => { l.y += l.speed; if (l.y > H + 40) l.y = -40; ctx.globalAlpha = Math.min(1,(l.y/H)*1.2)*0.7; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(W/2, l.y); ctx.lineTo(W/2, l.y+28); ctx.stroke(); });
        ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
        const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H*0.38, 20, W/2, H*0.38, H*0.5); g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)');
        ctx.fillStyle = g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        highwayRAF = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
      })();
    } else if (visualType === 'spiral') {
      const svg = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','svg');
      svg.setAttribute('class','spiral-svg'); svg.setAttribute('viewBox','0 0 100 100');
      let d = 'M 50 50 ';
      for (let t=0;t<30;t+=0.1) { const r=0.5*t; d += `L ${(50+r*Math.cos(t)).toFixed(2)} ${(50+r*Math.sin(t)).toFixed(2)} `; }
      const p = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','path');
      p.setAttribute('d',d); p.setAttribute('stroke','rgba(107,148,184,0.4)'); p.setAttribute('stroke-width','0.4'); p.setAttribute('fill','none');
      svg.appendChild(p); stage.insertBefore(svg, stage.firstChild);
    } else {
      // Default: CSS pulse rings
      const wrap = document.createElement('div'); wrap.className = 'pulse-rings';
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) { const r = document.createElement('div'); r.className = 'pulse-ring'; wrap.appendChild(r); }
      stage.insertBefore(wrap, stage.firstChild);
    }
  }
  const stopVisuals = () => {
    if (highwayRAF) cancelAnimationFrame(highwayRAF); highwayRAF = null;
    if (vizRAF) cancelAnimationFrame(vizRAF); vizRAF = null;
    if (stageResizeObs) { stageResizeObs.disconnect(); stageResizeObs = null; }
  };

  // ====================================================================
  // PERSONA EDITOR
  // ====================================================================
  function openPersonaEditor(id) {
    state.editingPersonaId = id;
    $('personaModalTitle').textContent = id ? 'edit persona' : 'create custom persona';
    if (id) {
      const p = state.personas.find(x => x.id === id);
      $('personaFormName').value = p.name;
      $('personaFormTagline').value = p.tagline;
      $('personaFormPrompt').value = p.systemPrompt;
      $('personaFormCategory').value = p.category || 'contemplative';
    } else {
      $('personaFormName').value = '';
      $('personaFormTagline').value = '';
      $('personaFormPrompt').value = '';
      $('personaFormCategory').value = 'contemplative';
    }
    $('personaModal').classList.add('visible');
  }
  const closePersonaEditor = () => { $('personaModal').classList.remove('visible'); state.editingPersonaId = null; };
  function savePersonaFromForm() {
    const name = $('personaFormName').value.trim();
    const tagline = $('personaFormTagline').value.trim();
    const systemPrompt = $('personaFormPrompt').value.trim();
    const category = $('personaFormCategory').value || 'contemplative';
    if (!name || !systemPrompt) { notify.warn('Name and voice instruction required.'); return; }
    let custom = loadCustomPersonas();
    if (state.editingPersonaId) {
      custom = custom.map(p => p.id === state.editingPersonaId ? { ...p, name, tagline, systemPrompt, category } : p);
    } else {
      const id = 'custom_' + Date.now();
      custom.push({ id, name, tagline: tagline || '(custom)', systemPrompt, category });
      state.selectedPersonaId = id;
      markFeatureUsed(FEAT.CUSTOM_PERSONA); // mark feature only when a NEW custom persona is created
    }
    if (!saveCustomPersonas(custom)) { notify.error('Could not save: browser storage may be full.'); return; }
    refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); closePersonaEditor();
  }
  async function deletePersona(id) {
    if (!await confirmAsync('Delete this persona?')) return;
    saveCustomPersonas(loadCustomPersonas().filter(p => p.id !== id));
    if (state.selectedPersonaId === id) state.selectedPersonaId = 'driver';
    refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail();
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // CRAFTER
  // ====================================================================
  let _aiInProgress = false; // Prevents double-click firing two concurrent AI calls

  async function craftSuggestion() {
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('An AI call is already in progress.'); return; }
    // Resolve \{\{...\}\} tokens before feeding the AI so the model sees concrete text.
    const rough = resolveTokens($('intentionInput').value.trim());
    const skipTypes = ['trance', 'sleep'];
    if (!rough && !skipTypes.includes(state.intentionType)) { notify.warn('Describe what you want first.'); return; }
    const type = INTENTION_TYPES[state.intentionType];
    if (!type) { notify.warn('Select an intention type first.'); return; }
    _aiInProgress = true;
    const progressLabel = $('craftProgressLabel');
    setLoading('craftBtn', true);
    setLoading('recraftBtn', true);
    $('craftProgress').classList.add('visible');
    progressLabel.textContent = 'crafting your suggestion — about 2–3 minutes...';
    const stopTimer = makeElapsedTimer(s => { progressLabel.textContent = `crafting... ${s}s elapsed`; });

    // Token-budgeted prompt assembly. The JSON-output schema and
    // universal rules are priority-5 (never trimmed); profile context trims
    // first if we're near the context limit.
    const headerBlock = `You are a master hypnotherapist converting a user's rough intention into a technically-precise hypnotic suggestion.

TYPE: ${type.label}
USER'S ROUGH DESCRIPTION: "${rough}"

UNIVERSAL RULES:
• Second person ("you")
• Presupposition ("you'll notice" not "you will feel") [For convincer/novelty: direct present-tense fine]
• Somatic anchoring (tie states to physical sensations)
• Automaticity ("automatically", "without effort")
• Progressive intensification
• Future-pacing ("from now on")
• Positive construction only
• Specificity

TYPE-SPECIFIC GUIDANCE:
${type.guidance}`;
    const profileBlock = getProfileContext();
    const schemaBlock = `
Output EXACTLY this JSON, no other text, no markdown fences:
{
  "craftedSuggestion": "Complete hypnotic suggestion, 3-5 sentences, ready to deliver verbatim. Second person.",
  "trigger": "Specific trigger phrase, or 'ongoing state'",
  "coreResponse": "Specific response/effect, 3-7 words",
  "reinforcementPhrases": ["Three or four short variants (5-10 words)"],
  "explanation": "ONE sentence on the technique used"
}`;
    const instruction = trimToTokenBudget([
      { name: 'header',   text: headerBlock,  priority: 5 },
      { name: 'profile',  text: profileBlock, priority: 2 },
      { name: 'schema',   text: schemaBlock,  priority: 5 },
    ], 600);

    try {
      const data = await root.aiTextPlugin({ instruction, startWith: '{', stopSequences: ['\n\n\n'], hideStartWith: true });
      // guard against error status AND empty output
      if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') throw new Error('AI generation encountered an error.');
      let text = (data.generatedText || '').trim();
      if (!text) throw new Error('AI returned empty text — please try again.');
      if (!text.startsWith('{')) text = '{' + text;
      const lb = text.lastIndexOf('}'); if (lb > -1) text = text.substring(0, lb + 1);
      state.craftedSuggestion = JSON.parse(text);
      showCrafted();
      updateStepUI();
      notify.success('Suggestion crafted successfully.');
    } catch (e) { console.error(e); notify.warn('Crafting failed: ' + e.message + '. Try again.'); }
    finally {
      _aiInProgress = false;
      stopTimer();
      setLoading('craftBtn', false, 'craft hypnotic suggestion →');
      setLoading('recraftBtn', false);
      $('craftProgress').classList.remove('visible');
    }
  }
  function showCrafted() {
    const c = state.craftedSuggestion;
    $('craftedText').textContent = c.craftedSuggestion;
    $('craftedText').style.display = 'block';
    $('craftedEditable').style.display = 'none';
    $('saveEditBtn').style.display = 'none';
    $('craftedMeta').innerHTML = `<strong>trigger:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.trigger||'—')}  ·  <strong>effect:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.coreResponse||'—')}<br><strong>technique:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.explanation||'—')}`;
    $('craftedPreview').classList.add('visible');
  }
  function hideCrafted() { state.craftedSuggestion = null; $('craftedPreview').classList.remove('visible'); hideScript(); }
  function toggleEditCrafted() {
    const t = $('craftedText'), e = $('craftedEditable'), s = $('saveEditBtn');
    e.value = state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion;
    t.style.display = 'none'; e.style.display = 'block'; s.style.display = 'inline-block';
  }
  function saveEditCrafted() {
    state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion = $('craftedEditable').value.trim();
    showCrafted(); hideScript();
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SCRIPT GEN — per-phase generation with live progress
  // ====================================================================

  /** Session work block count by selected length */
  function getWorkBlockCount() {
    if (state.length === 'long') return 5;
    if (state.length === 'medium') return 2;
    return 1;
  }

  function getPhaseLabel(phaseId) {
    if (!phaseId) return 'Phase';
    const base = phaseId.replace(/-\d+$/, '');
    const idx = phaseId.includes('-') ? phaseId.split('-').pop() : '';
    const labels = {
      settling: 'Settling',
      induction: 'Induction',
      deepener: 'Deepener',
      lightener: 'Lightener',
      wake: 'Wake',
      reintroduction: 'Reintroduction',
      emergence: 'Emergence',
      work: idx ? `Work ${idx}` : 'Work',
      affirm: idx ? `Affirmation ${idx}` : 'Affirmation',
    };
    return labels[base] || phaseId;
  }

  function phaseIdToMarker(phaseId) {
    return String(phaseId || 'work').toUpperCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
  }

  function markerToPhaseId(marker) {
    return String(marker || '').toLowerCase();
  }

  const PHASE_MARKER_CAPTURE_RX = /===\s*([A-Z0-9-]+)\s*===/gi;
  const PHASE_MARKER_SPLIT_RX = /(===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===)/gi;
  const PHASE_MARKER_STRIP_RX = /===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===/gi;

  function stripLeadingPhaseHeader(text, phaseId = '') {
    let out = String(text || '').replace(/^﻿/, '').trimStart();
    // Canonical marker line, including numbered phases like WORK-1 / AFFIRM-2
    out = out.replace(/^===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===\s*(?:\r?\n)?/i, '');
    // Markdown / label-only heading lines at the top of a generated phase
    const base = String(phaseId || '').replace(/-\d+$/, '');
    const num = (String(phaseId || '').match(/-(\d+)$/) || [])[1];
    const labelMap = {
      settling: 'settling',
      induction: 'induction',
      deepener: 'deepener',
      lightener: 'lightener',
      wake: 'wake',
      reintroduction: 'reintroduction',
      emergence: 'emergence',
      work: num ? `work(?:\s*[-:]?\s*${num})?` : 'work(?:\s*[-:]?\s*\d+)?',
      affirm: num ? `affirm(?:ation)?(?:\s*[-:]?\s*${num})?` : 'affirm(?:ation)?(?:\s*[-:]?\s*\d+)?',
    };
    const phaseRx = labelMap[base];
    if (phaseRx) {
      const headingOnly = new RegExp(`^(?:[#>*-]+\s*)?(?:phase\s*[:\-]\s*)?(?:${phaseRx})\s*:?(?:\r?\n)+`, 'i');
      out = out.replace(headingOnly, '');
      const bareLine = new RegExp(`^(?:phase\s*[:\-]\s*)?(?:${phaseRx})\s*:?\s*(?:\r?\n)+`, 'i');
      out = out.replace(bareLine, '');
    }
    return out.trim();
  }

  function stripAllPhaseMarkers(text) {
    return String(text || '').replace(/===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===/gi, ' ');
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // PHASE PAIRS — Induction↔Emergence, Deepener↔Lightener (nestable)
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * "Trance entry" pair: an Induction must be matched by wake + reintroduction
   * (the two phases that together form Emergence).
   * "Depth" pair: every Deepener must be matched by a Lightener. Multiple
   * Deepeners can be nested; their Lighteners unwind in reverse (LIFO).
   *
   * Sleep sessions (state.intentionType === 'sleep') deliberately skip the
   * trance-entry closers — the user is meant to drift into natural sleep.
   */
  const PHASE_BASE_RX = /-\d+$/;
  const phaseBase = id => String(id || '').replace(PHASE_BASE_RX, '');

  const PHASE_PAIR_GROUP = {
    induction: 'trance',
    wake: 'trance',
    reintroduction: 'trance',
    deepener: 'depth',
    lightener: 'depth',
  };
  /** Phases that must exist at end of session for a "safe" finish. */
  const SAFE_ENDING_PHASES = ['lightener', 'wake', 'reintroduction'];

  /**
   * Default structure per spec:
   *   \{\{Settling\}\} \{\{Induction\}\} \{\{Deepener\}\} -> (\{\{Work\}\}, \{\{Affirm\}\}) x N -> \{\{Lightener\}\} \{\{Wake\}\} \{\{Reintroduction\}\}
   * Sleep intention skips the ending trio (drifts into sleep).
   */
  function getSessionPhaseBlueprint() {
    const phases = ['settling', 'induction', 'deepener'];
    const workCount = getWorkBlockCount();
    const userAff = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    const hasAff = !!userAff;
    for (let i = 1; i <= workCount; i++) {
      // (Work, Affirm) pair — affirm follows each work when user has affirmations
      phases.push(workCount > 1 ? `work-${i}` : 'work');
      if (hasAff) phases.push(workCount > 1 ? `affirm-${i}` : 'affirm');
    }
    if (state.intentionType === 'sleep') return phases;
    phases.push('lightener', 'wake', 'reintroduction');
    return phases;
  }

  /**
   * Count how many Deepener and Lightener phases are currently in sections,
   * used to determine nesting depth when adding another.
   */
  function countPhaseBase(sections, base) {
    return sections.filter(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === base).length;
  }

  /**
   * Find the insertion index for a new phase of a given kind, respecting the
   * canonical order: settling → induction → deepeners → (work/affirm) → lighteners → wake → reintro.
   * Returns an index into `sections` where the new phase should be spliced in.
   */
  function findPhaseInsertionIdx(sections, kind) {
    const idxOf = (pred) => sections.findIndex(pred);
    const lastIdxOf = (pred) => {
      let last = -1;
      sections.forEach((s, i) => { if (pred(s)) last = i; });
      return last;
    };
    if (kind === 'settling') {
      return 0; // always first
    }
    if (kind === 'induction') {
      // After last settling, before first deepener/work/lightener/wake/reintro
      const afterSettling = lastIdxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'settling');
      const anchor = idxOf(s => ['deepener','work','affirm','lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (anchor >= 0) return anchor;
      if (afterSettling >= 0) return afterSettling + 1;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'deepener') {
      // After last existing deepener (nesting), before first work/affirm
      const lastDeepener = lastIdxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'deepener');
      if (lastDeepener >= 0) return lastDeepener + 1;
      // Otherwise after induction, before work
      const afterInduction = lastIdxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'induction');
      const beforeWork = idxOf(s => ['work','affirm','lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (beforeWork >= 0) return beforeWork;
      if (afterInduction >= 0) return afterInduction + 1;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'work' || kind === 'affirm') {
      // Before first lightener/wake/reintro; after last existing work/affirm
      const beforeReturn = idxOf(s => ['lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (beforeReturn >= 0) return beforeReturn;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'lightener') {
      // After last work/affirm, before wake (LIFO unwind — outermost lightener last)
      const lastWork = lastIdxOf(s => ['work','affirm'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      const firstWake = idxOf(s => ['wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (firstWake >= 0) {
        // Insert immediately before the first wake, so the newest lightener
        // sits closest to wake (LIFO: later-added deepeners get closed first).
        return firstWake;
      }
      if (lastWork >= 0) return lastWork + 1;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'wake') {
      const reintroIdx = idxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'reintroduction');
      if (reintroIdx >= 0) return reintroIdx;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'reintroduction') {
      return sections.length;
    }
    return sections.length;
  }

  function getPhaseList() {
    return getSessionPhaseBlueprint();
  }

  function getPlaybackPhaseOrder() {
    if (state.generatedPhaseOrder?.length) return [...state.generatedPhaseOrder];
    if (state.parsedScript?.ordered?.length) return [...state.parsedScript.ordered];
    return getPhaseList();
  }

  /** Render phase progress with state: pending, streaming, done, error, warn */
  function renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, eta, retryCallback) {
    const wrap = $('genProgress');
    const container = $('genPhases');
    const etaEl = $('genEta');
    if (!wrap || !container) return;
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    container.innerHTML = phases.map((p, i) => {
      const label = getPhaseLabel(p);
      const st = stateMask[i] || 'pending';
      return `<div class="gen-phase ${st}" data-phase-idx="${i}"><div class="gen-dot"></div><span>${label}</span></div>`;
    }).join('');
    if (etaEl) etaEl.textContent = eta || '';
    // Streaming preview box — ensure it exists under the phase list.
    if (!$('genStreamBox')) {
      const box = document.createElement('div');
      box.id = 'genStreamBox';
      box.className = 'gen-stream-box';
      box.innerHTML = `<div class="gen-stream-label" id="genStreamLabel">generating…</div><div class="gen-stream-text" id="genStreamText"></div>`;
      container.parentNode.insertBefore(box, container.nextSibling);
    }
    if (retryCallback) {
      container.querySelectorAll('.gen-phase.error, .gen-phase.warn').forEach(el => {
        el.addEventListener('click', () => retryCallback(parseInt(el.dataset.phaseIdx)));
      });
    }
  }

  /** Show/update the streaming preview for the phase currently generating. */
  function setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, text, opts = {}) {
    const box = $('genStreamBox'); if (!box) return;
    if (opts.hide) { box.classList.remove('active', 'done'); return; }
    box.classList.add('active');
    if (opts.done) box.classList.add('done'); else box.classList.remove('done');
    const label = $('genStreamLabel');
    const textEl = $('genStreamText');
    if (label) label.textContent = phaseLabel ? `generating · ${phaseLabel.toLowerCase()}` : 'generating…';
    if (textEl) {
      // Truncate displayed text to keep the DOM light on very long phases —
      // tail-biased so user sees fresh content.
      const display = text.length > 1400 ? '…' + text.slice(text.length - 1400) : text;
      textEl.textContent = display;
      // Auto-scroll to bottom so streaming feels like a running transcript.
      box.scrollTop = box.scrollHeight;
    }
  }

  // Generation state held outside so retry can access it
  let _genState = null;

  async function generateFullScript() {
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('An AI call is already in progress.'); return; }
    const editedText = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (state.fullScript && editedText && editedText !== state.fullScript.trim()) {
      if (!await confirmAsync('Your manual edits to the script will be discarded. Regenerate anyway?')) return;
    }
    _aiInProgress = true;
    const persona = getPersona();
    const method = getMethod();
    const durations = PHASE_DURATIONS[state.length];
    // Resolve \{\{...\}\} tokens in user-written text BEFORE feeding the AI, so
    // the model sees real values. Any token the AI later emits in its output
    // will be caught again at TTS-time by the resolver in speakScript.
    const rough = resolveTokens($('intentionInput').value.trim());
    const wpm = 50;
    const targetWords = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(durations).map(([k,v]) => [k, Math.round(v * wpm / 60)]));
    const scriptBuildProgress = $('scriptBuildProgress');
    if (scriptBuildProgress) scriptBuildProgress.style.display = 'block';

    setLoading('generateScriptBtn', true);
    setLoading('regenScriptBtn', true);

    const phases = getPhaseList();
    const stateMask = phases.map(() => 'pending');
    const phaseTimes = [];
    const phaseResults = {};

    const craftedBlock = state.craftedSuggestion ? `\nCRAFTED SUGGESTION: "${state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion}"\nTRIGGER: ${state.craftedSuggestion.trigger}\nEFFECT: ${state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse}` : '';
    const userAffRaw = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    // Resolve tokens in user affirmations line-by-line so \{\{user\}\} etc. in
    // affirmations become concrete text before being injected into prompts.
    const affirmLines = userAffRaw ? userAffRaw.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).map(l => resolveTokens(l.trim())) : [];
    const affirmBlock = affirmLines.length ? `\nUSER AFFIRMATIONS:\n${affirmLines.map(l => `"${l}"`).join('\n')}` : '';
    const demoNote = method.category === 'demonstration' ? '\nDEMONSTRATION METHOD: direct suggestions, build effect, include TEST.' : '';

    const profileCtx = getProfileContext();
    // Smart Director gate — when off, don't pull adaptive or memory context at all.
    // getProfileContext() already gates itself. See _debug for bypass considerations.
    const sdOn = state.smartDirectorEnabled !== false;
    let adaptiveCtx = '';
    if (sdOn) {
      try { const ap = await getAdaptive(); adaptiveCtx = getAdaptivePromptBlock(ap); } catch {}
    } else { sdLog('adaptiveCtx skipped — Smart Director off'); }

    // Director Brief — built once per session generation (not per phase)
    // so it adds ≤ 1 extra round-trip of IDB reads, no AI call. Formatted block
    // is short (≤ 300 chars) and takes priority 3 alongside profile.
    let directorBriefCtx = '';
    if (sdOn) {
      try {
        const living = await buildLivingProfile();
        const brief = computeDirectorBrief(living, {
          persona: persona.name,
          method: method.name,
          intention: rough,
          length: state.length,
        });
        directorBriefCtx = formatDirectorBriefForPrompt(brief);
        // Stash the brief on state so the session record can capture which
        // brief was active (useful for retrospective debugging in future).
        state._lastDirectorBrief = brief;
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Director brief build failed:', e); }
    } else { sdLog('directorBriefCtx skipped — Smart Director off'); }

    // Memory context — prefer semantic retrieval over pure recency.
    // Fall back to rolling window + long-term profile when embeddings aren't
    // available or no relevant matches exist.
    let memoryCtx = '';
    if (sdOn) {
      try {
        const mem = await getMemory();
        // Top-K most semantically similar past digests (embedding-based)
        const relevant = await findRelevantDigests(rough || (persona.name + ' ' + method.name), 3);
        const relevantBlock = relevant.length
          ? '\nMOST RELEVANT PAST SESSIONS (by semantic similarity to this intention):\n' +
            relevant.map(r => `- [similarity ${((1 - r.distance) * 100).toFixed(0)}%] ${r.digest.digest}`).join('\n')
          : '';
        const baseBlock = (mem.rollingWindow || mem.longTermProfile)
          ? `\nPRACTITIONER MEMORY:${mem.longTermProfile ? '\nProfile: ' + mem.longTermProfile : ''}${mem.rollingWindow ? '\nRecent patterns: ' + mem.rollingWindow : ''}`
          : '';
        memoryCtx = baseBlock + relevantBlock;
        sdLog('memoryCtx built', { relevantCount: relevant.length, hasRolling: !!mem.rollingWindow, hasLongTerm: !!mem.longTermProfile });
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Memory context build failed:', e); }
    } else { sdLog('memoryCtx skipped — Smart Director off'); }

    // Build sharedContext under a token budget — priority order
    // determines what gets dropped first if the user has a huge profile +
    // long memory + many affirmations.
    const headerBlock = `You are ${persona.name}. ${persona.systemPrompt}\nMETHOD: ${method.name}. ${method.detail}\nPACING: ${PACING_RULES[method.pacing]}\nTHEME: "${rough || 'general trance experience'}"`;
    const sharedContext = trimToTokenBudget([
      { name: 'header',    text: headerBlock,       priority: 5 }, // persona + method + theme — never drop
      { name: 'crafted',   text: craftedBlock,      priority: 4 },
      { name: 'affirm',    text: affirmBlock,       priority: 4 },
      { name: 'demoNote',  text: demoNote,          priority: 4 },
      { name: 'director',  text: directorBriefCtx,  priority: 3 }, // short, actionable, high-value
      { name: 'profile',   text: profileCtx,        priority: 3 },
      { name: 'adaptive',  text: adaptiveCtx,       priority: 2 },
      { name: 'memory',    text: memoryCtx,         priority: 1 }, // first to drop
    ], 1200); // leave generous headroom for per-phase task block + output

    // Count nested Deepener/Lightener pairs so we can produce depth-aware prompts.
    // getSessionPhaseBlueprint yields 'deepener' (unnumbered) when there's one, otherwise
    // 'deepener-1', 'deepener-2', etc. Post-blueprint edits (user add/remove) can also
    // produce arbitrary configurations; we look at the actual phase list.
    const deepenerPhases = phases.filter(p => phaseBase(p) === 'deepener');
    const lightenerPhases = phases.filter(p => phaseBase(p) === 'lightener');
    const totalDepth = deepenerPhases.length;

    // Phase-specific instructions (base kinds — expanded below for nested/numbered variants)
    const phaseInstructions = {
      settling: `Write the SETTLING phase (~${targetWords.settling} words). Orient the user. Open naturally — don't say "hello". Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY the script text.`,
      induction: `Write the INDUCTION phase (~${targetWords.induction} words). Move from awareness toward trance using ${method.name}. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`,
      wake: `Write the WAKE phase (~${targetWords.wake} words). Bring the user fully awake and alert. Use a distinct upward count or direct waking sequence. Re-alert clearly. Eyes open. Fully awake. This is the actual wake-up phase and must not be replaced by reintroduction. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`,
      reintroduction: `Write the REINTRODUCTION phase (~${targetWords.reintroduction} words). This phase happens AFTER wake. The user is already awake. Include a warm welcome-back, a suggestion to slowly get up only when ready, stretch, shake it off, and continue the day. If this is a demonstration method, the test can be mentioned after wake and before the final welcome-back, but the ending must fully reintroduce the user. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`,
    };

    // Deepener instructions — depth-aware. Each level takes the user one step deeper.
    // Total words for the deepener phase are divided across the nested deepeners.
    const deepenerWordsEach = totalDepth > 0 ? Math.round(targetWords.deepener / totalDepth) : targetWords.deepener;
    deepenerPhases.forEach((p, i) => {
      const depth = i + 1; // 1-based: first deepener = depth 1
      let intensity;
      if (totalDepth === 1) intensity = 'light-to-medium trance';
      else if (depth === 1) intensity = 'light trance (first layer)';
      else if (depth === totalDepth) intensity = 'deep trance (innermost layer)';
      else intensity = `medium trance (layer ${depth} of ${totalDepth})`;
      const note = `Write DEEPENER phase ${depth} of ${totalDepth} (~${deepenerWordsEach} words). Target state: ${intensity}. ${depth === 1 ? 'Move from post-induction awareness into the first layer of trance.' : `The user is already at layer ${depth - 1}; take them ONE LEVEL deeper, not all the way from waking.`}${state.craftedSuggestion && depth === totalDepth ? ' Foreshadow the crafted suggestion at this innermost layer.' : ''}${affirmLines.length && depth === totalDepth ? ' Begin weaving affirmations.' : ''} Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D. Output ONLY script text.`;
      phaseInstructions[p] = note;
    });

    // Lightener instructions — LIFO unwind. Phases appear in the order they'll play
    // (outermost-last), but each is paired with its deepener at the same depth.
    const lightenerWordsEach = lightenerPhases.length > 0 ? Math.round(targetWords.lightener / lightenerPhases.length) : targetWords.lightener;
    lightenerPhases.forEach((p, i) => {
      // lightener[0] pairs with the DEEPEST deepener (LIFO: innermost closes first).
      const closesDepth = lightenerPhases.length - i; // first lightener closes innermost
      const fromDepth = closesDepth;
      const toDepth = closesDepth - 1;
      const note = fromDepth === 1
        ? `Write the LIGHTENER phase (~${lightenerWordsEach} words). Ease intensity down gradually from light trance toward waking awareness. Keep the same narrator voice and continuity — this phase works with the narrator rather than stopping them. Use gentle return language, body awareness, orientation, breath, movement, and upward pacing. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`
        : `Write LIGHTENER phase for level ${fromDepth} → ${toDepth} (~${lightenerWordsEach} words). The user is currently at depth ${fromDepth}; bring them up ONE LEVEL toward depth ${toDepth}, not all the way. Subsequent lighteners will continue the ascent. Gentle upward language, breath, light. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`;
      phaseInstructions[p] = note;
    });

    // Work phase instructions — role-tagged by position for long sessions.
    const workCount = phases.filter(p => phaseBase(p) === 'work').length;
    const workWordsEach = workCount > 0 ? Math.round(targetWords.work / workCount) : targetWords.work;
    phases.forEach(p => {
      const base = phaseBase(p);
      if (base === 'affirm') {
        // Affirmation interlude — short, poetic, uses the user's exact words.
        // Follows its paired Work block per the default (Work, Affirm) structure.
        phaseInstructions[p] = `Write a brief affirmation interlude (~40-60 words). Deliver these affirmations in ${persona.name}'s voice, woven into flowing, hypnotic language:\n${affirmLines.map(l => `"${l}"`).join('\n')}\nUse the user's exact words. Add \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D between each. Poetic, rhythmic, repetitive. Output ONLY script text.`;
      } else if (base === 'work') {
        const workIdx = p.includes('-') ? parseInt(p.split('-')[1]) : 1;
        // Role assignment scales with workCount — prevents 10 blocks sounding identical.
        let role;
        if (workCount === 1) role = 'single-block: deliver and consolidate.';
        else if (workIdx === 1) role = state.craftedSuggestion ? 'INTRODUCE: deliver the crafted suggestion verbatim for the first time. Plant the seed.' : method.category === 'demonstration' ? 'INTRODUCE: begin building the demonstration effect.' : 'INTRODUCE: establish the core therapeutic theme.';
        else if (workIdx === workCount) role = state.craftedSuggestion ? 'CONSOLIDATE + FUTURE-PACE: final reinforcement at peak intensity. Project the effect forward in time.' : 'CONSOLIDATE: bring the work to its peak and anchor it for the future.';
        else if (workIdx === workCount - 1) role = state.craftedSuggestion ? 'PEAK: most intense reinforcement of the crafted suggestion. Highest suggestibility.' : 'PEAK: highest intensity — the crux of the work.';
        else {
          // Middle blocks — rotate through DEVELOP / INTENSIFY / REINFORCE
          const midRoles = ['DEVELOP: expand with a fresh metaphor you have not yet used.', 'INTENSIFY: deliver the suggestion at higher conviction and specificity.', 'REINFORCE: a different angle on the same core effect.'];
          role = midRoles[(workIdx - 2) % midRoles.length];
        }
        const note = `Write WORK phase ${workIdx} of ${workCount} (~${workWordsEach} words). ROLE: ${role}${state.craftedSuggestion ? '' : ' Therapeutic deepening tied to the intention.'} Do not repeat imagery or phrasing from earlier work blocks. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D. Output ONLY script text.`;
        phaseInstructions[p] = note;
      }
    });

    // Save gen state for retry access
    _genState = { phases, stateMask, phaseResults, phaseTimes, sharedContext, phaseInstructions, persona, method, genStartTime: Date.now(), priorSummary: '' };

    const retryPhase = async (idx) => {
      // Guard: need gen state to exist and no concurrent AI call in flight
      if (!_genState) return;
      if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('Please wait — another phase is still being generated.'); return; }
      const gs = _genState;
      const phaseId = gs.phases[idx];
      // Capture the current (original) phase text BEFORE regenerating so we can
      // offer a diff comparison after. Empty original = first-time
      // generation, no diff needed.
      const originalText = gs.phaseResults[phaseId] || '';
      _aiInProgress = true;
      gs.stateMask[idx] = 'streaming';
      renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
      try {
        const newText = await generateSinglePhase(gs, idx);
        // Only show diff if there was prior content to compare against
        let chosen = newText;
        if (originalText && originalText.trim() && originalText.trim() !== newText.trim()) {
          const pick = await showPhaseDiffModal(originalText, newText, getPhaseLabel(phaseId));
          chosen = pick === 'old' ? originalText : newText;
        }
        gs.phaseResults[phaseId] = chosen;
        gs.stateMask[idx] = 'done';
        renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
        assembleAndShowScript(gs);
        if (chosen === originalText) {
          notify.info(`Kept original "${getPhaseLabel(phaseId)}".`);
        } else {
          notify.success(`Phase "${getPhaseLabel(phaseId)}" regenerated successfully.`);
        }
      } catch (e) {
        gs.stateMask[idx] = 'error';
        renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
        notify.error(`Retry failed: ${e.message}. Click the red indicator to try again.`);
      } finally {
        _aiInProgress = false;
      }
    };

    // Show initial progress
    renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, `Estimated: ~${phases.length * 60}s remaining`, retryPhase);
    const genStartTime = Date.now();
    const stopTimer = makeElapsedTimer(s => {
      const avgTime = phaseTimes.length > 0 ? phaseTimes.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / phaseTimes.length : 60;
      const remSec = Math.max(0, Math.round(avgTime * (phases.length - phaseTimes.length)));
      $('genEta').textContent = `${s}s elapsed · ~${remSec}s remaining`;
    });

    try {
      let priorSummary = '';

      for (let i = 0; i < phases.length; i++) {
        const phase = phases[i];
        const phaseStart = Date.now();
        stateMask[i] = 'streaming';
        renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, null, retryPhase);

        try {
          const result = await generateSinglePhase(_genState, i);
          phaseResults[phase] = result;
          priorSummary += `\n${phase.toUpperCase()}: ${result.length > 200 ? result.substring(0, 150).replace(/\x5BPAUSE \d+\]/g, '') + '...' : result.replace(/\x5BPAUSE \d+\]/g, '')}`;
          _genState.priorSummary = priorSummary;
          stateMask[i] = 'done';
          phaseTimes.push((Date.now() - phaseStart) / 1000);
        } catch (e) {
          console.error(`Phase "${phase}" failed:`, e);
          if (e.message.includes('AI') || e.message.includes('error') || e.message.includes('failed')) {
            stateMask[i] = 'error';
            notify.error(`"${phase}" failed: ${e.message}. Click the red indicator to retry.`);
          } else {
            stateMask[i] = 'warn';
            notify.warn(`"${phase}" had an issue: ${e.message}. Click the yellow indicator to retry.`);
          }
          // Continue to next phase — partial script is better than nothing
          phaseTimes.push(60); // estimate for ETA
        }
        renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, null, retryPhase);
      }

      assembleAndShowScript(_genState);
      const totalTime = Math.round((Date.now() - genStartTime) / 1000);
      const failures = stateMask.filter(s => s === 'error' || s === 'warn').length;
      if (failures > 0) {
        notify.warn(`Script generated in ${totalTime}s with ${failures} phase(s) needing retry. Click indicators to fix.`);
      } else {
        notify.success(`Script generated in ${totalTime}s — ${phases.length} phases complete.`);
      }

    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
      notify.error('Script generation failed: ' + e.message);
    } finally {
      _aiInProgress = false;
      stopTimer();
      setLoading('generateScriptBtn', false, 'generate full script');
      setLoading('regenScriptBtn', false);
      if (scriptBuildProgress) scriptBuildProgress.style.display = 'none';
      // Hide streaming preview once generation completes
      setStreamingPreview('', '', { hide: true });
    }
  }

  /** Generate a single phase via aiTextPlugin */
  async function generateSinglePhase(gs, idx) {
    const phase = gs.phases[idx];
    const phaseLabel = getPhaseLabel(phase);
    const summaryBlock = gs.priorSummary ? `\n\nSO FAR (summary — continue seamlessly, DO NOT repeat):\n${gs.priorSummary}` : '';
    const taskBlock = `\n\n═══ YOUR TASK ═══\n${gs.phaseInstructions[phase]}\n\nStay in ${gs.persona.name}'s voice. Continue naturally. No ===PHASE=== markers. Start immediately:`;

    // Token budget — drop the prior-summary block first if we're over budget.
    // The sharedContext + task block are priority 5 (never trimmed).
    const finalInstruction = trimToTokenBudget([
      { name: 'sharedContext', text: gs.sharedContext, priority: 5 },
      { name: 'priorSummary',  text: summaryBlock,     priority: 1 },
      { name: 'taskBlock',     text: taskBlock,        priority: 5 },
    ], 900);

    // Streaming — render text as it arrives so users see progress
    // within ~1s instead of waiting ~30-60s for the full phase.
    let accumulated = '';
    const onChunk = (data) => {
      if (data.isFromStartWith) return;
      const chunk = data.textChunk || '';
      if (!chunk) return;
      accumulated += chunk;
      setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, accumulated);
    };

    let data;
    try {
      // Perchance ai-text-plugin returns a thenable that resolves when done.
      // Providing onChunk enables streaming — it's ignored if unsupported.
      const streamObj = root.aiTextPlugin({
        instruction: finalInstruction,
        stopSequences: ['\n\n\n\n'],
        hideStartWith: true,
        onChunk,
      });
      data = await streamObj;
    } catch (e) {
      setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, accumulated, { done: true });
      throw new Error('AI call threw: ' + (e?.message || e));
    }

    // explicit error-before-text check
    if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') {
      setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, accumulated, { done: true });
      throw new Error('AI returned an error');
    }

    let raw = (data.generatedText || accumulated || '').trim();
    let text = stripLeadingPhaseHeader(raw, phase);
    if ((!text || text.length < 15) && raw) {
      text = raw
        .replace(PHASE_MARKER_STRIP_RX, ' ')
        .replace(/^(?:[#>*-]+\s*)?(?:phase\s*[:\-]\s*)?[a-z][a-z0-9\s\-]{1,40}:?\s*/i, '')
        .trim();
    }
    setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, text, { done: true });
    if (!text || text.length < 15) throw new Error('Phase returned too little text');
    return text;
  }

  /** Assemble all completed phases into a full script */
  function assembleAndShowScript(gs) {
    let fullScript = '';
    gs.phases.forEach(p => {
      if (!gs.phaseResults[p]) return;
      fullScript += `===${phaseIdToMarker(p)}===
${gs.phaseResults[p]}

`;
    });
    if (fullScript.trim().length > 50) {
      state.fullScript = fullScript.trim();
      state.generatedPhaseOrder = [...gs.phases];
      state.parsedScript = parseScript(state.fullScript);
      showScript();
      updateStepUI();
    }
  }

  function parseScript(text) {
    const phases = {};
    const ordered = [];
    const matches = [...text.matchAll(PHASE_MARKER_CAPTURE_RX)];
    if (!matches.length) return { ...phases, ordered: [] };
    for (let i = 0; i < matches.length; i++) {
      const marker = matches[i][1];
      const phaseId = markerToPhaseId(marker);
      const start = matches[i].index + matches[i][0].length;
      const end = i + 1 < matches.length ? matches[i + 1].index : text.length;
      const body = text.substring(start, end).trim();
      phases[phaseId] = body;
      ordered.push(phaseId);
      if (phaseId.startsWith('work')) phases.work = [phases.work, body].filter(Boolean).join('\n\n');
    }
    phases.ordered = ordered;
    return phases;
  }

  function getScriptMetrics(text) {
    const full = String(text || '');
    const spokenOnly = stripAllPhaseMarkers(full)
      .replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D/gi, ' ');
    const words = spokenOnly.split(/\s+/).filter(w => w.length > 0).length;
    const pauses = (full.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D/gi) || []).length;
    const pauseSecs = (full.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/gi) || []).reduce((sum, m) => sum + parseInt(m.match(/\d+/)[0], 10), 0);
    const parsed = parseScript(full);
    const phaseCount = (parsed.ordered || []).length;
    const workBlocks = (parsed.ordered || []).filter(p => p.startsWith('work')).length;
    const affirmBlocks = (parsed.ordered || []).filter(p => p.startsWith('affirm')).length;
    const estimatedMin = Math.round(words / 50 + pauseSecs / 60);
    return { words, pauses, pauseSecs, phaseCount, workBlocks, affirmBlocks, estimatedMin, ordered: parsed.ordered || [] };
  }

  function normalizePhaseSections(sections) {
    const cleaned = (sections || []).filter(s => s && s.text && s.text.trim()).map(s => ({ ...s, text: s.text.trim() }));
    let workIdx = 0;
    let affirmIdx = 0;
    return cleaned.map(section => {
      const base = String(section.phaseId || 'work').replace(/-\d+$/, '');
      if (base === 'work') {
        workIdx += 1;
        section.phaseId = `work-${workIdx}`;
      } else if (base === 'affirm') {
        affirmIdx += 1;
        section.phaseId = `affirm-${affirmIdx}`;
      } else {
        section.phaseId = base;
      }
      return section;
    });
  }

  function getScriptSectionsFromState() {
    const ordered = state.parsedScript?.ordered?.length ? state.parsedScript.ordered : getPlaybackPhaseOrder();
    return ordered.map(phaseId => ({ phaseId, text: state.parsedScript?.[phaseId] || '' })).filter(s => s.text && s.text.trim());
  }

  function getSpokenScriptPreviewText() {
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    return sections.map(s => stripLeadingPhaseHeader(s.text, s.phaseId).trim()).filter(Boolean).join('\n\n');
  }

  function setScriptFromSections(sections, opts = {}) {
    const cleaned = normalizePhaseSections(sections);
    state.scriptSections = cleaned.map(s => ({ ...s }));
    state.generatedPhaseOrder = cleaned.map(s => s.phaseId);
    state.fullScript = cleaned.map(s => `===${phaseIdToMarker(s.phaseId)}===
${s.text.trim()}`).join('\n\n').trim();
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(state.fullScript);
    if (!opts.skipRender) showScript();
    updateStepUI();
  }

  /**
   * For a given sections list, assign a `pairGroup` and `depth` to each phase.
   * - pairGroup: 'trance' | 'depth' | null — drives editor color coding.
   * - depth: integer (1-based) for deepener/lightener nesting — how deep this
   *   pair is nested. Deepeners number outward-to-inward; their matched
   *   Lighteners mirror that (LIFO — innermost unwinds first).
   * Returns an array of { pairGroup, depth } parallel to sections.
   */
  function computePairMetadata(sections) {
    // Walk forward: every Deepener pushes a depth level.
    // Walk lighteners in reverse order to pair them up with the deepest unclosed deepener.
    const deepenerStack = []; // each entry is {idx, depth}
    const meta = sections.map(() => ({ pairGroup: null, depth: null }));
    let curDepth = 0;
    sections.forEach((s, i) => {
      const base = phaseBase(s.phaseId);
      if (base === 'deepener') {
        curDepth++;
        deepenerStack.push({ idx: i, depth: curDepth });
        meta[i] = { pairGroup: 'depth', depth: curDepth };
      } else if (base === 'lightener') {
        // Pair with the most-recently-added unclosed deepener (LIFO).
        const pair = deepenerStack.pop();
        const depth = pair ? pair.depth : 1;
        meta[i] = { pairGroup: 'depth', depth };
        if (curDepth > 0) curDepth--;
      } else if (base === 'induction' || base === 'wake' || base === 'reintroduction') {
        meta[i] = { pairGroup: 'trance', depth: null };
      }
    });
    return meta;
  }

  function renderPhaseEditor() {
    const panel = $('phaseEditorPanel');
    const list = $('phaseEditorList');
    if (!panel || !list) return;
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    state.scriptSections = sections;
    if (!sections.length) {
      panel.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }
    panel.style.display = 'block';
    const meta = computePairMetadata(sections);
    list.innerHTML = sections.map((s, i) => {
      const m = meta[i];
      const rowClass = 'toggle-row phase-editor-row' + (m.pairGroup ? ' pair-' + m.pairGroup : '');
      const depthAttr = m.depth ? ` data-depth="${m.depth}"` : '';
      const tag = m.pairGroup === 'trance'
        ? '<span class="phase-pair-tag tag-trance" title="Induction ↔ Wake / Reintroduction">↕ trance</span>'
        : m.pairGroup === 'depth'
          ? `<span class="phase-pair-tag tag-depth" title="Deepener ↔ Lightener (level ${m.depth})">↕ depth ${m.depth}</span>`
          : '';
      const preview = escapeHtml((s.text || '').replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D/gi, ' ').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim().slice(0, 100) || 'empty');
      return `
      <div class="${rowClass}" data-phase-idx="${i}"${depthAttr} style="align-items:flex-start;">
        <div style="flex:1; min-width:0;">
          <label>${escapeHtml(getPhaseLabel(s.phaseId))}${tag}<span class="hint">${preview}</span></label>
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(3, minmax(72px, auto)); gap:6px; margin-left:8px;">
          <button class="preview-btn phase-up" data-idx="${i}" ${i === 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>↑</button>
          <button class="preview-btn phase-down" data-idx="${i}" ${i === sections.length - 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>↓</button>
          <button class="preview-btn phase-remove" data-idx="${i}">remove</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-up').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => movePhaseSection(parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10), -1)));
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-down').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => movePhaseSection(parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10), 1)));
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-remove').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => removePhaseSection(parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10))));
    // Pair-highlighting: hovering a paired phase highlights its partner(s).
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-editor-row').forEach((row, i) => {
      const m = meta[i];
      if (!m.pairGroup) return;
      row.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
        list.querySelectorAll('.phase-editor-row').forEach((other, j) => {
          if (j === i) return;
          const om = meta[j];
          if (m.pairGroup === 'trance' && om.pairGroup === 'trance') other.classList.add('highlight-pair');
          else if (m.pairGroup === 'depth' && om.pairGroup === 'depth' && om.depth === m.depth) other.classList.add('highlight-pair');
        });
      });
      row.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
        list.querySelectorAll('.phase-editor-row').forEach(r => r.classList.remove('highlight-pair'));
      });
    });
  }

  function movePhaseSection(idx, delta) {
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    const j = idx + delta;
    if (j < 0 || j >= sections.length) return;
    [sections[idx], sections[j]] = [sections[j], sections[idx]];
    setScriptFromSections(sections);
  }

  /**
   * Remove a phase, with pair-aware cascade:
   *  - Removing an Induction prompts to also remove Wake + Reintroduction (and any trailing trance-cycle partners).
   *  - Removing a Deepener auto-removes its paired Lightener (LIFO — the one that would close this depth level).
