   *  - Removing a Lightener auto-removes its paired Deepener (preserves structural integrity).
   * User confirmation is requested when multiple phases will be removed.
   */
  async function removePhaseSection(idx) {
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    if (idx < 0 || idx >= sections.length) return;
    const target = sections[idx];
    const base = phaseBase(target.phaseId);

    // Indexes of partners to remove alongside the primary target.
    const partnerIndexes = [];

    if (base === 'induction') {
      // Remove this induction PLUS any remaining wake + reintroduction (the Emergence pair).
      sections.forEach((s, i) => {
        if (i === idx) return;
        const b = phaseBase(s.phaseId);
        if (b === 'wake' || b === 'reintroduction') partnerIndexes.push(i);
      });
    } else if (base === 'deepener') {
      // Find the matching Lightener for THIS deepener using LIFO pairing.
      const meta = computePairMetadata(sections);
      const targetDepth = meta[idx]?.depth;
      if (targetDepth != null) {
        // Walk forward from idx: the first Lightener at this depth is the partner.
        for (let k = idx + 1; k < sections.length; k++) {
          if (meta[k].pairGroup === 'depth' && phaseBase(sections[k].phaseId) === 'lightener' && meta[k].depth === targetDepth) {
            partnerIndexes.push(k);
            break;
          }
        }
      }
    } else if (base === 'lightener') {
      // Remove the paired Deepener for this Lightener.
      const meta = computePairMetadata(sections);
      const targetDepth = meta[idx]?.depth;
      if (targetDepth != null) {
        // Walk BACK from idx: find the matching deepener at same depth.
        for (let k = idx - 1; k >= 0; k--) {
          if (meta[k].pairGroup === 'depth' && phaseBase(sections[k].phaseId) === 'deepener' && meta[k].depth === targetDepth) {
            partnerIndexes.push(k);
            break;
          }
        }
      }
    } else if (base === 'wake') {
      // Removing Wake alone is structurally incomplete — prompt to also remove Reintroduction.
      const reintroIdx = sections.findIndex(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'reintroduction');
      if (reintroIdx >= 0 && reintroIdx !== idx) {
        const also = await confirmAsync('Also remove Reintroduction? Reintroduction without Wake leaves the user mid-emergence.', { okText: 'remove both', cancelText: 'only wake' });
        if (also) partnerIndexes.push(reintroIdx);
      }
    }

    const toRemove = [idx, ...partnerIndexes];
    if (toRemove.length > 1) {
      const names = toRemove.map(i => getPhaseLabel(sections[i].phaseId)).join(', ');
      const ok = await confirmAsync(`Remove ${toRemove.length} paired phases: ${names}?\n\nPhases in a pair should be kept together for safe session structure.`, { okText: 'remove all', cancelText: 'cancel' });
      if (!ok) return;
    }

    // Remove in descending index order so splicing doesn't shift later indexes.
    toRemove.sort((a, b) => b - a).forEach(i => sections.splice(i, 1));
    setScriptFromSections(sections);
    if (partnerIndexes.length > 0) notify.info(`Removed ${toRemove.length} paired phases.`);
  }

  /**
   * Scaffold text for a new phase. Depth-aware for nested deepener/lightener.
   */
  function scaffoldForPhase(phaseId, depth = 1) {
    if (phaseId === 'settling') return 'Find a comfortable position. Let the day settle. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseId === 'induction') return 'Begin the induction here. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseId === 'deepener' || phaseBase(phaseId) === 'deepener') {
      if (depth <= 1) return 'Deepen the state. Each breath takes you further. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      if (depth === 2) return 'Now deeper still — another level down. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      if (depth === 3) return 'Deeper, and deeper yet. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      return `Descend another level — level ${depth}. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D`;
    }
    if (phaseId === 'lightener' || phaseBase(phaseId) === 'lightener') {
      if (depth <= 1) return 'Begin easing intensity down. Notice the room. Notice the body. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      return `Come back up one level — from depth ${depth} toward ${depth - 1}. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D`;
    }
    if (phaseBase(phaseId) === 'work') return 'Continue the work here. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseBase(phaseId) === 'affirm') return 'Return to the user\'s affirmations here. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseId === 'wake') return 'In a moment, coming all the way back now. Five, returning. Four, breathing deeper. Three, energy returning. Two, eyes beginning to open. One, fully awake and alert. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseId === 'reintroduction') return 'Welcome back. When you feel ready, slowly get up. Stretch. Shake it off. Go about your day. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    return 'New phase text. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
  }

  /**
   * Add a new phase to the session. Pair-aware:
   *  - Adding an Induction auto-adds Wake + Reintroduction if missing (unless sleep intention).
   *  - Adding a Deepener auto-adds a paired Lightener in the LIFO unwind slot.
   *  - Work and Affirm are naked additions (no pair).
   *  - Lightener, Wake, Reintroduction can be added naked (for repair of an incomplete session).
   */
  function addPhaseSection(phaseId) {
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    const base = phaseBase(phaseId);
    const added = [];

    /** Build a uniquely-IDed section for a given base kind. */
    const buildSection = (kind, opts = {}) => {
      const existingCount = countPhaseBase(sections.concat(added), kind);
      let id = kind;
      // Numbered IDs for anything that can legitimately appear multiple times
      if (['work', 'affirm', 'deepener', 'lightener'].includes(kind)) {
        const nextN = existingCount + 1;
        id = nextN > 1 ? `${kind}-${nextN}` : kind;
        // Rename the first occurrence to `${kind}-1` for consistency once we have 2+.
        // Done after insertion below.
      }
      return { phaseId: id, text: scaffoldForPhase(id, opts.depth || existingCount + 1) };
    };

    /** Insert a section at the correct canonical position, then register it. */
    const insertSection = (section) => {
      const insertIdx = findPhaseInsertionIdx(sections, phaseBase(section.phaseId));
      sections.splice(insertIdx, 0, section);
      added.push(section);
    };

    // Pair logic — also queues partners in canonical positions.
    if (base === 'induction') {
      // Multi-induction sessions (fractionation) aren't fully modeled yet — guard.
      if (countPhaseBase(sections, 'induction') > 0) {
        notify.warn('This session already has an Induction. Fractionation (multi-induction cycles) is not yet supported — add a Deepener for deeper trance within the current cycle, or remove the existing Induction first.');
        return;
      }
      insertSection(buildSection('induction'));
      if (state.intentionType !== 'sleep') {
        const hasWake = countPhaseBase(sections, 'wake') > 0;
        const hasReintro = countPhaseBase(sections, 'reintroduction') > 0;
        if (!hasWake) insertSection(buildSection('wake'));
        if (!hasReintro) insertSection(buildSection('reintroduction'));
      }
    } else if (base === 'deepener') {
      // Nesting — each call adds one deepener + one lightener (paired).
      const depthBefore = countPhaseBase(sections, 'deepener');
      const depth = depthBefore + 1;
      insertSection({ phaseId: depth > 1 ? `deepener-${depth}` : 'deepener', text: scaffoldForPhase('deepener', depth) });
      insertSection({ phaseId: depth > 1 ? `lightener-${depth}` : 'lightener', text: scaffoldForPhase('lightener', depth) });
    } else if (base === 'settling' || base === 'wake' || base === 'reintroduction') {
      // Naked (repair) additions.
      if (countPhaseBase(sections, base) === 0) insertSection(buildSection(base));
      else notify.info(`${getPhaseLabel(base)} already exists — skipping.`);
    } else if (base === 'lightener') {
      // Naked lightener add (for repair when the paired deepener exists unpaired).
      insertSection(buildSection('lightener'));
    } else if (base === 'work' || base === 'affirm') {
      insertSection(buildSection(base));
    } else {
      insertSection({ phaseId: base, text: scaffoldForPhase(base) });
    }

    // Normalize IDs: if we now have 2+ of a kind where the first was unnumbered,
    // promote it to `-1` so downstream code sees consistent numbering.
    ['work', 'affirm', 'deepener', 'lightener'].forEach(kind => {
      const indexes = sections.map((s, i) => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === kind ? i : -1).filter(i => i >= 0);
      if (indexes.length >= 2) {
        indexes.forEach((sectionIdx, n) => {
          sections[sectionIdx] = { ...sections[sectionIdx], phaseId: `${kind}-${n + 1}` };
        });
      }
    });

    setScriptFromSections(sections);
    if (added.length > 1) {
      const labels = added.map(s => getPhaseLabel(s.phaseId)).join(' + ');
      notify.info(`Added paired phases: ${labels}`);
    }
  }

  function resetPhaseOrderToDefault() {
    if (!state.fullScript) return;
    state.generatedPhaseOrder = getPhaseList();
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(state.fullScript);
    const sections = [];
    const used = new Set();
    for (const phaseId of state.generatedPhaseOrder) {
      if (state.parsedScript[phaseId]) {
        sections.push({ phaseId, text: state.parsedScript[phaseId] });
        used.add(phaseId);
      }
    }
    for (const phaseId of state.parsedScript.ordered || []) {
      if (!used.has(phaseId)) sections.push({ phaseId, text: state.parsedScript[phaseId] });
    }
    setScriptFromSections(sections);
  }

  function showScript() {
    _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
    if (!state.fullScript) { $('scriptStats').innerHTML = 'No script loaded.'; $('scriptPreview').classList.add('visible'); renderPhaseEditor(); return; }
    $('scriptText').value = state.fullScript;
    const metrics = getScriptMetrics(state.fullScript);
    $('scriptStats').innerHTML = `<strong>${metrics.words}</strong> words · <strong>${metrics.pauses}</strong> pauses (${metrics.pauseSecs}s) · <strong>${metrics.phaseCount}</strong> phases · <strong>${metrics.workBlocks}</strong> work block${metrics.workBlocks === 1 ? '' : 's'} · estimated: <strong>${metrics.estimatedMin} min</strong><br>Phase header lines are internal structure markers. Spoken content is preserved below them.`;
    $('scriptPreview').classList.add('visible');
    renderPhaseEditor();
  }
  function hideScript() { state.fullScript = null; state.parsedScript = null; state.generatedPhaseOrder = []; state.scriptSections = []; $('scriptPreview').classList.remove('visible'); renderPhaseEditor(); updateStepUI(); }

  // ====================================================================
  // SCRIPT TIMING FIXER — recalculates \x5BPAUSE N\x5D markers heuristically
  // ====================================================================
  let _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;

  /** Detect directive phrases that need longer pauses after them */
  const DIRECTIVE_RX = /\b(focus|notice|feel|imagine|relax|breathe|let|allow|sense|listen|watch|follow|deepen|drift|sink|melt|soften|release|surrender|drop|sleep|close|open|rest|calm|trust|safe|deeper|down|slowly|gently|carefully|now|picture|visualize|float)\b/i;
  const ELLIPSIS_RX = /\.{2,}|…/;

  /**
   * Fix \x5BPAUSE N\x5D timings in a script based on content heuristics.
   * - Removes existing pauses and recalculates
   * - Breaks sentences >30 words at clause boundaries
   * - Combines fragments <3 words with adjacent sentences
   * - Inserts pauses based on content type and length
   */
  function fixScriptTimings(scriptText) {
    const phaseRx = PHASE_MARKER_SPLIT_RX;

    // Compute pause duration based on sentence content
    function pauseFor(sentence) {
      const words = sentence.split(/\s+/).length;
      const isDirective = DIRECTIVE_RX.test(sentence);
      const hasEllipsis = ELLIPSIS_RX.test(sentence);
      const isQuestion = sentence.endsWith('?');
      // Directives: hold for the suggestion to land
      if (isDirective && words <= 8) return 5;
      if (isDirective) return Math.min(6, 4 + Math.floor(words / 10));
      // Ellipsis / questions: moderate + scale
      if (hasEllipsis) return Math.min(5, 3 + Math.floor(words / 10));
      if (isQuestion) return Math.min(5, 3 + Math.floor(words / 8));
      // Everything else: scale with sentence length
      // 1-4w → 2s, 5-9w → 3s, 10-14w → 4s, 15+w → 5s
      return Math.min(5, 2 + Math.floor(words / 5));
    }

    // Process a text segment (no existing pauses inside it)
    function processSegment(text) {
      // Strip bracket annotations that aren't \x5BPAUSE N\x5D (e.g. [Topic Sentence], [Step 1])
      const clean = text
        .replace(/^#+\s+.*$/gm, '') // strip markdown headings
        .replace(/\[[^\]]+\]/g, m =>
          /^\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]$/i.test(m) ? m : ''
        ).replace(/  +/g, ' ').trim();
      if (!clean) return '';

      // Split into sentences at . ! ?
      let sentences = clean.split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+/).filter(s => s.trim().length > 0);

      // Break sentences over 30 words at clause boundaries
      const broken = [];
      for (const sent of sentences) {
        if (sent.split(/\s+/).length > 30) {
          const clauses = sent.split(/(?<=[;—–])\s+|(?<=,)\s+(?=\w)/);
          let buf = '';
          for (const cl of clauses) {
            const combined = buf ? buf + ' ' + cl : cl;
            // Only split if BOTH sides are substantial (≥ 4 words each)
            if (combined.split(/\s+/).length > 22 && buf && buf.split(/\s+/).length >= 4) {
              broken.push(buf.trim()); buf = cl;
            } else buf = combined;
          }
          if (buf.trim()) broken.push(buf.trim());
        } else broken.push(sent);
      }
      sentences = broken;
      if (!sentences.length) return clean;

      // Build output: sentence \x5BPAUSE N\x5D sentence \x5BPAUSE N\x5D ... sentence
      const out = [sentences[0]];
      for (let i = 1; i < sentences.length; i++) {
        out.push(`\x5BPAUSE ${pauseFor(sentences[i - 1])}\x5D`);
        out.push(sentences[i]);
      }
      return out.join(' ');
    }

    // Split by phase markers, process each non-marker section
    const phaseParts = scriptText.split(phaseRx);
    const isMarker = /===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===/i; // non-global for safe .test()
    const processed = phaseParts.map(part => {
      if (isMarker.test(part)) return part;
      // Split by existing \x5BPAUSE N\x5D — preserve author pauses as boundaries
      const chunks = part.split(/(\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\])/gi);
      return chunks.map(chunk =>
        /\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/i.test(chunk) ? chunk : processSegment(chunk)
      ).join(' ');
    });

    let fixed = processed.join('\n').replace(/  +/g, ' ');

    // Monotone detector: if all computed pauses are the same value
    // (no directive words triggered variance), apply jittered timing
    const pauses = (fixed.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/gi) || []).map(p => parseInt(p.match(/\d+/)[0], 10));
    const unique = new Set(pauses);
    if (pauses.length > 4 && unique.size === 1) {
      fixed = fixed.replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, () => {
        const jitter = Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) - 1; // -1 to +2
        return `\x5BPAUSE ${Math.max(2, 3 + jitter)}\x5D`;
      });
    }

    // Normalize all pause marker casing to canonical form
    fixed = fixed.replace(/\x5Bpause\s+(\d+)\x5D/gi, (m, n) => `\x5BPAUSE ${n}\x5D`);

    return fixed;
  }

  /** Show/hide the fix timings button based on edit state */

  // ====================================================================
  // SESSION HISTORY & STATS
  // ====================================================================
  async function renderSessionHistory() {
    const panel = $('sessionStatsPanel');
    const list = $('sessionHistoryList');
    if (!panel || !list) return;

    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    if (history.length === 0) {
      panel.innerHTML = '';
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="library-empty">no sessions yet — complete a session to see stats</div>';
      return;
    }

    // Panel cleared — stats are shown in sidebarStats, sparkline appends here
    panel.innerHTML = '';

    // Recent sessions list (last 20)
    list.innerHTML = '';
    history.slice(0, 20).forEach((s, idx) => {
      const d = new Date(s.date);
      const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
      const timeStr = d.toLocaleTimeString(undefined, { hour: 'numeric', minute: '2-digit' });
      const mins = Math.round((s.durationSec || 0) / 60);
      const hasScript = !!(s.script && s.script.length > 20);
      const status = s.completed ? `${mins}m` : `${mins}m · inc`;
      const metrics = s.metrics || getScriptMetrics(s.script || '');
      const phaseCount = Array.isArray(s.phaseOrder) ? s.phaseOrder.length : metrics.phaseCount;
      const workBlocks = s.workBlockCount || metrics.workBlocks || 0;
      const profileName = s.profileSnapshot?.name || s.profileName || '';
      const affirmMode = s.affirmationMode || '';

      // Script preview — first ~150 chars, strip markers
      let preview = '';
      if (hasScript) {
        const cleaned = s.script.replace(PHASE_MARKER_STRIP_RX, '').replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, '').trim();
        preview = cleaned.substring(0, 150).replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
        if (cleaned.length > 150) preview += '…';
      }

      const item = document.createElement('div');
      item.className = 'history-item';
      item.innerHTML = `
        <div class="h-title">${dateStr} ${timeStr} · ${status}</div>
        <div class="h-meta">${escapeHtml(s.guide || '—')} · ${escapeHtml(s.method || '—')} · ${phaseCount} phases · ${workBlocks} work block${workBlocks === 1 ? '' : 's'}${affirmMode ? ' · ' + escapeHtml(affirmMode) : ''}${profileName ? ' · ' + escapeHtml(profileName) : ''}${s.intentionText ? ' · ' + escapeHtml(s.intentionText.substring(0, 30)) : ''}</div>
        ${preview ? `<div class="h-preview">${escapeHtml(preview)}</div>` : '<div class="h-no-script">no script stored</div>'}
        <div class="h-actions">
          <button class="h-btn h-play" data-idx="${idx}" title="Replay session" ${hasScript ? '' : 'disabled'}>▶</button>
          <button class="h-btn h-edit" data-idx="${idx}" title="Edit script" ${hasScript ? '' : 'disabled'}>✎</button>
          <button class="h-btn h-delete" data-idx="${idx}" title="Delete">✕</button>
        </div>`;
      list.appendChild(item);
    });

    // Wire play buttons
    list.querySelectorAll('.h-play').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async e => {
        const idx = parseInt(e.target.closest('.h-btn').dataset.idx, 10);
        const entry = history[idx];
        if (!entry?.script) { notify.warn('No script stored for this session.'); return; }
        replayFromHistory(entry);
      });
    });

    // Wire edit buttons — load script into editor without starting session
    list.querySelectorAll('.h-edit').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async e => {
        const idx = parseInt(e.target.closest('.h-btn').dataset.idx, 10);
        const entry = history[idx];
        if (!entry?.script) { notify.warn('No script stored for this session.'); return; }
        editFromHistory(entry);
      });
    });

    // Wire delete buttons
    list.querySelectorAll('.h-delete').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async e => {
        const idx = parseInt(e.target.closest('.h-btn').dataset.idx, 10);
        if (!await confirmAsync('Are you sure you want to delete this session?\n\nThis can\'t be undone.')) return;
        const h = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
        h.splice(idx, 1);
        await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', h);
        await rebuildAnalytics(h);
        renderSessionHistory();
        renderSidebarStats();
        renderHeatmap();
        renderSparkline();
        notify.info('Session deleted.');
      });
    });
  }

  /** Replay a session from history — restores all settings and script */
  function _restoreFromEntry(entry) {
    entry = normalizeHistoryEntry(entry);
    if (entry.personaId) state.selectedPersonaId = entry.personaId;
    if (entry.methodId) state.selectedMethodId = entry.methodId;
    if (entry.intention) { state.intentionType = entry.intention; const el = $('intentionType'); if (el) el.value = entry.intention; }
    if (entry.length) { state.length = entry.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.length; }
    if (entry.soundscape) { state.soundscape = entry.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = entry.soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.soundscape; }
    if (entry.speechRate != null) { state.speechRate = entry.speechRate; const el = $('speechRate'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(entry.speechRate * 100); }
    if (entry.voicePitch != null) state.voicePitch = entry.voicePitch;
    if (entry.voiceVolume != null) state.voiceVolume = entry.voiceVolume;
    if (entry.droneVolume != null) state.droneVolume = entry.droneVolume;
    if (entry.vizOverride) { state.vizOverride = entry.vizOverride; const el = $('vizSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.vizOverride; }
    if (entry.vizSettings) state.vizSettings = { ...state.vizSettings, ...entry.vizSettings };
    if (entry.duckingEnabled != null) { state.duckingEnabled = entry.duckingEnabled; const el = $('duckingToggle'); if (el) el.checked = entry.duckingEnabled; }
    if (entry.intentionText) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = entry.intentionText; }
    if (entry.userAffirmations != null) { const el = $('userAffirmations'); if (el) el.value = entry.userAffirmations; }
    if (entry.affirmationMode) { state.affirmationMode = entry.affirmationMode; const el = $('affirmationMode'); if (el) el.value = entry.affirmationMode; }
    if (entry.voiceName) state._savedVoiceName = entry.voiceName;
    applySavedVoiceSelection(); updateVoiceInfo();
    if (entry.profileSnapshot) applyProfileToForm(entry.profileSnapshot);
    state.fullScript = entry.script || '';
    state.parsedScript = entry.script ? parseScript(entry.script) : { ordered: [] };
    state.generatedPhaseOrder = entry.phaseOrder || state.parsedScript?.ordered || [];
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: true, 5: true, 6: false };
    renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
    updateIntentionHint(); showScript();
    return entry;
  }

  function replayFromHistory(entry) {
    entry = _restoreFromEntry(entry);
    state.currentStep = 6; updateStepUI(); switchScreen('setup-wizard'); goToStep(6);
    $('sidebar')?.classList.remove('open'); $('sidebarOverlay')?.classList.remove('open');
    notify.success(`Session from ${new Date(entry.date).toLocaleDateString()} loaded — ready to replay.`);
  }

  function editFromHistory(entry) {
    entry = _restoreFromEntry(entry);
    showEl('generateScriptBtn', true);
    state.currentStep = 6; updateStepUI(); switchScreen('setup-wizard'); goToStep(6);
    $('sidebar')?.classList.remove('open'); $('sidebarOverlay')?.classList.remove('open');
    setTimeout(() => $('scriptText')?.focus(), 300);
    notify.info(`Script loaded for editing. Modify and press Begin when ready.`);
  }

  /** Populate sidebar stats and streak from session history */
  async function renderSidebarStats() {
    const statsEl = $('sidebarStats');
    const streakEl = $('sidebarStreak');
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    const analytics = await getAnalytics();

    // Use analytics for all-time aggregates (never decremented by deletions)
    const totalSessions = Math.max(analytics.comp.total, history.length);
    const totalMinutes = analytics.dur.n > 0
      ? Math.round(analytics.dur.sum / 60)
      : Math.round(history.reduce((sum, s) => sum + (s.durationSec || 0), 0) / 60);
    const completionPct = analytics.comp.total > 0
      ? Math.round(analytics.comp.finished / analytics.comp.total * 100)
      : (history.length > 0 ? Math.round(history.filter(s => s.completed).length / history.length * 100) : 0);

    if (totalSessions === 0) {
      if (statsEl) statsEl.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:var(--text-faint);">No sessions yet</div>';
      if (streakEl) streakEl.textContent = 'New practitioner';
      return;
    }

    // Streak calculated from history dates (temporal — reflects current record)
    const today = new Date(); today.setHours(0,0,0,0);
    const dayMs = 86400000;
    const sessionDays = [...new Set(history.map(s => { const d = new Date(s.date); d.setHours(0,0,0,0); return d.getTime(); }))].sort((a,b) => b - a);
    let streak = 0, freezesUsed = 0, checkDay = today.getTime();
    for (const day of sessionDays) {
      const gap = (checkDay - day) / dayMs;
      if (gap <= 1) { streak++; checkDay = day; }
      else if (gap === 2 && freezesUsed < 2) { streak++; freezesUsed++; checkDay = day; }
      else break;
    }
    if (streakEl) streakEl.textContent = streak > 0 ? `${streak}-day streak` : `${totalSessions} sessions`;

    if (statsEl) {
      let html = `
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Sessions</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${totalSessions}</span></div>
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Minutes</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${totalMinutes}</span></div>
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Streak</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${streak} days</span></div>
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Completion</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${completionPct}%</span></div>`;

      // Analytics insights (after 2+ tracked sessions)
      if (analytics.comp.total >= 2) {
        try {
          const ins = deriveInsights(analytics);
          const hourLabel = ins.peakHour < 12 ? `${ins.peakHour || 12}am` : `${ins.peakHour === 12 ? 12 : ins.peakHour - 12}pm`;
          html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;border-top:1px solid var(--glass-border);padding-top:6px;">`;
          if (ins.avgImprovement && parseFloat(ins.avgImprovement) > 0) {
            html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Avg improvement</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val" style="color:var(--accent-green);">+${ins.avgImprovement}</span></div>`;
          }
          html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Peak time</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${hourLabel}</span></div>`;
          if (ins.favPersona) html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Fav guide</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val" style="font-size:0.7rem;">${ins.favPersona}</span></div>`;
          if (ins.favSoundscape && ins.favSoundscape !== 'none') html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Fav sound</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val" style="font-size:0.7rem;">${ins.favSoundscape}</span></div>`;
          html += `</div>`;
        } catch {}
      }

      statsEl.innerHTML = html;
    }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // STATS CHARTS MODAL — Canvas 2D chart rendering
  // ====================================================================
  const CHART_COLORS = {
    cyan: '#00e5ff', amber: '#ffab00', magenta: '#ff4081', purple: '#ba68c8',
    green: '#39ff8e', blue: '#4fc3f7', orange: '#ff9800', teal: '#26a69a',
    bars: ['#4fc3f7','#00e5ff','#26a69a','#39ff8e','#ffab00','#ff9800','#ff4081','#ba68c8','#7c4dff','#e0e0e0'],
    gridLine: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)', label: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)', title: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.7)',
  };

  function drawBarChart(canvasId, labels, values, color) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 200;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    if (!values.length || values.every(v => v === 0)) { ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '12px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; ctx.fillText('No data yet', W/2, H/2); return; }
    const pad = { top: 10, right: 10, bottom: 40, left: 32 };
    const chartW = W - pad.left - pad.right, chartH = H - pad.top - pad.bottom;
    const maxVal = Math.max(...values, 1);
    const barW = Math.min(40, (chartW / labels.length) * 0.65);
    const gap = chartW / labels.length;
    // Grid lines
    ctx.strokeStyle = CHART_COLORS.gridLine; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    for (let i = 0; i <= 4; i++) { const y = pad.top + chartH * (1 - i/4); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y); ctx.lineTo(W - pad.right, y); ctx.stroke(); }
    // Bars
    labels.forEach((label, i) => {
      const barH = (values[i] / maxVal) * chartH;
      const x = pad.left + gap * i + (gap - barW) / 2;
      const y = pad.top + chartH - barH;
      const c = Array.isArray(color) ? color[i % color.length] : color;
      ctx.fillStyle = c; ctx.beginPath();
      const r = Math.min(3, barW/2);
      ctx.moveTo(x, y + r); ctx.arcTo(x, y, x + r, y, r); ctx.arcTo(x + barW, y, x + barW, y + r, r);
      ctx.lineTo(x + barW, pad.top + chartH); ctx.lineTo(x, pad.top + chartH); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
      // Value label
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.title; ctx.font = 'bold 10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.fillText(values[i], x + barW/2, y - 4);
      // Axis label
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '9px sans-serif';
      ctx.save(); ctx.translate(x + barW/2, pad.top + chartH + 6);
      if (labels.length > 6) { ctx.rotate(-0.5); ctx.textAlign = 'right'; } else { ctx.textAlign = 'center'; }
      ctx.fillText(label.length > 12 ? label.slice(0,11) + '…' : label, 0, 8); ctx.restore();
    });
  }

  function drawLineChart(canvasId, labels, values, color) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 740, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 220;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    if (!values.length) return;
    const pad = { top: 14, right: 14, bottom: 36, left: 32 };
    const chartW = W - pad.left - pad.right, chartH = H - pad.top - pad.bottom;
    const maxVal = Math.max(...values, 1);
    const xStep = chartW / (labels.length - 1 || 1);
    // Grid
    ctx.strokeStyle = CHART_COLORS.gridLine; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    for (let i = 0; i <= 4; i++) { const y = pad.top + chartH * (1 - i/4); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y); ctx.lineTo(W - pad.right, y); ctx.stroke(); }
    // Fill area
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, pad.top + chartH);
    values.forEach((v, i) => { ctx.lineTo(pad.left + i * xStep, pad.top + chartH - (v / maxVal) * chartH); });
    ctx.lineTo(pad.left + (values.length-1) * xStep, pad.top + chartH); ctx.closePath();
    // Convert hex color to translucent rgba for the fill — handles both '#rrggbb' and 'rgb(...)'
    let fillColor;
    if (color.startsWith('#')) {
      const hex = color.slice(1);
      const full = hex.length === 3 ? hex.split('').map(c => c + c).join('') : hex;
      const r = parseInt(full.slice(0, 2), 16), g = parseInt(full.slice(2, 4), 16), b = parseInt(full.slice(4, 6), 16);
      fillColor = `rgba(${r},${g},${b},0.12)`;
    } else {
      fillColor = color.replace(')', ',0.12)').replace('rgb', 'rgba');
    }
    ctx.fillStyle = fillColor; ctx.fill();
    // Line
    ctx.beginPath();
    values.forEach((v, i) => { const x = pad.left + i * xStep, y = pad.top + chartH - (v / maxVal) * chartH; i === 0 ? ctx.moveTo(x, y) : ctx.lineTo(x, y); });
    ctx.strokeStyle = color; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
    // Dots
    values.forEach((v, i) => { const x = pad.left + i * xStep, y = pad.top + chartH - (v / maxVal) * chartH; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x, y, 3, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = color; ctx.fill(); });
    // Peak annotation
    const peakIdx = values.indexOf(Math.max(...values));
    if (values[peakIdx] > 0) {
      const px = pad.left + peakIdx * xStep, py = pad.top + chartH - (values[peakIdx] / maxVal) * chartH;
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.amber; ctx.font = 'bold 10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.fillText(`Peak: ${labels[peakIdx]} (${values[peakIdx]})`, Math.min(Math.max(px, 60), W - 60), py - 10);
    }
    // X labels
    ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '9px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    labels.forEach((l, i) => { if (labels.length <= 10 || i % 2 === 0) ctx.fillText(l, pad.left + i * xStep, H - pad.bottom + 16); });
  }

  function drawDonutChart(canvasId, segments) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 220;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    const total = segments.reduce((s, seg) => s + seg.value, 0);
    if (total === 0) { ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '12px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; ctx.fillText('No data yet', W/2, H/2); return; }
    const cx = W / 2, cy = H / 2 - 6, outerR = Math.min(W, H) / 2 - 30, innerR = outerR * 0.55;
    let angle = -Math.PI / 2;
    segments.forEach(seg => {
      const sweep = (seg.value / total) * Math.PI * 2;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, outerR, angle, angle + sweep); ctx.arc(cx, cy, innerR, angle + sweep, angle, true); ctx.closePath();
      ctx.fillStyle = seg.color; ctx.fill();
      // Label
      const mid = angle + sweep / 2;
      const lx = cx + Math.cos(mid) * (outerR + 16), ly = cy + Math.sin(mid) * (outerR + 16);
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.title; ctx.font = '10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = Math.cos(mid) > 0 ? 'left' : 'right';
      ctx.fillText(`${seg.label} ${Math.round(seg.value / total * 100)}%`, lx, ly);
      angle += sweep;
    });
  }

  function drawHorizBars(canvasId, labels, values, maxVal, colors) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 200;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    const pad = { left: 80, right: 40, top: 10, bottom: 10 };
    const rowH = (H - pad.top - pad.bottom) / labels.length;
    const barMaxW = W - pad.left - pad.right;
    labels.forEach((label, i) => {
      const y = pad.top + i * rowH;
      const barW = (values[i] / (maxVal || 1)) * barMaxW;
      ctx.fillStyle = colors[i % colors.length]; ctx.beginPath();
      const r = 3; ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y + 4); ctx.lineTo(pad.left + barW - r, y + 4); ctx.arcTo(pad.left + barW, y + 4, pad.left + barW, y + rowH - 8, r); ctx.arcTo(pad.left + barW, y + rowH - 8, pad.left + barW - r, y + rowH - 8, r); ctx.lineTo(pad.left, y + rowH - 8); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'right';
      ctx.fillText(label, pad.left - 6, y + rowH/2 + 3);
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.title; ctx.font = 'bold 10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText(values[i].toFixed(2), pad.left + barW + 6, y + rowH/2 + 3);
    });
  }

  function drawFeatureGrid(canvasId, featBitmask) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 200;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    const features = [
      { name: 'Affirmations', bit: 1 }, { name: 'Programs', bit: 2 }, { name: 'Custom Persona', bit: 4 },
      { name: 'Skip-to-Script', bit: 8 }, { name: 'Timing Fix', bit: 16 }, { name: 'Share', bit: 32 },
      { name: 'Backup', bit: 64 }, { name: 'Double Induction', bit: 128 },
    ];
    const rowH = (H - 10) / features.length;
    features.forEach((f, i) => {
      const y = 8 + i * rowH;
      const used = !!(featBitmask & f.bit);
      ctx.fillStyle = used ? CHART_COLORS.cyan : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)';
      const rx = 20, ry = y, rw = W - 40, rh = rowH - 4, rr = 4;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(rx + rr, ry); ctx.lineTo(rx + rw - rr, ry); ctx.arcTo(rx + rw, ry, rx + rw, ry + rr, rr); ctx.lineTo(rx + rw, ry + rh - rr); ctx.arcTo(rx + rw, ry + rh, rx + rw - rr, ry + rh, rr); ctx.lineTo(rx + rr, ry + rh); ctx.arcTo(rx, ry + rh, rx, ry + rh - rr, rr); ctx.lineTo(rx, ry + rr); ctx.arcTo(rx, ry, rx + rr, ry, rr); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
      ctx.fillStyle = used ? '#111' : CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = `${used ? 'bold ' : ''}11px sans-serif`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText(`${used ? '✓' : '○'}  ${f.name}`, 30, y + rowH/2 + 1);
    });
  }

  // Chart render dispatch — maps tile data-chart to render calls
  let _statsAnalytics = null;
  function renderChart(tile) {
    const chart = tile.dataset.chart;
    const a = _statsAnalytics; if (!a) return;
    const sorted = (map) => Object.entries(map || {}).sort((x,y) => y[1] - x[1]);
    const topItems = (map, n) => { const s = sorted(map); return { labels: s.slice(0,n).map(e => e[0]), values: s.slice(0,n).map(e => e[1]) }; };
    switch(chart) {
      case 'persona': { const d = topItems(a.p, 8); drawBarChart('chartPersona', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'method': { const d = topItems(a.m, 8); drawBarChart('chartMethod', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'intention': { const d = topItems(a.i, 8); drawBarChart('chartIntention', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'soundscape': { const d = topItems(a.s, 8); drawBarChart('chartSoundscape', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'hourly': { drawLineChart('chartHourly', Array.from({length:24}, (_,i) => i.toString()), a.hr, CHART_COLORS.cyan); break; }
      case 'weekday': { drawBarChart('chartWeekday', ['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat'], a.dw, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'mood': {
        if (a.mood.n > 0) {
          const postN = a.mood.postN || 0;
          const avgPre = a.mood.preSum / a.mood.n;
          const avgPost = postN > 0 && a.mood.postSum > 0 ? a.mood.postSum / postN : null;
          const mL = avgPost ? ['Pre','Post'] : ['Pre'], mV = avgPost ? [+avgPre.toFixed(1), +avgPost.toFixed(1)] : [+avgPre.toFixed(1)];
          drawBarChart('chartMood', mL, mV, [CHART_COLORS.blue, CHART_COLORS.green]);
        } else drawBarChart('chartMood', [], [], CHART_COLORS.cyan);
        break;
      }
      case 'completion': {
        const other = a.comp.total - a.comp.finished - a.comp.emergency;
        drawDonutChart('chartCompletion', [
          { label: 'Finished', value: a.comp.finished, color: CHART_COLORS.cyan },
          { label: 'Emergency', value: a.comp.emergency, color: CHART_COLORS.amber },
          { label: 'Incomplete', value: Math.max(0, other), color: CHART_COLORS.green },
        ]); break;
      }
      case 'settings': {
        if (a.cfg.n > 0) {
          const avgPhase = a.shape?.n ? (a.shape.phaseSum / a.shape.n) : 0;
          const avgWork = a.shape?.n ? (a.shape.workSum / a.shape.n) : 0;
          const cL = ['Rate','Pitch','Narr Vol','Drone','Phases','Work'];
          const cV = [a.cfg.rateSum/a.cfg.n, a.cfg.pitchSum/a.cfg.n, a.cfg.volSum/a.cfg.n, a.cfg.droneSum/a.cfg.n, avgPhase / 10, avgWork / 5];
          drawHorizBars('chartSettings', cL, cV, 1.2, [CHART_COLORS.cyan, CHART_COLORS.blue, CHART_COLORS.amber, CHART_COLORS.green, CHART_COLORS.purple || CHART_COLORS.cyan, CHART_COLORS.blue]);
        } else drawBarChart('chartSettings', [], [], CHART_COLORS.cyan);
        break;
      }
      case 'features': drawFeatureGrid('chartFeatures', a.feat); break;
    }
  }

  function renderAllCharts() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.stats-tile').forEach(tile => renderChart(tile));
  }

  async function openStatsModal() {
    const a = await getAnalytics();
    _statsAnalytics = a;
    const modal = $('statsModal');
    if (a.comp.total < 1) {
      $('statsKpiGrid').innerHTML = '';
      $('statsGrid').style.display = 'none';
      $('statsEmptyMsg').style.display = '';
      modal.style.display = 'flex'; return;
    }
    $('statsEmptyMsg').style.display = 'none';
    $('statsGrid').style.display = '';
    const ins = deriveInsights(a);
    const durMin = Math.floor(ins.avgDurationSec / 60), durSec = ins.avgDurationSec % 60;
    const hrLbl = ins.peakHour < 12 ? `${ins.peakHour || 12}am` : `${ins.peakHour === 12 ? 12 : ins.peakHour - 12}pm`;
    $('statsKpiGrid').innerHTML = [
      { val: ins.totalSessions, label: 'sessions' },
      { val: `${ins.completionRate}%`, label: 'completed' },
      { val: ins.avgImprovement && parseFloat(ins.avgImprovement) > 0 ? `+${ins.avgImprovement}` : (ins.avgImprovement || '—'), label: 'mood gain' },
      { val: `${durMin}m${durSec ? durSec + 's' : ''}`, label: 'avg duration' },
      { val: hrLbl, label: 'peak hour' },
      { val: ins.peakDayName.slice(0,3), label: 'peak day' },
    ].map(k => `<div class="stats-kpi"><div class="stats-kpi-val">${k.val}</div><div class="stats-kpi-label">${k.label}</div></div>`).join('');

    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    // Render after display so canvas has layout dimensions
    requestAnimationFrame(() => renderAllCharts());
  }

  function closeStatsModal() { $('statsModal').style.display = 'none'; _statsAnalytics = null; }

  function toggleStatsTile(tile) {
    const wasExpanded = tile.classList.contains('expanded');
    // Collapse all first
    document.querySelectorAll('.stats-tile.expanded').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('expanded'));
    if (!wasExpanded) tile.classList.add('expanded');
    // Re-render affected charts after CSS transition
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (wasExpanded) renderChart(tile);
      else document.querySelectorAll('.stats-tile').forEach(t => renderChart(t));
    }, 280);
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // EXPORT, SHARE, BACKUP/RESTORE
  // ====================================================================
  function exportScript() {
    const script = $('scriptText')?.value?.trim();
    if (!script) { notify.warn('No script to export.'); return; }
    const persona = getPersona(), method = getMethod();
    const header = `# Hypnosis Script\n# Guide: ${persona.name} | Method: ${method.name} | Length: ${state.length}\n# Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}\n\n`;
    const blob = new Blob([header + script], { type: 'text/plain' });
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = `hypnosis-${method.id}-${state.length}-${Date.now()}.txt`;
    a.click();
    // Delay revoke so the browser actually initiates the download
    setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href), 5000);
    notify.success('Script downloaded.');
  }

  /**
   * Fetch and process a `?data=<fileId>.gz` uploadPlugin share payload.
   * Supports two payload kinds: 'session-config' and 'custom-persona'.
   * Shows a confirmation modal for personas (per skill — age gate the link).
   */
  async function loadUploadedSharePayload(fileId) {
    if (!fileId) return false;
    try {
      // uploadPlugin share URLs resolve to user.uploads.dev/<id>
      const url = `https://user.uploads.dev/file/${encodeURIComponent(fileId)}`;
      let resp;
      try { resp = await fetch(url); } catch (e) {
        // Try superFetch if direct fetch is CORS-blocked
        if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.superFetch) resp = await root.superFetch(url);
        else throw e;
      }
      if (!resp || !resp.ok) throw new Error('Could not fetch shared payload');
      const blob = await resp.blob();
      let json;
      try {
        const stream = blob.stream().pipeThrough(new DecompressionStream('gzip'));
        json = await new Response(stream).text();
      } catch { json = await blob.text(); }
      const payload = JSON.parse(json);
      if (!payload || !payload.kind) throw new Error('Malformed share payload');

      if (payload.kind === 'custom-persona') {
        // Age-gate warning per Perchance skill convention
        const confirmed = await confirmAsync(
          `Someone shared a custom persona with you:\n\n"${payload.persona.name}"\n\n${payload.persona.tagline || ''}\n\nThis is user-generated content — review the voice instruction before using. Shared personas may describe sensitive themes. If you are under 18, click cancel.`,
          { okText: 'review & add', cancelText: 'cancel' }
        );
        if (!confirmed) return true;
        const existing = loadCustomPersonas();
        // Prevent duplicate IDs — if one exists, prompt to replace
        const dup = existing.find(p => p.id === payload.persona.id);
        if (dup) {
          const replace = await confirmAsync(`A persona with ID "${payload.persona.id}" already exists. Replace it?`, { okText: 'replace', cancelText: 'keep existing' });
          if (!replace) return true;
          saveCustomPersonas(existing.filter(p => p.id !== payload.persona.id).concat([payload.persona]));
        } else {
          saveCustomPersonas([...existing, payload.persona]);
        }
        refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid();
        state.selectedPersonaId = payload.persona.id;
        renderPersonaDetail(); updateStepUI();
        notify.success(`Added persona: ${payload.persona.name}`);
        return true;
      }

      if (payload.kind === 'session-config') {
        const c = payload.config || {};
        // Also install any custom persona attached to the config
        if (payload.customPersona) {
          const existing = loadCustomPersonas();
          if (!existing.find(p => p.id === payload.customPersona.id)) {
            saveCustomPersonas([...existing, payload.customPersona]);
            refreshPersonas();
          }
        }
        if (c.selectedPersonaId && state.personas.find(p => p.id === c.selectedPersonaId)) state.selectedPersonaId = c.selectedPersonaId;
        if (c.selectedMethodId && METHODS.find(m => m.id === c.selectedMethodId)) state.selectedMethodId = c.selectedMethodId;
        if (c.intentionType && INTENTION_TYPES[c.intentionType]) { state.intentionType = c.intentionType; const el = $('intentionType'); if (el) el.value = c.intentionType; }
        if (c.length && PHASE_DURATIONS[c.length]) { state.length = c.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = c.length; }
        if (c.soundscape) { state.soundscape = c.soundscape; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = c.soundscape; }
        if (c.vizOverride) { state.vizOverride = c.vizOverride; const el = $('vizSelect'); if (el) el.value = c.vizOverride; }
        if (typeof c.speechRate === 'number') state.speechRate = c.speechRate;
        if (typeof c.voicePitch === 'number') state.voicePitch = c.voicePitch;
        if (typeof c.tempoMultiplier === 'number') state.tempoMultiplier = c.tempoMultiplier;
        if (c.affirmationMode) { state.affirmationMode = c.affirmationMode; const el = $('affirmationMode'); if (el) el.value = c.affirmationMode; }
        if (c.intentionInput) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = c.intentionInput.slice(0, 500); }
        if (c.userAffirmations) { const el = $('userAffirmations'); if (el) el.value = c.userAffirmations.slice(0, 500); }
        if (c.craftedSuggestion) state.craftedSuggestion = c.craftedSuggestion;
        if (c.script) {
          const scriptEl = $('scriptText'); if (scriptEl) scriptEl.value = c.script;
          state.fullScript = c.script;
          state.parsedScript = parseScript(c.script);
          showScript();
        }
        renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
        if (typeof updateIntentionHint === 'function') updateIntentionHint();
        if (state.craftedSuggestion) { try { showCrafted(); } catch {} }
        state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: true, 5: true, 6: !!c.script };
        goToStep(c.script ? 6 : 5);
        const persona = getPersona(), method = getMethod();
        notify.info(`Shared config loaded: ${persona.name} · ${method.name} · ${c.length || 'medium'}.`, 8000);
        return true;
      }

      notify.warn('Unknown payload kind: ' + payload.kind);
      return false;
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('Share payload load failed:', e);
      notify.error('Could not load shared link: ' + (e.message || e));
      return false;
    }
  }

  async function loadSharedConfig() {
    // new uploadPlugin-backed share links (`?data=<fileId>.gz`)
    try {
      const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      const dataId = urlParams.get('data');
      if (dataId) {
        const handled = await loadUploadedSharePayload(dataId);
        if (handled) {
          // Clean up URL so a reload doesn't reinstall
          history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname);
          return;
        }
      }
    } catch (e) { console.warn('data= param handling failed:', e); }

    const hash = window.location.hash;
    if (!hash.startsWith('#cfg=')) return;
    const paramStr = hash.slice(5);
    try {
      const params = new URLSearchParams(paramStr);
      const personaId = params.get('p');
      const methodId = params.get('m');
      const intentType = params.get('i');
      const length = params.get('l');
      const soundscape = params.get('s');
      const rate = params.get('r');
      const viz = params.get('v');
      const intentText = params.get('t');
      const aff = params.get('a');
      const affirmMode = params.get('am') || params.get('affirm');
      const voiceName = params.get('vn') || params.get('voice') || params.get('narrator');

      // Apply settings
      if (personaId && state.personas.find(p => p.id === personaId)) state.selectedPersonaId = personaId;
      if (methodId && METHODS.find(m => m.id === methodId)) state.selectedMethodId = methodId;
      if (intentType && INTENTION_TYPES[intentType]) { state.intentionType = intentType; $('intentionType').value = intentType; }
      if (length && PHASE_DURATIONS[length]) { state.length = length; $('lengthSelect').value = length; }
      if (soundscape) { state.soundscape = soundscape; state.droneEnabled = soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = soundscape; }
      if (rate) state.speechRate = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(1, parseInt(rate, 10) / 100));
      if (viz) { state.vizOverride = viz; const el = $('vizSelect'); if (el) el.value = viz; }
      if (intentText) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = decodeURIComponent(intentText).slice(0, 500); }
      if (aff) { const el = $('userAffirmations'); if (el) el.value = decodeURIComponent(aff).slice(0, 500); }
      if (affirmMode) { state.affirmationMode = affirmMode; const el = $('affirmationMode'); if (el) el.value = affirmMode; }
      if (voiceName) { state._savedVoiceName = decodeURIComponent(voiceName).slice(0, 200); applySavedVoiceSelection(); updateVoiceInfo(); }

      renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
      updateIntentionHint(); updateStepUI();

      // Onboarding banner for the recipient
      const persona = getPersona();
      const method = getMethod();
      notify.info(`Shared config loaded: ${persona.name} · ${method.name} · ${length || 'medium'}. Review settings and generate when ready.`, 8000);

      // Mark steps as complete so they can jump to configure/generate in the new 6-step flow
      state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: true, 5: false, 6: false };
      goToStep(5); // Start at Configure so they can review

      // Clean URL
      history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
    } catch(e) {
      // Fallback: try old gzip+base64 format for backward compat
      try {
        const bytes = Uint8Array.from(atob(paramStr), c => c.charCodeAt(0));
        const stream = new Blob([bytes]).stream().pipeThrough(new DecompressionStream('gzip'));
        const json = await new Response(stream).text();
        const cfg = JSON.parse(json);
        if (cfg.p) state.selectedPersonaId = cfg.p;
        if (cfg.m) state.selectedMethodId = cfg.m;
        if (cfg.i) { state.intentionType = cfg.i; $('intentionType').value = cfg.i; }
        if (cfg.l) { state.length = cfg.l; $('lengthSelect').value = cfg.l; }
        renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail(); updateStepUI();
        state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: true, 5: false, 6: false };
        goToStep(5); // Configure — let user review before generating
        notify.info('Shared config loaded (legacy format). Review and generate.');
        history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
      } catch(e2) { console.error('Failed to parse shared config:', e2); }
    }
  }

  async function exportBackup() {
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.BACKUP);
    const backup = { version: 5, exportedAt: Date.now(), personas: loadCustomPersonas(), history: (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [], program: (await idbGet('stillness_program_v1')) || null, profile: getProfile(), settings: _buildSettingsObj(), analytics: (await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY)) || null, adaptive: (await idbGet(ADAPTIVE_KEY)) || null };
    const json = JSON.stringify(backup);
    let blob;
    try {
      const stream = new Blob([json]).stream().pipeThrough(new CompressionStream('gzip'));
      blob = await new Response(stream).blob();
    } catch(e) { blob = new Blob([json], { type: 'application/json' }); }
    const a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = `stillness-backup-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.gz`;
    a.click();
    // Delay revoke — some browsers cancel the download if URL is revoked before it starts
    setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href), 5000);
    notify.success('Backup exported (.gz).');
  }

  async function importBackup(file) {
    try {
      let text;
      try {
        const stream = file.stream().pipeThrough(new DecompressionStream('gzip'));
        text = await new Response(stream).text();
      } catch(e) {
        text = await file.text();
      }
      const backup = JSON.parse(text);
      if (!backup.version) { notify.error('Invalid backup file.'); return; }
      const ep = loadCustomPersonas(), eIds = new Set(ep.map(p => p.id));
      const np = (backup.personas||[]).filter(p => !eIds.has(p.id));
      if (np.length) { saveCustomPersonas([...ep,...np]); refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); }
      const existingHistoryRaw = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
      const existingHistory = existingHistoryRaw.map(normalizeHistoryEntry);
      const ehIds = new Set(existingHistory.map(h => h.id));
      const incomingHistory = (backup.history || []).map(normalizeHistoryEntry);
      const nh = incomingHistory.filter(h => !ehIds.has(h.id));
      if (nh.length || existingHistoryRaw.length !== existingHistory.length) {
        const mergedHistory = [...nh, ...existingHistory].map(normalizeHistoryEntry).sort((a,b)=>(b.date||0)-(a.date||0));
        mergedHistory.length = Math.min(mergedHistory.length, 50);
        await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', mergedHistory);
        renderSessionHistory();
      }
      if (backup.program && !(await idbGet('stillness_program_v1'))) { await idbSet('stillness_program_v1', backup.program); renderPrograms(); }
      if (backup.analytics) {
        const mergedAnalytics = mergeAnalyticsData(await getAnalytics(), backup.analytics);
        await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, mergedAnalytics);
      }
      if (backup.adaptive && !(await idbGet(ADAPTIVE_KEY))) { await idbSet(ADAPTIVE_KEY, backup.adaptive); }
      if (backup.settings) {
        const merged = normalizeSettings({ ..._buildSettingsObj(), ...normalizeSettings(backup.settings) });
        if (_kv) { try { await _kv.settings.set(SETTINGS_KEY, merged); } catch {} }
        try {
          localStorage.setItem(SETTINGS_KEY, JSON.stringify(merged));
          localStorage.removeItem('stillness_settings_v4');
          localStorage.removeItem('stillness_settings_v3');
          localStorage.removeItem('stillness_settings_v2');
        } catch {}
        await loadUserSettings();
      }
      if (backup.profile) {
        const hasExistingProfile = !!($('pfName')?.value?.trim() || $('pfAbout')?.value?.trim() || $('pfGoals')?.value?.trim());
        if (!hasExistingProfile) applyProfileToForm(backup.profile, { save: true });
      }
      await rebuildAnalytics((await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || []);
      renderSidebarStats();
      renderHeatmap();
      renderSparkline();
      notify.success(`Imported: ${np.length} personas, ${nh.length} sessions.`);
    } catch(e) { notify.error('Import failed: ' + e.message); }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TRANSCRIPT
  // ====================================================================
  function populateTranscript() {
    const panel = $('transcriptPanel');
    if (!panel || !state.parsedScript) return;
    const phases = getPlaybackPhaseOrder();
    let html = '';
    for (const phase of phases) {
      const text = state.parsedScript[phase];
      if (!text || text.trim().length < 10) continue;
      const clean = stripLeadingPhaseHeader(text, phase).replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, ' ⋯ ').trim();
      html += `<div class="t-phase">${escapeHtml(getPhaseLabel(phase))}</div><div>${escapeHtml(clean)}</div>`;
    }
    panel.innerHTML = html;
  }

  function toggleTranscript() {
    const panel = $('transcriptPanel');
    if (!panel) return;
    panel.classList.toggle('visible');
    const btn = $('transcriptToggle');
    if (btn) btn.textContent = panel.classList.contains('visible') ? '✕ close' : '📜 script';
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SESSION PLAYER
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * Validate that the current script has a safe ending structure.
   * Per spec: \{\{Lightener\}\} + \{\{Wake\}\} + \{\{Reintroduction\}\} must exist before session playback.
   * Sleep intention type is exempt — it deliberately drifts into sleep.
   * Also flags unbalanced Deepener/Lightener nesting.
   *
   * @returns \{\{ ok: boolean, missing: string[], unbalanced: object|null, isSleep: boolean \}\}
   */
  function validateSessionSafety() {
    const isSleep = state.intentionType === 'sleep';
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    const has = (base) => sections.some(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === base);
    const missing = [];
    if (!isSleep) {
      if (!has('lightener'))       missing.push('Lightener');
      if (!has('wake'))            missing.push('Wake');
      if (!has('reintroduction'))  missing.push('Reintroduction');
    }
    const deepenerCount = sections.filter(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'deepener').length;
    const lightenerCount = sections.filter(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'lightener').length;
    let unbalanced = null;
    if (!isSleep && deepenerCount !== lightenerCount) {
      unbalanced = { deepenerCount, lightenerCount, diff: deepenerCount - lightenerCount };
    }
    const ok = missing.length === 0 && !unbalanced;
    return { ok, missing, unbalanced, isSleep };
  }

  /**
   * Show the pre-session unsafe-structure warning modal.
   * Returns true if user chooses to proceed anyway, false to go back.
   */
  function showUnsafeSessionModal(safety) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
      backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
      const issues = [];
      if (safety.missing.length) {
        issues.push(`<li>Missing: <strong>${safety.missing.join(', ')}</strong> — without these, the session ends in trance.</li>`);
      }
      if (safety.unbalanced) {
        const u = safety.unbalanced;
        if (u.diff > 0) issues.push(`<li>${u.deepenerCount} Deepener${u.deepenerCount>1?'s':''} but only ${u.lightenerCount} Lightener${u.lightenerCount===1?'':'s'} — you will go deeper than you return.</li>`);
        else            issues.push(`<li>${u.lightenerCount} Lightener${u.lightenerCount>1?'s':''} without matching Deepeners (${u.deepenerCount}) — structurally inconsistent.</li>`);
      }
      backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal unsafe-modal">
        <div class="unsafe-header">⚠ Incomplete session structure</div>
        <div style="font-size:0.88rem; line-height:1.55; color:var(--text-dim);">
          This session is missing finishing phases required for safe emergence from trance.
        </div>
        <ul class="unsafe-list">${issues.join('')}</ul>
        <div class="unsafe-note">
          <strong>Why this matters.</strong> A proper hypnosis session brings you fully back to normal
          waking awareness. Skipping the Lightener, Wake, or Reintroduction phases may leave you feeling
          groggy, partially dissociated, or — in rare cases — still in a light trance state.
          Only proceed if this is deliberate (e.g. you're running a custom sleep-induction session and intend to drift off).
        </div>
        <div class="modal-actions">
          <button class="btn" id="_unsafeBack">← Go Back</button>
          <button class="btn btn-unsafe" id="_unsafeProceed">Proceed Anyway (Unsafe)</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
      const cleanup = (val) => { backdrop.remove(); resolve(val); };
      backdrop.querySelector('#_unsafeBack').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(false));
      backdrop.querySelector('#_unsafeProceed').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(true));
      backdrop.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup(false); });
    });
  }

  async function startSession() {
    // Emergency cooldown check
    if (state._cooldownUntil && Date.now() < state._cooldownUntil) {
      if (state._debug?.skipCooldown) {
        sdLog('cooldown bypassed — debugSkipCooldown on');
      } else {
        const remaining = Math.ceil((state._cooldownUntil - Date.now()) / 1000);
        notify.warn(`Please wait ${remaining}s before starting another session.`);
        return;
      }
    }

    let scriptText = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (!scriptText) { notify.warn('Generate or paste a script first.'); return; }

    // Structural safety gate — user must explicitly proceed if ending phases are missing
    // or deepener/lightener are unbalanced. Sleep intention is exempt by design.
    const safety = validateSessionSafety();
    if (!safety.ok) {
      if (state._debug?.skipSafetyGate) {
        sdLog('safety gate bypassed — debugSkipSafetyGate on', safety);
        state._startedUnsafe = true;
      } else {
        const proceed = await showUnsafeSessionModal(safety);
        if (!proceed) return;
        // Record the unsafe-start in analytics so we can surface it in the post-session review
        state._startedUnsafe = true;
      }
    } else {
      state._startedUnsafe = false;
    }

    // If script was edited, offer to fix pause timings
    if (_scriptEditedSinceGen) {
      const fix = await confirmAsync('You\'ve edited the script. Would you like to recalculate pause timings to match your changes?\n\nYes = auto-fix pause markers based on sentence length\nNo = keep current timings as-is', { okText: 'recalculate', cancelText: 'keep as-is' });
      if (fix) {
        const fixed = fixScriptTimings(scriptText);
        $('scriptText').value = fixed;
        state.fullScript = fixed;
        state.parsedScript = parseScript(fixed);
        showScript();
        notify.success('Pause timings recalculated.');
        scriptText = fixed; // update local so the session plays the fixed text
      }
      _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
    }

    // Daily session cap
    if (!(await checkDailyCap())) return;

    // Check TTS availability
    const voiceList = (typeof speechSynthesis !== 'undefined') ? speechSynthesis.getVoices() : [];
    if (voiceList.length === 0) {
      if (!await confirmAsync('No text-to-speech voices are available in this browser. The session will run silently (visuals only). Continue anyway?', { okText: 'continue', cancelText: 'go back' })) return;
    }

    // Stop any configure-tab previews before starting session
    if (typeof _stopAllPreviews === 'function') _stopAllPreviews();

    state.fullScript = scriptText;
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(scriptText);
    state.voice = getSelectedVoice();
    state.abortFlag = false;
    state._finishing = false;
    state._sessionStartTime = Date.now();
    state._pausedTotalMs = 0;      // cumulative time spent paused
    state._pauseStartedAt = null;  // wallclock of current pause start (if paused)
    state._currentPhase = 'settling';
    const method = getMethod();

    // Double induction: pick a contrasting second voice
    state._doubleInduction = method.id === 'double-induction';
    state._secondVoice = null;
    if (state._doubleInduction) {
      markFeatureUsed(FEAT.DOUBLE_INDUCT);
      const voices = speechSynthesis.getVoices().filter(v => v.lang.startsWith('en') && v.name !== state.voice?.name);
      // Try to find an opposite-gender voice for maximum contrast
      const primaryName = (state.voice?.name || '').toLowerCase();
      const isMale = /male|daniel|james|david|mark|george/i.test(primaryName) && !/female/i.test(primaryName);
      const opposite = voices.find(v => isMale ? /female|samantha|karen|moira|zira/i.test(v.name) : /male|daniel|james|david|mark/i.test(v.name) && !/female/i.test(v.name));
      state._secondVoice = opposite || voices[0] || null;
      if (state._secondVoice) {
        notify.info(`Double induction: ${state.voice?.name || 'primary'} + ${state._secondVoice.name}`);
      }
    }

    switchScreen('session-screen');
    document.body.classList.add('in-session');
    showSessionControls(); // start auto-hide timer
    $('personaIndicator').textContent = '· ' + getPersona().name.toLowerCase() + ' ·';
    $('methodIndicator').textContent = '· ' + method.name.toLowerCase() + ' ·';

    // Reset progress UI
    $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = '0%';
    updatePhaseDots(-1);

    // Apply HUD visibility toggles from Configure tab
    const h = state.hud;
    const $s = (id, vis) => { const el = $(id); if (el) el.style.display = vis ? '' : 'none'; };
    $s('fixationDot', h.fixationDot);
    $s('textDisplay', h.textDisplay);
    $s('phaseDots', h.phaseDots);
    $s('phaseIndicator', h.phaseLabel);
    document.querySelector('.session-progress-wrap')?.style.setProperty('display', h.progressBar ? '' : 'none');
    $s('sessionTime', h.sessionTime);
    $s('personaIndicator', h.labels);
    $s('methodIndicator', h.labels);
    $s('audioIndicator', h.labels);

    // Apply visual override (user selection or method default)
    const vizChoice = state.vizOverride === 'auto' ? method.visual : state.vizOverride;
    if (vizChoice === 'none') {
      // Black screen only — skip visual setup
      const stage = $('stage');
      Array.from(stage.children).forEach(c => {
        if (!c.classList.contains('fixation-dot') && !c.classList.contains('audio-indicator')
          && !c.classList.contains('persona-indicator') && !c.classList.contains('method-indicator')
          && !c.classList.contains('session-progress-wrap') && !c.classList.contains('transcript-panel')) c.remove();
      });
    } else {
      setupVisual(vizChoice);
    }
    populateTranscript();
    $('transcriptPanel')?.classList.remove('visible');
    const tBtn = $('transcriptToggle');
    if (tBtn) tBtn.textContent = '📜 script';

    // Start soundscape (replaces old drone toggle)
    if (state.soundscape && state.soundscape !== 'none') {
      try {
        await drone.start(state.droneVolume, state.soundscape);
        $('audioIndicator').textContent = '· ' + state.soundscape + ' ·';
      } catch(e) {
        notify.info('Audio unavailable — tap the screen to enable audio, then try again.');
      }
    }

    // Haptic marker — double-pulse on session start (Android/Chrome)
    vibrateSessionMarker();

    // Warm overlay for sleep sessions (blue-light reduction)
    setSleepOverlay(state.intentionType === 'sleep');

    // Background engine — activate chosen background source
    bgEngine.source = state.bgSource || 'none';
    bgEngine.prompt = state.bgPrompt || '';
    if (bgEngine.source === 'ai') {
      bgEngine.pregenerate(5); // non-blocking — starts generating in background
    } else if (bgEngine.source === 'local-image' && state._bgFile) {
      bgEngine.setLocalFile(state._bgFile);
    } else if (bgEngine.source === 'local-video' && state._bgFile) {
      bgEngine.setLocalFile(state._bgFile);
    } else if (bgEngine.source === 'youtube' && state.bgYoutubeUrl) {
      bgEngine.setYouTube(state.bgYoutubeUrl);
    } else if (bgEngine.source === 'url' && state.bgStaticUrl) {
      bgEngine.setStaticImage(state.bgStaticUrl);
    }
    if (bgEngine.source !== 'none') bgEngine.activate();

    // Media Session API — lock-screen controls for mobile
    setMediaSession(true);

    // Reset post-session controls for fresh state
    const postSlider = $('postStateSlider'); if (postSlider) { postSlider.value = 5; }
    const postVal = $('postStateVal'); if (postVal) postVal.textContent = '5';
    const alertSlider = $('alertnessSlider'); if (alertSlider) { alertSlider.value = 7; }
    const alertVal = $('alertnessVal'); if (alertVal) alertVal.textContent = '7';
    const depthSl = $('depthSlider'); if (depthSl) { depthSl.value = 5; }
    const depthV = $('depthVal'); if (depthV) depthV.textContent = '5';
    const journal = $('journalText'); if (journal) journal.value = '';

    // Wake Lock — prevent screen timeout during session
    try {
      if (navigator.wakeLock) {
        state._wakeLock = await navigator.wakeLock.request('screen');
        state._wakeLock.addEventListener('release', () => { state._wakeLock = null; });
      }
    } catch(e) { /* Wake Lock not available or denied */ }

    // Content warning for advanced/intense methods or authoritarian personas
    const needsWarning = method.category === 'advanced' || ['drill-instructor','dominatrix','interrogator','commander','headmistress','surgeon'].includes(getPersona().id);
    if (needsWarning) {
      const warningShown = await confirmAsync(
        'This session uses advanced techniques that may produce intense experiences including dissociation, hallucination, or strong emotional responses.\n\nEnsure you are in a safe, comfortable environment. Do not drive or operate machinery after.\n\nThe "end & re-alert" button is always available.',
        { okText: 'proceed', cancelText: 'go back' }
      );
      if (!warningShown) {
        switchScreen('setup-wizard');
        document.body.classList.remove('in-session'); document.body.classList.remove('controls-hidden'); clearTimeout(_controlsTimer);
        await drone.stop(); stopVisuals();
        bgEngine.clear();
        setSleepOverlay(false);
        // Clear media session metadata set earlier in startSession
        if ('mediaSession' in navigator) {
          try {
            navigator.mediaSession.metadata = null;
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('play', null);
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('pause', null);
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('stop', null);
          } catch {}
        }
        // Reset session state so visibilitychange doesn't treat this as an active session
        state._sessionStartTime = null;
        state._pausedTotalMs = 0;
        state._pauseStartedAt = null;
        try { state._wakeLock?.release(); } catch(e) {}
        return;
      }
    }

    // Session time tracker
    state._timeInterval = setInterval(() => {
      if (state.paused) return;
      const pausedMs = (state._pausedTotalMs || 0);
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - state._sessionStartTime - pausedMs) / 1000);
      const mins = Math.floor(elapsed / 60);
      const secs = elapsed % 60;
      const timeEl = $('sessionTime');
      if (timeEl) timeEl.textContent = `${mins}:${String(secs).padStart(2,'0')} elapsed`;
    }, 1000);

    const phases = getPlaybackPhaseOrder().filter(phase => state.parsedScript?.[phase]);
    renderSessionPhaseDots(phases);
    const phaseLabels = Object.fromEntries(phases.map(phase => [phase, getPhaseLabel(phase).toLowerCase()]));

    const durations = PHASE_DURATIONS[state.length] || PHASE_DURATIONS.medium;
    const expectedSec = phases.reduce((sum, phase) => {
      const base = phase.replace(/-\d+$/, '');
      if (base === 'affirm') return sum + 45;
      return sum + (durations[base] || 60);
    }, 0);
    const safetyCheck = () => {
      if (state._finishing || !state._sessionStartTime) return;
      // If user is paused, reschedule — don't force-end a user-paused session
      if (state.paused) { state._safetyTimeout = setTimeout(safetyCheck, 60000); return; }
      notify.warn('Session exceeded maximum expected duration — auto-finishing.');
      state._finishing = true;
      state.abortFlag = true;
      speechSynthesis.cancel();
      finishSession(false);
    };
    state._safetyTimeout = setTimeout(safetyCheck, (expectedSec * 2 + 300) * 1000);

    for (let pi = 0; pi < phases.length; pi++) {
      const phase = phases[pi];
      if (state.abortFlag) break;
      const phaseText = state.parsedScript[phase];
      if (!phaseText || phaseText.trim().length < 10) continue;

      // Update phase state
      state._currentPhase = phase;
      $('phaseIndicator').textContent = phaseLabels[phase];

      // Update phase dots
      updatePhaseDots(pi);

      // Update progress bar
      const pct = Math.round((pi / Math.max(phases.length, 1)) * 100);
      $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = pct + '%';

      // Modulate drone frequency per phase
      if (state.droneEnabled && drone.running) drone.setPhaseFreq(phase);

      const cleanText = stripLeadingPhaseHeader(phaseText, phase).trim();
      try { await speakScript(cleanText); }
      catch(e) { console.error(`Phase "${phase}" speak error:`, e); }
    }

    // Complete progress bar
    $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = '100%';
    updatePhaseDots(phases.length, phases.length);

    // Always finish the session — if abortFlag was set by emergencyEnd,
    // that path calls finishSession(true) itself, so only call if not aborting.
    // Guard against double-finish with a flag.
    if (!state.abortFlag && !state._finishing) {
      state._finishing = true;
      finishSession(false);
    }
  }

  // Interruptible sleep — checks abortFlag & paused state in 200ms chunks so
  // pause/end during a \x5BPAUSE n\x5D marker responds quickly instead of waiting
  // for the whole sleep to finish.
  async function interruptibleSleep(totalMs, bypassAbort = false) {
    const CHUNK = 200;
    let elapsed = 0;
    while (elapsed < totalMs) {
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) return;
      while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) { await sleep(CHUNK); }
      const remaining = totalMs - elapsed;
      await sleep(Math.min(CHUNK, remaining));
      elapsed += CHUNK;
    }
  }

  async function speakScript(text, bypassAbort = false) {
    // Resolve \{\{user\}\}, \{\{nar\}\}, \{\{intention\}\}, \{\{affirmation\}\} tokens before
    // speech. Runs BEFORE sanitization so any expanded content (e.g. a
    // pasted affirmation with punctuation) is normalized by the passes below.
    let canonical = resolveTokens(text);
    // Sanitize: strip phase markers and malformed pause markers
    canonical = canonical.replace(PHASE_MARKER_STRIP_RX, '');
    canonical = canonical.replace(/\[\s*pause[^\]]*\]/gi, (m) => {
      const num = m.match(/\d+/);
      return num ? `\x5BPAUSE ${num[0]}\x5D` : '';
    });
    canonical = canonical.replace(/\[[^\]]+\]/g, m =>
      /^\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D$/i.test(m) ? m : ''
    );
    // Normalize whitespace — strip newlines, collapse spaces
    canonical = canonical.replace(/[\r\n]+/g, ' ').replace(/  +/g, ' ').trim();

    const parts = canonical.split(/\x5BPAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/i);
    const display = $('textDisplay');
    const shouldDuck = drone.running && state.duckingEnabled;
    let isDucked = false;

    for (let i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;
      while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) await sleep(200);
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;

      if (i % 2 === 0) {
        // ── TEXT SEGMENT — split into sentences for per-sentence TTS ──
        const segment = parts[i].trim();
        if (!segment) continue;
        const sentences = segment.split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+/).filter(s => s.trim());

        // Duck FIRST — let it ramp down during display fade
        if (shouldDuck && !isDucked) { drone.duck(); isDucked = true; }

        for (const sentence of sentences) {
          if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;
          while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) await sleep(200);
          if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;

          if (display) {
            display.style.opacity = 0;
            await sleep(200);
            display.textContent = sentence;
            display.style.opacity = 0.5;
          }
          await speak(sentence);
          await sleep(120); // post-speak buffer — let last audio samples drain
        }

      } else {
        // ── PAUSE MARKER ──
        const seconds = parseInt(parts[i], 10) || 4;
        const tempo = state.tempoMultiplier || 1.0;
        const rateScale = 1 / Math.sqrt(Math.max(state.speechRate || 0.65, 0.4));
        const scaled = Math.max(1, Math.round(seconds * tempo * rateScale));

        // Only unduck for pauses ≥ 5s base (long dramatic pauses)
        // Short pauses: stay ducked to avoid pumping
        if (shouldDuck && isDucked && seconds >= 5) {
          drone.unduck(); isDucked = false;
          await interruptibleSleep(scaled * 1000, bypassAbort);
        } else {
          // Stay ducked through short pauses — cleaner audio
          await interruptibleSleep(scaled * 1000, bypassAbort);
        }
      }
    }
    // Always unduck at end of phase
    if (shouldDuck && isDucked) { drone.unduck(); isDucked = false; }
  }

  function speak(text) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      if (!('speechSynthesis' in window)) { setTimeout(resolve, text.length * 80); return; }
      // Only cancel if something is unexpectedly still speaking
      if (speechSynthesis.speaking || speechSynthesis.pending) speechSynthesis.cancel();
      setTimeout(() => _doSpeak(text, resolve), speechSynthesis.speaking ? 80 : 20);
    });
  }
  function _doSpeak(text, resolve) {
    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
    u.voice = state.voice || getSelectedVoice();
    u.rate = state.speechRate; u.pitch = state.voicePitch || 0.85; u.volume = state.voiceVolume ?? 1.0;
    let settled = false;
    let lastBoundaryAt = Date.now();
    let boundaryEverFired = false;
    const done = () => { if (!settled) { settled = true; clearInterval(silenceWatch); resolve(); } };
    u.onend = done;
    u.onerror = done;

    // Word-level highlighting via onboundary (Chrome/Safari desktop)
    const display = $('textDisplay');
    u.onboundary = (e) => {
      lastBoundaryAt = Date.now();
      boundaryEverFired = true;
      if (e.name === 'word' && display) {
        const before = text.slice(0, e.charIndex);
        const word = text.slice(e.charIndex, e.charIndex + e.charLength);
