        const after = text.slice(e.charIndex + e.charLength);
        display.innerHTML = `<span style="opacity:0.35">${escapeHtml(before)}</span><span style="opacity:1;color:var(--text)">${escapeHtml(word)}</span><span style="opacity:0.35">${escapeHtml(after)}</span>`;
      }
    };

    speechSynthesis.speak(u);

    // Double induction: fire a second utterance simultaneously
    if (state._doubleInduction && state._secondVoice) {
      const u2 = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
      u2.voice = state._secondVoice;
      u2.rate = state.speechRate * 0.92; u2.pitch = 0.75; u2.volume = 0.7;
      u2.onend = () => {}; u2.onerror = () => {};
      speechSynthesis.speak(u2);
    }

    // ACTIVE SILENCE WATCHDOG — every 2s, check if speech has made progress.
    // Only use boundary-based stuck detection if onboundary actually fires on
    // this platform. Many voices/browsers never fire it — in that case we rely
    // solely on the not-speaking check and hard ceiling.
    const speakStartedAt = Date.now();
    const silenceWatch = setInterval(() => {
      if (settled) { clearInterval(silenceWatch); return; }
      // CRITICAL: skip all checks while session is paused — speechSynthesis
      // reports speaking=false during pause, which triggers false done()
      if (state.paused) return;
      const silentFor = Date.now() - lastBoundaryAt;
      if (boundaryEverFired && speechSynthesis.speaking && silentFor > 8000) {
        // Chrome is stuck — boundaries were firing then stopped for 8s
        speechSynthesis.cancel();
        done();
      }
      // Grace period: don't check not-speaking until at least 1s after start
      if (Date.now() - speakStartedAt > 1000 && !speechSynthesis.speaking && !speechSynthesis.pending) {
        // Speech finished without firing onend (Firefox edge case)
        done();
      }
    }, 2000);

    // Hard ceiling — scaled by speech rate (slower rate = more time needed)
    // If paused, reschedule instead of killing — user might pause for minutes
    const rateMultiplier = 1 / Math.max(state.speechRate || 0.65, 0.4);
    const hardCeiling = Math.max(15000, text.length * 180 * rateMultiplier);
    const ceilingCheck = () => {
      if (settled) return;
      if (state.paused) { setTimeout(ceilingCheck, 5000); return; } // re-check after pause
      speechSynthesis.cancel(); done();
    };
    setTimeout(ceilingCheck, hardCeiling);
  }
  const sleep = ms => new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms));

  // ====================================================================
  // AUDIO RECORDER (ambience-only — TTS can't be captured via Web Audio)
  // ====================================================================
  let _recorder = null, _recordedChunks = [];

  function startRecording() {
    if (!drone.ctx || !drone.master) { notify.warn('Start a session with a soundscape first.'); return; }
    try {
      const dest = drone.ctx.createMediaStreamDestination();
      drone.master.connect(dest);
      _recorder = new MediaRecorder(dest.stream, { mimeType: 'audio/webm;codecs=opus' });
      _recordedChunks = [];
      _recorder.ondataavailable = e => { if (e.data.size > 0) _recordedChunks.push(e.data); };
      _recorder.onstop = () => {
        if (_recordedChunks.length === 0) return;
        const blob = new Blob(_recordedChunks, { type: 'audio/webm' });
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        a.download = `stillness-ambience-${Date.now()}.webm`;
        a.click();
        // Delay revoke so the browser actually initiates the download
        setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href), 5000);
        notify.success('Ambience recording downloaded.');
        _recordedChunks = [];
      };
      _recorder.start();
      notify.info('Recording ambience...');
      const btn = $('recordBtn');
      if (btn) { btn.textContent = '⏹ stop recording'; btn.classList.add('recording'); }
    } catch(e) { notify.error('Recording not supported in this browser.'); }
  }

  function stopRecording() {
    if (_recorder && _recorder.state === 'recording') {
      _recorder.stop(); _recorder = null;
      const btn = $('recordBtn');
      if (btn) { btn.textContent = '⏺ record ambience'; btn.classList.remove('recording'); }
    }
  }

  function toggleRecording() {
    if (_recorder && _recorder.state === 'recording') stopRecording();
    else startRecording();
  }

  async function finishSession(wasEmergency = false) {
    clearInterval(state._timeInterval);
    clearTimeout(state._safetyTimeout);
    state.paused = false; // don't leak paused state into the next session
    closeLivePanel();
    stopRecording(); // Stop any active recording before tearing down audio
    await drone.stop(); stopVisuals(); speechSynthesis.cancel();
    // Clear lock-screen media session so it doesn't linger post-session
    if ('mediaSession' in navigator) {
      try {
        navigator.mediaSession.metadata = null;
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('play', null);
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('pause', null);
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('stop', null);
      } catch {}
    }
    document.body.classList.remove('in-session'); document.body.classList.remove('controls-hidden'); clearTimeout(_controlsTimer);
    switchScreen('post-screen');

    // Release wake lock
    try { state._wakeLock?.release(); } catch(e) {}

    // Save session to history — exclude paused time from duration
    let pausedMs = (state._pausedTotalMs || 0);
    if (state._pauseStartedAt) pausedMs += (Date.now() - state._pauseStartedAt); // finishing while paused
    const elapsed = state._sessionStartTime ? Math.max(0, Math.round((Date.now() - state._sessionStartTime - pausedMs) / 1000)) : 0;
    const currentProfile = getProfile();
    const scriptMetrics = getScriptMetrics(state.fullScript || '');
    const sessionRecord = {
      id: 'sess_' + Date.now(),
      date: Date.now(),
      guide: getPersona().name,
      method: getMethod().name,
      intention: state.intentionType,
      length: state.length,
      soundscape: state.soundscape,
      durationSec: elapsed,
      completed: !wasEmergency,
      preMood: state._preMood ?? null,
      preTension: state._preTension ?? null,
      preEnergy: state._preEnergy ?? null,
      // Full reproducibility data
      script: state.fullScript || '',
      personaId: state.selectedPersonaId,
      methodId: state.selectedMethodId,
      intentionText: $('intentionInput')?.value || '',
      voiceName: $('voiceSelect')?.value || '',
      userAffirmations: $('userAffirmations')?.value || '',
      affirmationMode: $('affirmationMode')?.value || 'woven',
      speechRate: state.speechRate,
      voicePitch: state.voicePitch,
      voiceVolume: state.voiceVolume,
      droneVolume: state.droneVolume,
      vizOverride: state.vizOverride,
      vizSettings: { ...state.vizSettings },
      duckingEnabled: state.duckingEnabled,
      phaseOrder: getPlaybackPhaseOrder(),
      profileName: currentProfile.name || 'Practitioner',
      profileSnapshot: currentProfile,
      workBlockCount: scriptMetrics.workBlocks,
      metrics: scriptMetrics,
      workflowVersion: 11,
      stepsTotal: 6,
    };
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    history.unshift(sessionRecord);
    if (history.length > 50) history.length = 50; // Keep last 50
    await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', history);
    await recordAnalytics(sessionRecord, wasEmergency);
    updateAdaptiveProfile(sessionRecord, wasEmergency); // non-blocking
    updateSessionMemory(state.fullScript, sessionRecord); // Memory system — non-blocking
    renderHeatmap(); // Refresh activity heatmap
    renderSparkline(); // Refresh rising-score sparkline
    renderSidebarStats(); // Refresh sidebar stats

    // Haptic marker — double-pulse on session end
    vibrateSessionMarker();

    // Remove warm overlay
    setSleepOverlay(false);

    // Clean up background engine
    bgEngine.clear();

    // Advance structured program (non-emergency only)
    if (!wasEmergency) advanceProgramDay();

    // Refresh method gating (may unlock new categories)
    applyMethodGating();

    // Build post-session summary
    const mins = Math.floor(elapsed / 60), secs = elapsed % 60;
    const persona = getPersona(), method = getMethod();
    const summaryEl = $('postSummary');
    summaryEl.innerHTML = `
      <div class="post-card-title">session summary</div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">guide</span><span class="post-value">${escapeHtml(persona.name)}</span></div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">method</span><span class="post-value">${escapeHtml(method.name)}</span></div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">duration</span><span class="post-value">${mins}:${String(secs).padStart(2,'0')}</span></div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">completion</span><span class="post-value">${wasEmergency ? 'ended early' : 'completed'}</span></div>
    `;

    // Show trigger/suggestion reminder if relevant
    const triggerBox = $('postTriggerBox');
    if (state.craftedSuggestion && state.craftedSuggestion.trigger && state.craftedSuggestion.trigger !== 'ongoing state') {
      triggerBox.style.display = '';
      triggerBox.innerHTML = `
        <div class="post-trigger-title">your trigger</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-text">${escapeHtml(state.craftedSuggestion.trigger)}</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-sub">→ ${escapeHtml(state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse || '')}</div>`;
    } else if (state.craftedSuggestion && state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse) {
      triggerBox.style.display = '';
      triggerBox.innerHTML = `
        <div class="post-trigger-title">suggestion installed</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-text">${escapeHtml(state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse)}</div>`;
    } else {
      triggerBox.style.display = 'none';
      triggerBox.innerHTML = '';
    }

    // For demonstration methods, remind user of the test
    if (method.category === 'demonstration' && !wasEmergency) {
      triggerBox.style.display = '';
      triggerBox.innerHTML += `<div style="margin-top:8px; padding-top:8px; border-top:1px solid var(--glass-border);">
        <div class="post-trigger-title" style="color:var(--accent-purple);">test now</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-text" style="font-size:0.82rem;">Try the ${escapeHtml(method.name)} effect now.</div>
      </div>`;
    }

    // Emergency cooldown (30s after emergency end)
    const statusIcon = $('postStatusIcon');
    if (wasEmergency) {
      state._cooldownUntil = Date.now() + 30000;
      if ($('groundingBox')) $('groundingBox').style.display = 'block';
      if (statusIcon) { statusIcon.textContent = '⚠'; statusIcon.style.color = 'var(--neon-amber)'; }
      if ($('postMessage')) $('postMessage').textContent = 'You ended early. That\'s okay — take a moment to re-orient.';
    } else {
      if ($('groundingBox')) $('groundingBox').style.display = 'none';
      if (statusIcon) { statusIcon.textContent = '✓'; statusIcon.style.color = 'var(--neon-cyan)'; }
      if ($('postMessage')) $('postMessage').textContent = 'Take a moment. Notice how you feel.';
    }

    // Reset post-session state controls
    const moodFeedback = $('moodFeedback');
    if (moodFeedback) moodFeedback.textContent = '';
  }

  function emergencyEnd() {
    if (state._finishing) return;
    state._finishing = true;
    state.abortFlag = true;
    // If currently paused, resume speech engine + drone + unpause state
    // so the rescue sequence can actually play
    if (state.paused) {
      state.paused = false;
      if (state._pauseStartedAt) {
        state._pausedTotalMs = (state._pausedTotalMs || 0) + (Date.now() - state._pauseStartedAt);
        state._pauseStartedAt = null;
      }
      try { speechSynthesis.resume(); } catch {}
      if (drone.ctx && drone.running) { try { drone.ctx.resume(); } catch {} }
      $('pauseBtn').textContent = 'pause';
    }
    speechSynthesis.cancel();
    // DEBUG: skip rescue sequence if debug checkbox is checked
    // This setting intentionally defaults OFF and is NOT saved with settings
    if (state._debug?.skipRescue || $('debugSkipRescue')?.checked) {
      sdLog('rescue skipped — debugSkipRescue on');
      finishSession(true);
      return;
    }
    const persona = getPersona();
    const reAlert = PERSONA_REALERTS[persona.id] ||
      "And now... \x5BPAUSE 2\x5D bringing your awareness back. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D Wiggling fingers and toes. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D Taking a deeper breath. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D Opening your eyes. Fully alert.";
    speakScript(reAlert, /* bypassAbort */ true).then(() => finishSession(true));
  }
  function togglePause() {
    state.paused = !state.paused;
    $('pauseBtn').textContent = state.paused ? 'resume' : 'pause';
    if (state.paused) {
      state._pauseStartedAt = Date.now();
      speechSynthesis.pause();
      if (drone.ctx && drone.running) drone.ctx.suspend();
      document.body.classList.remove('controls-hidden'); // always show controls when paused
      clearTimeout(_controlsTimer);
    } else {
      if (state._pauseStartedAt) {
        state._pausedTotalMs = (state._pausedTotalMs || 0) + (Date.now() - state._pauseStartedAt);
        state._pauseStartedAt = null;
      }
      speechSynthesis.resume();
      if (drone.ctx && drone.running) drone.ctx.resume();
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (!state.paused && !speechSynthesis.speaking && speechSynthesis.paused) {
          speechSynthesis.cancel();
        }
      }, 300);
      showSessionControls(); // restart auto-hide timer
    }
  }

  // HANDLERS + INIT
  // ====================================================================
  // Stepper clicks (only backward)
  $('stepper').addEventListener('click', e => {
    const item = e.target.closest('.step-item');
    if (!item || !item.classList.contains('clickable')) return;
    goToStep(parseInt(item.dataset.step));
  });
  $('btnNext').addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(state.currentStep + 1));
  $('btnBack').addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(state.currentStep - 1));
$('jumpGuideBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(1));
  $('jumpMethodBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(2));
  $('jumpIntentionBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(3));
  $('jumpAffirmationsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(4));
  $('jumpConfigBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(5)); // Step 5 is Configure; step 4 is Affirmations
  $('btnSkipToScript').addEventListener('click', () => {
    state._skippedToScript = true;
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.SKIP_SCRIPT);
    state.currentStep = 6;
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: false, 2: false, 3: false, 4: false, 5: false, 6: false };
    // Show the script editor area with empty textarea for pasting
    $('scriptText').value = '';
    $('scriptStats').innerHTML = 'Paste or type your script here. Use <code>===SETTLING===</code>, <code>===INDUCTION===</code>, etc. markers to define phases, or just paste plain text.';
    $('scriptPreview').classList.add('visible');
    // Hide generate button and summary since we skipped config
    showEl('generateScriptBtn', false);
    showEl('genProgress', false);
    updateStepUI();
    notify.info('Paste your script into the editor below, then press Begin Session. You can still jump back with the back button if you want the guided builder again.');
    // Focus the textarea
    setTimeout(() => $('scriptText')?.focus(), 300);
  });

  // scriptText input handler — updates state when user edits/pastes
  $('scriptText').addEventListener('input', () => {
    const text = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (text.length > 20) {
      if (state.fullScript && text !== state.fullScript.trim()) {
        _scriptEditedSinceGen = true;
      }
      state.fullScript = text;
      state.parsedScript = parseScript(text);
      state.generatedPhaseOrder = state.parsedScript.ordered || [];
      const spokenOnly = text.replace(/===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===/gi, ' ').replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, ' ');
      const words = spokenOnly.split(/\s+/).filter(w => w.length > 0).length;
      const pauses = (text.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi) || []).length;
      const pauseSecs = (text.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/gi) || []).reduce((sum, m) => sum + parseInt(m.match(/\d+/)[0], 10), 0);
      const phaseCount = (state.parsedScript.ordered || []).length;
      $('scriptStats').innerHTML = `<strong>${words}</strong> words · <strong>${pauses}</strong> pauses (${pauseSecs}s) · <strong>${phaseCount}</strong> phases · estimated: <strong>${Math.round(words / 50 + pauseSecs / 60)} min</strong><br>Edit below before starting.`;
      renderPhaseEditor();
    } else {
      state.fullScript = null;
      state.parsedScript = null;
      state.generatedPhaseOrder = [];
      renderPhaseEditor();
    }
    updateStepUI();
  });

  // Fix Timings button
  $('autoTempoBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.TIMING_FIX);
    const text = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (!text) { notify.warn('Generate or paste a script first.'); return; }
    const fixed = fixScriptTimings(text);
    $('scriptText').value = fixed;
    state.fullScript = fixed;
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(fixed);
    _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
    showScript();
    notify.success('Pause timings recalculated based on content.');
  });

  // Filter tabs
  $('personaFilterTabs').addEventListener('click', e => {
    if (!e.target.dataset.filter) return;
    state.personaFilter = e.target.dataset.filter;
    document.querySelectorAll('#personaFilterTabs .filter-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.filter === state.personaFilter));
    renderPersonaGrid();
  });
  $('methodFilterTabs').addEventListener('click', async e => {
    if (!e.target.dataset.filter) return;
    const cat = e.target.dataset.filter;
    // Practice-unlock gating: block locked categories
    if (cat === 'rapid' || cat === 'advanced') {
      const count = await getSessionCount();
      const threshold = cat === 'rapid' ? 3 : 7;
      if (count < threshold) {
        notify.info(`${cat.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + cat.slice(1)} methods unlock after ${threshold} completed sessions (${count} so far).`);
        return;
      }
    }
    state.methodFilter = cat;
    document.querySelectorAll('#methodFilterTabs .filter-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.filter === state.methodFilter));
    renderMethodGrid();
  });

  $('droneVolume').addEventListener('input', e => {

  $('vizSelect')?.addEventListener('change', e => {

  // Step 5 — HUD element toggles
  ['cfgFixationDot','cfgTextDisplay','cfgPhaseDots','cfgPhaseLabel','cfgProgressBar','cfgSessionTime','cfgLabels'].forEach(id => {

  // ── Playback + transition controls (backported from Slideshow) ──
  function buildBgTransitionGrid() {
    const grid = $('bgTransitionGrid');
    if (!grid) return;
    const enabled = new Set(state.bgEnabledTransitions || BG_DEFAULT_ENABLED);
    grid.innerHTML = Object.keys(BG_TRANSITIONS).map(k => {
      const checked = enabled.has(k) ? ' checked' : '';
      return `<label>
        <input type="checkbox" value="${k}"${checked}>
        <span>${BG_TRANSITIONS[k].label}</span>
      </label>`;
    }).join('');
  }
  function syncBgEnabledFromGrid() {
    const boxes = document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]');
    state.bgEnabledTransitions = Array.from(boxes).filter(b => b.checked).map(b => b.value);
    saveUserSettings();
  }
  buildBgTransitionGrid();

  $('bgTransitionGrid')?.addEventListener('change', syncBgEnabledFromGrid);
  $('bgTxAll')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(b => b.checked = true);
    syncBgEnabledFromGrid();
  });
  $('bgTxNone')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(b => b.checked = false);
    syncBgEnabledFromGrid();
  });
  $('bgTxInvert')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(b => b.checked = !b.checked);
    syncBgEnabledFromGrid();
  });

  $('bgOrderSeg')?.addEventListener('click', e => {
    const btn = e.target.closest('button[data-order]');
    if (!btn) return;
    state.bgPlaybackOrder = btn.dataset.order;
    $('bgOrderSeg').querySelectorAll('button').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('active', b === btn));
    saveUserSettings();
  });

  $('bgRotationSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.bgRotationSec = Number(e.target.value);
    const lbl = $('bgRotationVal'); if (lbl) lbl.textContent = state.bgRotationSec;
    const hint = $('bgRotationHint'); if (hint) hint.textContent = state.bgRotationSec;
  });
  $('bgRotationSlider')?.addEventListener('change', saveUserSettings);

  $('bgTransitionDurSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.bgTransitionDuration = Number(e.target.value);
    const lbl = $('bgTransitionDurVal'); if (lbl) lbl.textContent = state.bgTransitionDuration.toFixed(1);
  });
  $('bgTransitionDurSlider')?.addEventListener('change', saveUserSettings);

  // Background generate handler — single image.
  async function _bgGenerate() {
    const btn = $('bgPreviewBtn');
    const btn2 = $('bgPreviewBtn2');
    const wrap = $('bgPreviewWrap');
    const status = $('bgPreviewStatus');
    const grid = $('bgPreviewGrid');
    const saveBtn = $('bgSaveLastBtn');
    if (!wrap || !status || !grid || !btn) return;
    btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'generating...';
    if (btn2) { btn2.disabled = true; btn2.textContent = 'generating...'; }
    wrap.style.display = '';
    status.textContent = 'Sending to Perchance AI... (typically 10-30 seconds)';
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    if (saveBtn) saveBtn.style.display = 'none';
    bgEngine.prompt = $('bgPromptInput')?.value || '';
    const url = await bgEngine.generateOne();
    btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'generate image';
    if (btn2) { btn2.disabled = false; btn2.textContent = 'generate another'; }
    if (url) {
      const img = document.createElement('img');
      img.src = url;
      grid.appendChild(img);
      if (saveBtn) saveBtn.style.display = '';
      const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
      status.textContent = `Saved. ${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} in cache.`;
      renderBgGallery();
    } else {
      status.textContent = typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.textToImagePlugin
        ? 'Generation failed — server may be busy. Try again.'
        : 'Plugin not found. Add textToImagePlugin = {import:text-to-image-plugin} to the top editor.';
    }
  }

  // Batch generate — fires 4 in parallel, populates grid progressively.
  async function _bgGenerateBatch() {
    const batchBtn = $('bgPreviewBatchBtn');
    const wrap = $('bgPreviewWrap');
    const status = $('bgPreviewStatus');
    const grid = $('bgPreviewGrid');
    if (!batchBtn || !wrap || !status || !grid) return;
    batchBtn.disabled = true; batchBtn.textContent = 'generating 4...';
    wrap.style.display = '';
    status.textContent = 'Generating 4 images in parallel...';
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    bgEngine.prompt = $('bgPromptInput')?.value || '';
    // Fire 4 in parallel; render each as it arrives rather than waiting for all.
    let completed = 0;
    const promises = Array.from({ length: 4 }, () =>
      bgEngine.generateOne().then(url => {
        completed++;
        if (url) {
          const img = document.createElement('img');
          img.src = url;
          grid.appendChild(img);
        }
        status.textContent = `${completed} of 4 complete...`;
      })
    );
    await Promise.all(promises);
    batchBtn.disabled = false; batchBtn.textContent = 'generate 4 (parallel)';
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    status.textContent = `Batch done. ${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} in cache.`;
    renderBgGallery();
  }

  $('bgPreviewBtn')?.addEventListener('click', _bgGenerate);
  $('bgPreviewBtn2')?.addEventListener('click', _bgGenerate);
  $('bgPreviewBatchBtn')?.addEventListener('click', _bgGenerateBatch);
  $('bgSaveLastBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    if (manifest.length > 0) {
      await bgCacheDownload(manifest[manifest.length - 1].id);
      notify.success('Image saved to your device.');
    }
  });
  $('bgManageBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { renderBgGallery(); $('bgGalleryModal')?.classList.add('visible'); });
  $('bgGalleryCloseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => $('bgGalleryModal')?.classList.remove('visible'));

    if (!await confirmAsync('Clear all cached background images?')) return;
    await bgCacheClear(); renderBgGallery(); notify.info('Background cache cleared.');
  });
  $('bgDownloadAllBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    if (!manifest.length) { notify.info('No images to download.'); return; }
    notify.info(`Downloading ${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}...`);
    for (const entry of manifest) {
      await bgCacheDownload(entry.id);
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300)); // stagger to avoid browser blocking
    }
  });

    saveUserSettings();
  });

  $('bgUrlInput')?.addEventListener('input', e => { state.bgStaticUrl = e.target.value; saveUserSettings(); });

  // Slider batch save — fires only on release (change), not every drag tick (input)

    state.duckingEnabled = e.target.checked;

    $(id)?.addEventListener('input', e => {
      state.vizSettings[key] = parseInt(e.target.value, 10) / 100;
      const v = $(id + 'Val'); if (v) v.textContent = state.vizSettings[key].toFixed(decimals) + suffix;
    });
    $(id)?.addEventListener('change', () => saveUserSettings());

  $('addWorkPhaseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => addPhaseSection('work'));
  $('addAffirmPhaseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => addPhaseSection('affirm'));
  $('addLightenerPhaseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => addPhaseSection('lightener'));

  // Pre-session mood emoji buttons
  document.querySelectorAll('.mood-emoji').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      document.querySelectorAll('.mood-emoji').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
      btn.classList.add('selected');
      state._preMood = parseInt(btn.dataset.val, 10);
    });

  // Pre-session tension and energy sliders
  $('preTensionSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state._preTension = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('preTensionVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
  });
  $('preEnergySlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state._preEnergy = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('preEnergyVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
  });

  // Post-session mood slider (0-10)
  $('postStateSlider')?.addEventListener('input', async e => {
    const val = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('postStateVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
    const fb = $('moodFeedback');
    const delta = val - (state._preMood ?? 5);
    if (fb) fb.textContent = delta > 0 ? `+${delta} improvement` : delta === 0 ? 'same as before' : `${delta} — be gentle with yourself`;
    // Save to most recent session record
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    if (history.length > 0) {
      history[0].postMood = val;
      history[0].preMood = state._preMood ?? null;
      history[0].preTension = state._preTension ?? null;
      history[0].preEnergy = state._preEnergy ?? null;
      history[0].depth = parseInt($('depthSlider')?.value ?? 5, 10);
      await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', history);
    }
    recordPostMood(val);
    // Retroactively correct adaptive reward now that real postMood is known
    try {
      const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
      const h = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
      if (h.length > 0 && adaptive.ts > 0) {
        const rec = h[0];
        const oldReward = ((5) - (rec.preMood ?? 5)) + (rec.completed ? 1 : -1);
        const newReward = (val - (rec.preMood ?? 5)) + (rec.completed ? 1 : -1);
        const correction = newReward - oldReward;
        if (Math.abs(correction) > 0.01) {
          const bump = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + correction; };
          bump(adaptive.w.p, rec.personaId); bump(adaptive.w.m, rec.methodId);
          bump(adaptive.w.s, rec.soundscape); bump(adaptive.w.ln, rec.length);
          await idbSet(ADAPTIVE_KEY, adaptive);
        }
      }
    } catch {}
  });

  // Depth slider
  $('depthSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    const el = $('depthVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
  });

  // Alertness check — auto-trigger grounding if low
  $('alertnessSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    const val = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('alertnessVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
    // Howard Alertness Scale: if alertness < 5, show grounding exercise
    const groundingBox = $('groundingBox');
    if (groundingBox) {
      if (val < 5) {
        groundingBox.style.display = 'block';
        if ($('moodFeedback')) $('moodFeedback').textContent = 'You seem drowsy — please do the grounding exercise before standing up.';
      } else {
        groundingBox.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
  });

    if (!await confirmAsync('Stop the session and return to the script editor?')) return;
    state.abortFlag = true;
    state._finishing = true;            // prevent playback loop from calling finishSession
    state.paused = false;               // don't inherit paused state into next session
    clearInterval(state._timeInterval); // stop elapsed timer
    clearTimeout(state._safetyTimeout); // prevent ghost post-screen switch
    state._sessionStartTime = null;
    speechSynthesis.cancel();
    drone.stop(); stopVisuals();
    setSleepOverlay(false);
    bgEngine.clear();
    stopRecording();
    closeLivePanel();
    // Clear lock-screen media session
    if ('mediaSession' in navigator) {
      try {
        navigator.mediaSession.metadata = null;
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('play', null);
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('pause', null);
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('stop', null);
      } catch {}
    }
    try { state._wakeLock?.release(); } catch(e) {}
    document.body.classList.remove('in-session'); document.body.classList.remove('controls-hidden'); clearTimeout(_controlsTimer);
    switchScreen('setup-wizard');
    goToStep(6); // Step 6 is Generate (holds scriptText); Step 5 is Configure
    notify.info('Session stopped. You can edit the script and restart.');
  });
  $('restartBtn').addEventListener('click', () => resetWizardForNewSession({ preserveSelections: true }));

    switchScreen('setup-wizard');

  $('postBackToScriptBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    switchScreen('setup-wizard');
    goToStep(6); // Step 6 is Generate (holds scriptText); Step 5 is Configure
  });

  $('fullscreenBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const stage = $('stage');
    if (!stage) return;
    if (document.fullscreenElement) {
      document.exitFullscreen().catch(() => {});
    } else {
      // Try standard first, fall back to webkit. Each returns a promise that can reject
      // (user denied, iframe blocked, etc.) — swallow to avoid uncaught-rejection warnings.
      const req = stage.requestFullscreen?.() ?? stage.webkitRequestFullscreen?.();
      if (req && typeof req.catch === 'function') req.catch(() => {});
    }
  });
  document.addEventListener('fullscreenchange', () => {
    const btn = $('fullscreenBtn');
    if (btn) btn.textContent = document.fullscreenElement ? '⛶ exit' : '⛶ fullscreen';
  });

  // ── Live Settings Panel ────────────────────────────────────────────
  function openLivePanel() {
    const panel = $('livePanel');
    const overlay = $('livePanelOverlay');
    if (!panel) return;
    // Sync controls to current state before opening
    const $v = (id, val) => { const el = $(id); if (el) el.value = val; };
    $v('liveVizSelect', state.vizOverride === 'auto' ? (getMethod().visual) : state.vizOverride);
    $v('liveSoundscapeSelect', state.soundscape);
    $v('liveSoundVol', Math.round(state.droneVolume * 100));
    $v('liveVoiceSpeed', Math.round(state.speechRate * 100));
    $v('liveVoicePitch', Math.round((state.voicePitch || 0.85) * 100));
    $v('liveVoiceVol', Math.round((state.voiceVolume ?? 1) * 100));
    $('liveSoundVolVal').textContent = Math.round(state.droneVolume * 100);
    $('liveVoiceSpeedVal').textContent = state.speechRate.toFixed(2) + '×';
    $('liveVoicePitchVal').textContent = (state.voicePitch || 0.85).toFixed(2);
    $('liveVoiceVolVal').textContent = Math.round((state.voiceVolume ?? 1) * 100);
    $v('liveTempo', Math.round((state.tempoMultiplier || 1) * 100));
    $('liveTempoVal').textContent = (state.tempoMultiplier || 1).toFixed(1) + '×';
    // Sync HUD toggles
    const hudMap = { liveFixDot:'fixationDot', liveText:'textDisplay', livePhaseDots:'phaseDots', livePhaseLabel:'phaseLabel', liveProgress:'progressBar', liveTime:'sessionTime', liveLabels:'labels' };
    for (const [elId, key] of Object.entries(hudMap)) {
      const el = $(elId); if (el) el.checked = state.hud[key] !== false;
    }
    // Sync background controls
    const bgSection = $('liveBgSection');
    if (bgSection) bgSection.style.display = bgEngine.source !== 'none' ? '' : 'none';
    const bgToggle = $('liveBgToggle'); if (bgToggle) bgToggle.checked = $('bgLayer')?.style.display !== 'none';
    panel.classList.add('open');
    if (overlay) overlay.classList.add('open');
  }
  function closeLivePanel() {
    $('livePanel')?.classList.remove('open');
    $('livePanelOverlay')?.classList.remove('open');
  }

  $('liveSettingsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const panel = $('livePanel');
    if (panel?.classList.contains('open')) closeLivePanel(); else openLivePanel();
  });
  $('livePanelClose')?.addEventListener('click', closeLivePanel);
  $('livePanelOverlay')?.addEventListener('click', closeLivePanel);

  // Live visual switch — tear down and rebuild mid-session
  $('liveVizSelect')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    const viz = e.target.value;
    state.vizOverride = viz;
    if (viz === 'none') {
      stopVisuals();
      const stage = $('stage');
      Array.from(stage.children).forEach(c => {
        if (!c.classList.contains('fixation-dot') && !c.classList.contains('audio-indicator')
          && !c.classList.contains('persona-indicator') && !c.classList.contains('method-indicator')
          && !c.classList.contains('session-progress-wrap') && !c.classList.contains('transcript-panel')) c.remove();
      });
    } else if (viz === 'pulse' || viz === 'spiral') {
      stopVisuals(); setupVisual(viz);
    } else {
      stopVisuals(); setupVisual(viz);
    }
  });

  // Live soundscape switch — stop and restart with new type
  $('liveSoundscapeSelect')?.addEventListener('change', async e => {
    const type = e.target.value;
    state.soundscape = type;
    state.droneEnabled = type !== 'none';
    state._soundscapeOverridden = true;
    // Sync the Configure-step select so the two stay aligned
    const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (ssSelect) ssSelect.value = type;
    saveUserSettings();
    await drone.stop();
    if (type !== 'none') {
      await drone.start(state.droneVolume, type);
      const ai = $('audioIndicator');
      if (ai) ai.textContent = '· ' + type + ' ·';
    } else {
      const ai = $('audioIndicator');
      if (ai) ai.textContent = '';
    }
  });

  // Live audio sliders
  $('liveSoundVol')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.droneVolume = parseInt(e.target.value,10)/100; drone.setVolume(state.droneVolume);
    $('liveSoundVolVal').textContent = e.target.value;
  });
  $('liveVoiceSpeed')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.speechRate = parseInt(e.target.value,10)/100;
    $('liveVoiceSpeedVal').textContent = (parseInt(e.target.value,10)/100).toFixed(2) + '×';
  });
  $('liveVoicePitch')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.voicePitch = parseInt(e.target.value,10)/100;
    $('liveVoicePitchVal').textContent = (parseInt(e.target.value,10)/100).toFixed(2);
  });
  $('liveVoiceVol')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.voiceVolume = parseInt(e.target.value,10)/100;
    $('liveVoiceVolVal').textContent = e.target.value;
  });
  $('liveTempo')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.tempoMultiplier = parseInt(e.target.value, 10) / 100;
    const v = $('liveTempoVal'); if (v) v.textContent = state.tempoMultiplier.toFixed(1) + '×';
    // Sync Configure-tab slider (Step 5)

    const s4v = $('tempoVal'); if (s4v) s4v.textContent = state.tempoMultiplier.toFixed(1) + '×';
    saveUserSettings();
  });

  // Live background controls
  $('liveBgToggle')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    const layer = $('bgLayer');
    if (layer) layer.style.display = e.target.checked ? '' : 'none';
    if (e.target.checked) document.body.classList.add('bg-active');
    else document.body.classList.remove('bg-active');
  });
  $('liveBgOpacity')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    const val = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const v = $('liveBgOpacityVal'); if (v) v.textContent = val + '%';
    document.querySelectorAll('.bg-img.active').forEach(img => { img.style.opacity = val / 100; });
    document.querySelectorAll('.bg-video').forEach(vid => { vid.style.opacity = val / 100; });
  });

  // Live HUD toggles — apply immediately during session
  const liveHudMap = { liveFixDot:'fixationDot', liveText:'textDisplay', livePhaseDots:'phaseDots', livePhaseLabel:'phaseLabel', liveProgress:'progressBar', liveTime:'sessionTime', liveLabels:'labels' };
  const liveHudElements = { fixationDot:'fixationDot', textDisplay:'textDisplay', phaseDots:'phaseDots', phaseLabel:'phaseIndicator', progressBar:null, sessionTime:'sessionTime', labels:null };

  for (const [elId, key] of Object.entries(liveHudMap)) {
    $(elId)?.addEventListener('change', e => {
      state.hud[key] = e.target.checked;
      // Also update the Step 5 checkboxes to stay in sync
      const cfgId = 'cfg' + key.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + key.slice(1);
      const cfgEl = $(cfgId); if (cfgEl) cfgEl.checked = e.target.checked;
      // Apply visibility immediately
      const targetId = liveHudElements[key];
      if (targetId) {
        const el = $(targetId); if (el) el.style.display = e.target.checked ? '' : 'none';
      }
      // Special cases
      if (key === 'progressBar') {
        document.querySelector('.session-progress-wrap')?.style.setProperty('display', e.target.checked ? '' : 'none');
      }
      if (key === 'labels') {
        ['personaIndicator','methodIndicator','audioIndicator'].forEach(id => {
          const el = $(id); if (el) el.style.display = e.target.checked ? '' : 'none';
        });
      }
    });
  }

  // Keyboard controls during session
  document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if ($('session-screen').style.display === 'none') return;
    if (e.target.tagName === 'INPUT' || e.target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') return;
    if (e.code === 'Space') { e.preventDefault(); togglePause(); }
    if (e.key === 'Escape') { e.preventDefault(); emergencyEnd(); }
    showSessionControls(); // any key shows controls
  });

  // Auto-hide session controls after 5s of inactivity
  var _controlsTimer = null;
  function showSessionControls() {
    document.body.classList.remove('controls-hidden');
    clearTimeout(_controlsTimer);
    if (state._sessionStartTime && !state.abortFlag && !state.paused) {
      _controlsTimer = setTimeout(() => document.body.classList.add('controls-hidden'), 5000);
    }
  }
  document.addEventListener('mousemove', () => {
    if ($('session-screen')?.style.display !== 'none') showSessionControls();
  });
  document.addEventListener('touchstart', () => {
    if ($('session-screen')?.style.display !== 'none') showSessionControls();
  }, { passive: true });

  // Wake Lock re-acquire + pause/resume on visibility change
  document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', async () => {
    if (document.visibilityState === 'visible' && state._sessionStartTime && !state.abortFlag) {
      // Re-acquire wake lock
      try {
        if (navigator.wakeLock && !state._wakeLock) {
          state._wakeLock = await navigator.wakeLock.request('screen');
          state._wakeLock.addEventListener('release', () => { state._wakeLock = null; });
        }
      } catch(e) {}
      // Resume audio context if suspended — but NOT if user explicitly paused the session
      if (!state.paused && drone.ctx?.state === 'suspended') { try { await drone.ctx.resume(); } catch(e) {} }
    } else if (document.visibilityState === 'hidden' && state._sessionStartTime && !state.abortFlag) {
      // Suspend audio context to save battery when tab hidden
      if (drone.ctx?.state === 'running') { try { drone.ctx.suspend(); } catch(e) {} }
    }
  });

  // Post-session save

  // Voice preview with stop
  $('voicePreviewBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
    const voice = getSelectedVoice();
    const samples = [
      "And now... noticing the weight of your hands... just resting there...",
      "Each breath carrying you a little deeper now... that's right...",
      "The sound of my voice becoming the only thing that matters...",
      "Drifting comfortably... nowhere to be... nothing to do...",
    ];
    const sample = samples[Math.floor(Math.random() * samples.length)];
    if (!('speechSynthesis' in window)) { notify.info('Text-to-speech is not available in this browser.'); return; }
    speechSynthesis.cancel();
    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(sample);
    u.voice = voice; u.rate = state.speechRate; u.pitch = state.voicePitch || 0.85; u.volume = state.voiceVolume ?? 1.0;
    u.onend = () => { _voicePreviewing = false; togglePreviewBtns('voice', false); };
    u.onerror = u.onend;
    speechSynthesis.speak(u);
    _voicePreviewing = true;
    togglePreviewBtns('voice', true);
  });
  $('voiceStopBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    speechSynthesis.cancel();
    _voicePreviewing = false;
    togglePreviewBtns('voice', false);
  });

  // Voice select change → update info
  $('voiceSelect').addEventListener('change', async () => { updateVoiceInfo(); state._savedVoiceName = $('voiceSelect').value; saveUserSettings(); try { if (_kv) await _kv.settings.set(SETTINGS_KEY, _buildSettingsObj()); } catch {} });

  // Soundscape preview
  $('soundPreviewBtn')?.addEventListener('click', previewSoundscape);
  $('soundStopBtn')?.addEventListener('click', stopSoundscapePreview);

  // Viz preview
  $('vizPreviewBtn')?.addEventListener('click', startVizPreview);
  $('vizStopBtn')?.addEventListener('click', stopVizPreview);

  // Stop all previews when leaving Step 5 (Configure)
  const _stopAllPreviews = () => { stopVizPreview(); stopSoundscapePreview(); if (_voicePreviewing) { speechSynthesis.cancel(); _voicePreviewing = false; togglePreviewBtns('voice', false); } };

  // ====================================================================
  // CAPABILITY DETECTION (from Studio capabilities.js)
  // ====================================================================
  const caps = { tts: false, webAudio: false, wakeLock: false, fullscreen: false, vibration: false };
  function detectCaps() {
    caps.tts = 'speechSynthesis' in window;
    caps.webAudio = 'AudioContext' in window || 'webkitAudioContext' in window;
    caps.wakeLock = 'wakeLock' in navigator;
    caps.fullscreen = 'requestFullscreen' in document.documentElement || 'webkitRequestFullscreen' in document.documentElement;
    caps.vibration = 'vibrate' in navigator;
    const missing = [];
    if (!caps.tts) missing.push('Text-to-speech is not available — sessions will be visual only.');
    if (!caps.webAudio) missing.push('Web Audio is not available — no soundscapes.');
    if (missing.length) notify.warn(missing.join(' '));
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // QUICK-START PRESETS
  // ====================================================================
  // ====================================================================
  // FIRST-RUN SAFETY / CONTRAINDICATION SCREEN
  // ====================================================================
  // Safety contraindication info moved to Help & Safety Resources button in sidebar

  // ====================================================================
  // RISING-SCORE SPARKLINE (renders pre/post improvement over sessions)
  // ====================================================================
  async function renderSparkline() {
    const wrap = $('sessionStatsPanel');
    if (!wrap) return;
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    // Filter sessions with both pre and post scores
    const scored = history.filter(s => s.preMood != null && s.postMood != null).slice(0, 20).reverse();
    if (scored.length < 2) return; // Need at least 2 data points

    // Append canvas if not already there
    let sparkWrap = $('sparklineWrap');
    if (!sparkWrap) {
      sparkWrap = document.createElement('div');
      sparkWrap.id = 'sparklineWrap';
      sparkWrap.className = 'sparkline-wrap';
      sparkWrap.innerHTML = '<div class="mood-label">your state improvement over sessions</div><canvas class="sparkline-canvas" id="sparklineCanvas"></canvas>';
      wrap.appendChild(sparkWrap);
    }
    const canvas = $('sparklineCanvas');
    if (!canvas) return;
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth || 280;
    canvas.height = 60;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    const W = canvas.width, H = canvas.height;

    // Pre scores (grey), post scores (accent), delta line (green)
    const pad = 8;
    const xStep = (W - pad * 2) / (scored.length - 1);

    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

    // Draw pre scores (dim)
    ctx.beginPath();
    scored.forEach((s, i) => {
      const x = pad + i * xStep, y = H - pad - (s.preMood / 10) * (H - pad * 2);
      i === 0 ? ctx.moveTo(x, y) : ctx.lineTo(x, y);
    });
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(107,148,184,0.25)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1; ctx.stroke();

    // Draw post scores (bright)
    ctx.beginPath();
    scored.forEach((s, i) => {
      const x = pad + i * xStep, y = H - pad - (s.postMood / 10) * (H - pad * 2);
      i === 0 ? ctx.moveTo(x, y) : ctx.lineTo(x, y);
    });
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(107,184,130,0.7)'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();

    // Dots on post scores
    scored.forEach((s, i) => {
      const x = pad + i * xStep, y = H - pad - (s.postMood / 10) * (H - pad * 2);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x, y, 2.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(107,184,130,0.9)'; ctx.fill();
    });
  }

  }

  function renderPresets() {
    const grid = $('presetGrid');
    if (!grid) return;
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    PRESETS.forEach(p => {
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = 'preset-card';
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="preset-icon">${p.icon}</div><div class="preset-name">${escapeHtml(p.name)}</div><div class="preset-desc">${escapeHtml(p.desc)}</div>`;
      card.addEventListener('click', () => applyPreset(p));
      grid.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  function applyPreset(p) {
    state.selectedPersonaId = p.persona; state.selectedMethodId = p.method;
    state.intentionType = p.intention; state.length = p.length;
    state.soundscape = p.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = p.soundscape !== 'none';
    if (p.vizOverride) { state.vizOverride = p.vizOverride; const ve = $('vizSelect'); if (ve) ve.value = p.vizOverride; }
    $('intentionType').value = p.intention;
    $('lengthSelect').value = p.length;
    const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect');
    if (ssSelect) ssSelect.value = p.soundscape;
    renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
    updateIntentionHint(); updateStepUI();
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: false, 5: false, 6: false };
    goToStep(4);
    notify.success(`Preset "${p.name}" loaded — configure and generate.`);
  }

  async function getActiveProgramState() {
    return (await idbGet('stillness_program_v1')) || null;
  }
  async function saveActiveProgramState(ps) {
    await idbSet('stillness_program_v1', ps);
  }

  async function renderPrograms() {
    const grid = $('programGrid');
    const activePanel = $('programActivePanel');
    if (!grid) return;

    const active = await getActiveProgramState();

    // Show active program status
    if (active && activePanel) {
      const prog = PROGRAMS.find(p => p.id === active.programId);
      if (prog) {
        const pct = Math.round((active.currentDay / prog.days) * 100);
        const todayFocus = prog.arc ? prog.arc[Math.min(active.currentDay, prog.arc.length - 1)] : `Day ${active.currentDay + 1}`;
        activePanel.innerHTML = `
          <div class="detail-panel" style="margin-bottom:12px;">
            <div class="detail-title">${prog.icon} ${escapeHtml(prog.name)} — Day ${active.currentDay + 1} of ${prog.days}</div>
            <div style="font-size:0.75rem;color:var(--text-dim);margin:6px 0;">Today's focus: <strong>${escapeHtml(todayFocus)}</strong></div>
            <div class="session-progress-wrap" style="position:relative;height:4px;margin:8px 0;"><div class="session-progress-fill" style="width:${pct}%;"></div></div>
            <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:8px;">
              <button class="btn secondary" id="programContinueBtn" style="flex:1;font-size:0.82rem;">continue program →</button>
              <button class="btn secondary" id="programQuitBtn" style="font-size:0.82rem;color:#8a5a58;">quit program</button>
            </div>
          </div>`;
        $('programContinueBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => startProgramDay(prog, active));
        $('programQuitBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
          if (await confirmAsync(`Quit "${prog.name}"? Your progress (Day ${active.currentDay + 1}) will be lost.`)) {
            await idbSet('stillness_program_v1', null);
            renderPrograms();
          }
        });
      }
    } else if (activePanel) {
      activePanel.innerHTML = '';
    }

    // Show program cards
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    PROGRAMS.forEach(prog => {
      const isActive = active?.programId === prog.id;
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = 'preset-card' + (isActive ? ' selected' : '');
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="preset-icon">${prog.icon}</div><div class="preset-name">${escapeHtml(prog.name)}</div><div class="preset-desc">${prog.days} days · ${escapeHtml(prog.desc)}</div>`;
      card.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        if (isActive) { startProgramDay(prog, active); return; }
        if (active) { if (!await confirmAsync('Starting a new program will replace your current one. Continue?')) return; }
        const newState = { programId: prog.id, currentDay: 0, startedAt: Date.now(), anchors: [], completedDays: [] };
        await saveActiveProgramState(newState);
        renderPrograms();
        notify.success(`Started "${prog.name}" — Day 1 of ${prog.days}.`);
      });
      grid.appendChild(card);
    });
  }

  function startProgramDay(prog, ps) {
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.PROGRAMS);
    // Apply program settings (base)
    state.selectedPersonaId = prog.persona; state.selectedMethodId = prog.method;
    state.intentionType = prog.intention; state.length = prog.length;
    state.soundscape = prog.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = prog.soundscape !== 'none';
    if (prog.vizOverride) { state.vizOverride = prog.vizOverride; const ve = $('vizSelect'); if (ve) ve.value = prog.vizOverride; }
    // Apply per-day overrides (soundscape, visual, method variety across the program)
    const dayNum = ps.currentDay + 1;
    const overrides = prog.dayOverrides?.[dayNum];
    if (overrides) {
      if (overrides.soundscape) { state.soundscape = overrides.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = overrides.soundscape !== 'none'; }
      if (overrides.vizOverride) { state.vizOverride = overrides.vizOverride; const ve = $('vizSelect'); if (ve) ve.value = overrides.vizOverride; }
      if (overrides.method) state.selectedMethodId = overrides.method;
      if (overrides.persona) state.selectedPersonaId = overrides.persona;
    }
    $('intentionType').value = prog.intention;
    $('lengthSelect').value = prog.length;
    const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (ssSelect) ssSelect.value = state.soundscape;

    // Set the intention input with program context
    const dayFocus = prog.arc ? prog.arc[Math.min(ps.currentDay, (prog.arc?.length || 1) - 1)] : `Day ${dayNum} of structured ${prog.name} program`;
    const anchors = Array.isArray(ps.anchors) ? ps.anchors : [];
    const anchorContext = anchors.length ? `Prior anchors: ${anchors.join(', ')}. ` : '';
    $('intentionInput').value = `${anchorContext}Day ${dayNum} of ${prog.days}: ${dayFocus}`;

    state._activeProgram = { prog, ps };
    renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
    updateIntentionHint(); updateStepUI();
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: false, 5: false, 6: false };
    goToStep(4);
    notify.success(`Day ${dayNum}: ${dayFocus}`);
  }

  // Advance program after successful session completion
  async function advanceProgramDay() {
    if (!state._activeProgram) return;
    const { prog, ps } = state._activeProgram;
    ps.currentDay = Math.min(ps.currentDay + 1, prog.days);
    if (!Array.isArray(ps.completedDays)) ps.completedDays = [];
    ps.completedDays.push(Date.now());
    await saveActiveProgramState(ps);
    if (ps.currentDay >= prog.days) {
      notify.success(`🎉 Congratulations! You completed "${prog.name}".`);
      await idbSet('stillness_program_v1', null); // Clear completed program
    }
    state._activeProgram = null;
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // MEDIA SESSION API — lock-screen controls for mobile
  // ====================================================================
  function setMediaSession(playing) {
    if (!('mediaSession' in navigator)) return;
    const persona = getPersona(), method = getMethod();
    navigator.mediaSession.metadata = new MediaMetadata({
      title: method.name + ' — ' + (state.length),
      artist: persona.name,
      album: 'Stillness Generator',
    });
    navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('play', () => { if (state.paused) togglePause(); });
    navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('pause', () => { if (!state.paused) togglePause(); });
    navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('stop', () => emergencyEnd());
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // ACTIVITY HEATMAP (from Studio metrics-history.js)
  // ====================================================================
  async function renderHeatmap() {
    const wrap = $('heatmapWrap');
    if (!wrap) return;
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    if (history.length === 0) { wrap.innerHTML = ''; return; }

    // Build day→count map for the last 16 weeks (112 days)
    const dayCounts = {};
    history.forEach(s => {
      const d = new Date(s.date); d.setHours(0,0,0,0);
      const key = d.toISOString().slice(0,10);
      dayCounts[key] = (dayCounts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });

    const today = new Date(); today.setHours(0,0,0,0);
    const dayMs = 86400000;
    // Start from 15 weeks ago, aligned to Monday
    const startDay = new Date(today.getTime() - 15 * 7 * dayMs);
    startDay.setDate(startDay.getDate() - ((startDay.getDay() + 6) % 7)); // Monday

    let html = '<div class="heatmap">';
    let d = new Date(startDay);
    while (d <= today) {
      html += '<div class="heatmap-col">';
      for (let row = 0; row < 7 && d <= today; row++) {
        const key = d.toISOString().slice(0,10);
        const count = dayCounts[key] || 0;
        const level = count === 0 ? 0 : count === 1 ? 1 : count === 2 ? 2 : count <= 4 ? 3 : 4;
        const title = `${key}: ${count} session${count !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
        html += `<div class="heatmap-cell" data-count="${level}" title="${title}"></div>`;
        d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1);
      }
      html += '</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';
    wrap.innerHTML = html;
  }

    { icon: '✨', title: 'You\'re ready', body: 'Pick a guide and method, or tap a preset. Your first session takes about 2 minutes to set up. Backup your data anytime from the sidebar. The <strong>help &amp; safety resources</strong> button in the sidebar has crisis resources.' },
  ];

  function shouldShowTour() { try { return !localStorage.getItem(TOUR_KEY); } catch { return false; } }
  function markTourSeen() { try { localStorage.setItem(TOUR_KEY, '1'); } catch {} }

  function startTour() {
    let step = 0;
    const overlay = document.createElement('div'); overlay.className = 'tour-overlay';
    const card = document.createElement('div'); card.className = 'tour-card';
    document.body.appendChild(overlay); document.body.appendChild(card);

    function render() {
      const s = TOUR_STEPS[step];
      const isLast = step === TOUR_STEPS.length - 1;
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div style="font-size:1.4rem;margin-bottom:8px;">${s.icon}</div>
        <h3>${s.title}</h3>
        <p>${s.body}</p>
        <div class="tour-dots">${TOUR_STEPS.map((_,i) => `<div class="tour-dot${i===step?' active':''}"></div>`).join('')}</div>
        <div class="tour-actions">
          <button class="tour-skip" id="tourSkip">${isLast ? '' : 'skip tour'}</button>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;">
            ${step > 0 ? '<button class="tour-next" id="tourBack" style="background:transparent;border:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--text-dim);">← back</button>' : ''}
            <button class="tour-next" id="tourNext">${isLast ? 'done ✓' : 'next →'}</button>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      $('tourSkip')?.addEventListener('click', dismiss);
      $('tourBack')?.addEventListener('click', () => { step--; render(); });
      $('tourNext')?.addEventListener('click', () => { if (isLast) dismiss(); else { step++; render(); } });
    }

    function dismiss() {
      markTourSeen(); overlay.remove(); card.remove();
      document.removeEventListener('keydown', kh);
    }
    const kh = e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') dismiss(); if (e.key === 'ArrowRight' && step < TOUR_STEPS.length-1) { step++; render(); } if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft' && step > 0) { step--; render(); } };
    document.addEventListener('keydown', kh);
    render();
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // VIBRATION HAPTICS (breathing feedback for supported devices)
  // ====================================================================
  function vibrateBreath() {
    // 4-7-8 breathing haptic: inhale pulse, hold, exhale pulse, hold
    if (caps.vibration) navigator.vibrate([400, 3600, 400, 7600]);
  }
  function vibrateSessionMarker() {
    if (caps.vibration) navigator.vibrate([100, 50, 100]);
  }

  // Crisis resources — accessible from footer at any time
  $('crisisLink')?.addEventListener('click', e => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const msg = 'If you are in crisis or experiencing distress:\n\n' +
      '🇺🇸 USA: 988 Suicide & Crisis Lifeline — call or text 988\n' +
      '🇬🇧 UK/IE: Samaritans — 116 123 (free, 24/7)\n' +
      '🇦🇺 Australia: Lifeline — 13 11 14\n' +
      '🇨🇦 Canada: Talk Suicide — 1-833-456-4566\n' +
      '🌍 International: findahelpline.com\n\n' +
      'This tool is not a substitute for professional care.';
    alertModal('Crisis Resources', msg);
  });

  // Sidebar toggle (mobile)
  $('sidebarToggle')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    $('sidebar')?.classList.toggle('open');
    $('sidebarOverlay')?.classList.toggle('open');
  });
  $('sidebarOverlay')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    $('sidebar')?.classList.remove('open');
    $('sidebarOverlay')?.classList.remove('open');
  });
  function openRemoteConsentModal() { $('remoteConsentModal')?.classList.add('visible'); }
  function closeRemoteConsentModal() { $('remoteConsentModal')?.classList.remove('visible'); }

  // Options modal
  $('openOptionsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => $('optionsModal')?.classList.add('visible'));
  $('optionsCloseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => $('optionsModal')?.classList.remove('visible'));

  // External AI provider selection
  $('extAiProvider')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    state.extAiProvider = e.target.value;
    $('extAiKeyRow').style.display = e.target.value === 'perchance' ? 'none' : '';
  });
  $('extAiKey')?.addEventListener('input', e => { state._extAiKey = e.target.value || null; });

  // Debug mode — all flags session-only, never persisted. Any change triggers a
  // re-sync of state._debug and re-renders the floating "DEBUG" banner.
  $('debugSkipRescue')?.addEventListener('change', () => {
    _syncDebugState();
    const memBtn = $('viewMemoriesBtn');
    if (memBtn) memBtn.style.display = $('debugSkipRescue')?.checked ? '' : 'none';
  });
  $('debugSkipCooldown')?.addEventListener('change', _syncDebugState);
  $('debugSkipSafetyGate')?.addEventListener('change', _syncDebugState);
  $('debugSkipMethodGating')?.addEventListener('change', () => {
    _syncDebugState();
    applyMethodGating(); // re-evaluate the visible tab locks immediately
  });
  $('debugVerbose')?.addEventListener('change', _syncDebugState);

  // ── Memories modal (Perchance-chat style: editable cards) ──
  async function renderMemoriesModal() {
    const memory = await getMemory();
    const container = $('memoriesContainer');
    if (!container) return;
    const cards = [];
    // Tier 3 — long-term profile
    cards.push({ tier: 'long-term profile', key: 'longTermProfile', text: memory.longTermProfile || '', placeholder: 'Generated after 15+ sessions. Describes your overall practice patterns.', nodelet: false });
    // Tier 2 — rolling analysis
    cards.push({ tier: 'rolling analysis', key: 'rollingWindow', text: memory.rollingWindow || '', placeholder: 'Generated after 5+ sessions. What works and what to avoid.', nodelet: false });
    // Tier 1 — session digests (individual cards)
    memory.sessionDigests.forEach((d, i) => {
      cards.push({ tier: `session · ${new Date(d.date).toLocaleDateString()}`, key: 'digest', idx: i, text: d.digest || '', placeholder: 'Session summary...', date: d.date, depth: d.depth, moodDelta: d.moodDelta, nodelet: true });
    });
    container.innerHTML = cards.map((c, ci) => `
      <div class="memory-card" data-ci="${ci}" data-key="${c.key}" data-idx="${c.idx ?? ''}">
        <div class="mem-tier">${c.tier}${c.depth != null ? ` · depth:${c.depth}` : ''}${c.moodDelta != null ? ` · Δ${c.moodDelta > 0 ? '+' : ''}${c.moodDelta}` : ''}</div>
        <div class="mem-actions">${c.nodelet ? `<button class="mem-del" data-idx="${c.idx}" title="delete">✕</button>` : ''}</div>
        <textarea rows="${c.text.length > 150 ? 3 : 2}" placeholder="${c.placeholder}">${escapeHtml(c.text)}</textarea>
      </div>
    `).join('') || '<div class="sublabel" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;">No memories yet. Complete some sessions to build your memory profile.</div>';
    // Wire delete buttons
    container.querySelectorAll('.mem-del').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const idx = parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10);
        const mem = await getMemory();
        mem.sessionDigests.splice(idx, 1);
        await saveMemory(mem);
        renderMemoriesModal();
      });
    });
    // Wire auto-save on textarea blur
    container.querySelectorAll('textarea').forEach(ta => {
      ta.addEventListener('blur', async () => {
        const card = ta.closest('.memory-card');
        const key = card.dataset.key;
        const idx = card.dataset.idx;
        const mem = await getMemory();
        if (key === 'longTermProfile') mem.longTermProfile = ta.value;
        else if (key === 'rollingWindow') mem.rollingWindow = ta.value;
        else if (key === 'digest' && idx !== '') mem.sessionDigests[parseInt(idx, 10)].digest = ta.value;
        await saveMemory(mem);
      });
    });
  }

  $('viewMemoriesBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    await renderMemoriesModal();
    $('memoriesModal')?.classList.add('visible');
  });
  $('memCloseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => $('memoriesModal')?.classList.remove('visible'));
  $('memAddBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    const memory = await getMemory();
    memory.sessionDigests.unshift({ sessionId: Date.now(), date: Date.now(), digest: '', depth: null, moodDelta: null });
    await saveMemory(memory);
    renderMemoriesModal();
    notify.info('New memory added. Type to edit, it auto-saves on blur.');
  });
  $('memRefreshBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    const memory = await getMemory();
    notify.info('Regenerating summaries...');
    memory.lastRollingAt = 0; memory.lastProfileAt = 0;
    await updateRollingMemory(memory);
    await updateLongTermProfile(memory);
    await saveMemory(memory);
    renderMemoriesModal();
    notify.success('Memory summaries regenerated.');
  });

  $('sidebarSettingsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    $('crisisLink')?.click();
  });

  $('remoteProcessingOptIn')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    if (e.target.checked && !state.remoteProcessingOptIn) {
      e.target.checked = false;
      openRemoteConsentModal();
      return;
    }
    state.remoteProcessingOptIn = !!e.target.checked;
    saveUserSettings();
    notify.info(state.remoteProcessingOptIn ? 'Remote backup + processing enabled.' : 'Remote backup + processing disabled.');
  });
  $('smartDirectorEnabled')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    state.smartDirectorEnabled = !!e.target.checked;
    saveUserSettings();
    _updateDirectorBiasUI(); // grey out the bias row when director is off
  });
  // Director calibration slider — updates label live, persists on change (release).
  // Semantic labels are chosen to reinforce "neutral default is 0" rather than
  // implying more-cautious-is-better or vice versa.
  const DIRECTOR_BIAS_LABELS = {
    '-3': 'strongly cautious',
    '-2': 'cautious',
    '-1': 'slightly cautious',
     '0': 'balanced',
     '1': 'slightly forward',
     '2': 'forward',
     '3': 'strongly forward',
  };
  function _updateDirectorBiasUI() {
    const slider = $('directorBiasSlider');
    const label  = $('directorBiasLabel');
    const row    = $('directorBiasRow');
    if (!slider || !label || !row) return;
    label.textContent = DIRECTOR_BIAS_LABELS[String(slider.value)] || 'balanced';
    // Grey out when Smart Director is off — bias has no effect if nothing runs.
    const enabled = state.smartDirectorEnabled !== false;
    row.style.opacity = enabled ? '' : '0.4';
    slider.disabled = !enabled;
    $('directorBiasResetBtn') && ($('directorBiasResetBtn').disabled = !enabled);
  }
  $('directorBiasSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state.directorBias = Number(e.target.value);
    _updateDirectorBiasUI();
    sdLog('directorBias changed (uncommitted)', state.directorBias);
  });
  $('directorBiasSlider')?.addEventListener('change', () => {
    saveUserSettings();
    sdLog('directorBias saved', state.directorBias);
  });
  $('directorBiasResetBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const slider = $('directorBiasSlider');
    if (slider) slider.value = 0;
    state.directorBias = 0;
    _updateDirectorBiasUI();
    saveUserSettings();
  });
  $('remoteConsentCancelBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const cb = $('remoteProcessingOptIn'); if (cb) cb.checked = false;
    state.remoteProcessingOptIn = false;
    saveUserSettings();
    closeRemoteConsentModal();
  });
  $('remoteConsentAgreeBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const cb = $('remoteProcessingOptIn'); if (cb) cb.checked = true;
    state.remoteProcessingOptIn = true;
    saveUserSettings();
    closeRemoteConsentModal();
    notify.info('Remote backup + processing enabled.');
  });
  $('remoteConsentModal')?.addEventListener('click', e => {
    if (e.target?.id === 'remoteConsentModal') closeRemoteConsentModal();
  });

  // Profile form — save on any input change
  ['pfName', 'pfAbout', 'pfAppearance', 'pfGoals'].forEach(id => {
    $(id)?.addEventListener('input', saveProfile);
  });
  ['pfPronouns', 'pfAge', 'pfExperience', 'pfUseFirstName'].forEach(id => {
    $(id)?.addEventListener('change', saveProfile);
  });
  // Session daily cap — max 3 sessions per day to prevent compulsive use
  async function checkDailyCap() {
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    const today = new Date(); today.setHours(0,0,0,0);
    const todayCount = history.filter(s => {
      const d = new Date(s.date); d.setHours(0,0,0,0);
      return d.getTime() === today.getTime();
    }).length;
    if (todayCount >= 3) {
      notify.info('You\'ve completed 3 sessions today — that\'s plenty. Rest and let the suggestions integrate. Come back tomorrow.');
      return false;
    }
    return true;
  }

  // Monthly safety re-check — re-display contraindication screen every 30 days

  // Practice-unlock gating — methods unlock with experience
  async function getSessionCount() {
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    return history.filter(s => s.completed).length;
  }

  async function applyMethodGating() {
    const count = await getSessionCount();
    const skip = state._debug?.skipMethodGating;
    if (skip) sdLog('method gating bypassed — debugSkipMethodGating on');
    // Thresholds: rapid unlocks at 3 sessions, advanced at 7
    document.querySelectorAll('#methodFilterTabs .filter-tab').forEach(tab => {
      const cat = tab.dataset.filter;
      if (!skip && cat === 'rapid' && count < 3) {
        tab.style.opacity = '0.4';
        tab.title = `Unlocks after 3 completed sessions (${count} so far)`;
      } else if (!skip && cat === 'advanced' && count < 7) {
        tab.style.opacity = '0.4';
        tab.title = `Unlocks after 7 completed sessions (${count} so far)`;
      } else {
        tab.style.opacity = '';
        tab.title = skip && (cat === 'rapid' || cat === 'advanced') ? 'Debug: unlocked' : '';
      }
    });
  }

  // Persona modal
  $('personaCancelBtn').addEventListener('click', closePersonaEditor);
  $('personaSaveBtn').addEventListener('click', savePersonaFromForm);
  $('personaShareBtn')?.addEventListener('click', shareCurrentPersona);
  $('personaModal').addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target.id === 'personaModal') closePersonaEditor(); });

  // Hypnotic Induction Profile quiz

  // Init — async to wait for IDB storage migration
  (async function init() {
    detectCaps();
    await _initStorage();
    refreshPersonas();
    const hadSavedSettings = await loadUserSettings();
    await loadProfile();
    if (typeof loadVoices === 'function') { loadVoices(); applySavedVoiceSelection(); updateVoiceInfo(); }
    renderPersonaGrid();
    renderPersonaDetail();
    renderMethodGrid();
    renderMethodDetail();
    // Restore filter tab visual state from saved settings
    document.querySelectorAll('#personaFilterTabs .filter-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.filter === state.personaFilter));
    document.querySelectorAll('#methodFilterTabs .filter-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.filter === state.methodFilter));
    renderPresets();
    renderPrograms();
    renderSessionHistory();
    renderHeatmap();
    renderSidebarStats();
    updateIntentionHint();
    // Update bg cache count
    bgCacheGetManifest().then(m => { const el = $('bgCacheCount'); if (el) el.textContent = m.length; });
    // Set soundscape default based on method — but only if no saved settings
    if (!hadSavedSettings) {
      const defaultMethod = getMethod();
      state.soundscape = defaultMethod.drone ? 'drone' : 'none';
      state.droneEnabled = defaultMethod.drone;
      const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect');
      if (ssSelect) ssSelect.value = state.soundscape;
    }
    updateStepUI();

    // Load shared config from URL fragment if present
    await loadSharedConfig();

    // AI preload (delayed on mobile to avoid slowing page load)
    if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.aiTextPlugin) {
      if (window.innerWidth < 500) setTimeout(() => root.aiTextPlugin({ preload: true }), 5000);
      else root.aiTextPlugin({ preload: true });
    }

    // Onboarding tour for first-time visitors
    if (shouldShowTour()) setTimeout(startTour, 800);

    // Rising-score sparkline
    renderSparkline();

    // Practice-unlock method gating
    applyMethodGating();

    // Sync debug state from DOM (checkboxes default unchecked, but this guarantees
    // state._debug matches the visible UI in all cases). Banner re-renders from here.
    _syncDebugState();
    _updateDirectorBiasUI();
  })();
</script>

<script id="workflow-copy-polish-v9">
  (() => {
    const setLabel = (id, label) => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.setAttribute('aria-label', label); };
    setLabel('jumpGuideBtn', 'Go back and change the guide');
    setLabel('jumpMethodBtn', 'Go back and change the method');
    setLabel('jumpIntentionBtn', 'Go back and change the intention');
    setLabel('jumpAffirmationsBtn', 'Go back and change your affirmations');
    setLabel('jumpConfigBtn', 'Go back and change the session settings');
    setLabel('btnSkipToScript', 'Skip the guided builder and use your own script');
    setLabel('returnToSetupBtn', 'Go back to the setup screens');
    setLabel('restartBtn', 'Start another session with the current setup');
  })();
</script>
